# QSP Disease Model Library

> **ΉηΡΈΠβ ΉΩΖΈΞ░Ήζ┤ΊΛ╕ ΉνΣ έΑΦ Automatically maintained by [Claude Code Routine (CCR)](https://code.claude.com)**  
> Έπν ΉΕ╕ΉΖαΈπΙΈΜν ΉΔΙ ΉπΙΊβα ΈςρΈΞ╕Ήζ┤ ΉηΡΈΠβΉε╝Έκε Ή╢ΦΆ░ΑΈΡσΈΜΙΈΜν ┬╖ A new disease model is added automatically each session.

---

## Ά░εΉγΦ (Overview)

### ΊΧεΆ╡φΉΨ┤

Ήζ┤ ΉιΑΉηξΉΗΝΈΛΦ **ΉιΧΈθΚΉιΒ ΉΜεΉΛνΊΖε ΉΧ╜ΈουΊΧβ(Quantitative Systems Pharmacology, QSP)** ΈςρΈΞ╕ΉζΕ ΉπΙΊβαΈ│ΕΈκε Ή▓┤Ά│ΕΉιΒΉε╝Έκε Ά╡υΉ╢Χ┬╖Ή╢ΧΉιΒΊΧαΈΛΦ ΉΓ┤ΉΧΕΉηΙΈΛΦ Έζ╝Ήζ┤Έ╕ΝΈθυΈουΉηΖΈΜΙΈΜν.

ΈςρΈΥι Ή╜αΊΖΡΉ╕ιΈΛΦ **AnthropicΉζα Claude Code Routine (CCR)** ΉζΕ ΊΗ╡ΊΧ┤ ΉβΕΉιΕ ΉηΡΈΠβΉε╝Έκε ΉΔζΉΕ▒ΈΡσΈΜΙΈΜν. CCRΉζΑ ΉδΡΆ▓σ ΊΒ┤Έζ╝Ήγ░ΈΥε Ή╗ρΊΖΝΉζ┤ΈΕΙΉΩΡΉΕε ClaudeΆ░Α ΉπΒΉιΣ Ή╜ΦΈΥεΈξ╝ ΉηΣΉΕ▒ΊΧαΆ│ι, ΊΝΝΉζ╝ΉζΕ ΈιΝΈΞΦΈπΒΊΧαΆ│ι, Ή╗νΈ░Μ┬╖ΊΣ╕ΉΜεΆ╣ΝΉπΑ ΉβΕΈμΝΊΧαΈΛΦ ΉηΡΉερ ΉΜνΊΨΚ ΊβαΆ▓╜ΉηΖΈΜΙΈΜν. Έπν ΉΕ╕ΉΖαΉζ┤ ΉλΖΈμΝΈΡι ΈΧΝ Έ░αΈΥεΉΜε Έ│ΑΆ▓╜ ΉΓυΊΧφΉζ┤ Ή╗νΈ░Μ┬╖ΊΣ╕ΉΜεΈΡαΉΨ┤ ΉηΙΉΨ┤ΉΧ╝ ΊΧαΈΛΦ **Stop Hook**(`stop-hook-git-check.sh`)Ήζ┤ ΉΕνΉιΧΈΡαΉΨ┤ ΉηΙΉΨ┤, **ΉΓυΈηΝΉζα Ά░εΉηΖ ΉΩΗΉζ┤ΈΠΕ ΉιΑΉηξΉΗΝΆ░Α ΉπΑΉΗΞΉιΒΉε╝Έκε Ά░▒ΉΜι**ΈΡσΈΜΙΈΜν.

#### Ά░Β ΈςρΈΞ╕ΉΩΡ ΊΠυΊΧρΈΡαΈΛΦ ΈΓ┤Ήγσ

| ΉΓ░Ή╢εΈυ╝ | ΈΓ┤Ήγσ |
|--------|------|
| **Ά╕░Ά│ΕΈκιΉιΒ ΉπΑΈΠΕ** (`.dot` / `.svg` / `.png`) | 100Ά░ε Ήζ┤ΉΔΒ ΈΖ╕ΈΥε, Graphviz DOT ΊαΧΉΜζ; ΉπΙΊβα ΊΛ╣Ήζ┤ ΉΔζΈυ╝ΊΧβΉιΒ Ά▓╜Έκε, ΉΧ╜Έυ╝ PK/PD, Έ░ΦΉζ┤ΉανΈπΙΉ╗ν, ΉηΕΉΔΒ ΉΩΦΈΥεΊΠυΉζ╕ΊΛ╕Έξ╝ ΊΧαΈΓαΉζα ΉΜεΆ░ΒΊβΦΈκε ΊΗ╡ΊΧσ |
| **mrgsolve ODE ΈςρΈΞ╕** (`.R`) | Έψ╕Έ╢ΕΈ░σΉιΧΉΜζ Ά╕░Έ░α PK/PD ΈςρΈΞ╕; Ήμ╝ΉγΦ ΉηΕΉΔΒΉΜεΊΩα ΊΝΝΈζ╝Έψ╕ΊΕ░Έκε Έ│┤ΉιΧ; Έ│╡ΉΙαΉζα Ή╣αΈμΝ ΉΜεΈΓαΈουΉαν ΉΜεΈχυΈιΙΉζ┤ΉΖα; ΉγσΈθΚ-Έ░αΉζΣ Έ╢ΕΉΕζ ΊΠυΊΧρ |
| **Shiny ΈΝΑΉΜεΈ│┤ΈΥε** (`.R`) | Ήζ╕ΊΕ░ΈηβΊΜ░Έ╕Ν Ήδ╣ ΉΧ▒; ΊβαΉηΡ ΊΝΝΈζ╝Έψ╕ΊΕ░ ΉΕνΉιΧ, ΉΧ╜Έυ╝ ΉΕιΊΔζ, PK/PD ΉΜνΉΜεΆ░Ε ΉΜεΆ░ΒΊβΦ, ΉΜεΈΓαΈουΉαν Έ╣ΕΆ╡ΡΊΣε, ΉηΕΉΔΒ ΉεΕΊΩα ΉπΑΊΣε |
| **Ή░╕Ά│ιΈυ╕ΊΩΝ** (`.md`) | PubMed ΈπΒΊΒυ ΊΠυΊΧρ 30Ά░ε Ήζ┤ΉΔΒΉζα ΉΕιΈ│Ε ΈΖ╝Έυ╕; Έ│ΣΊΔεΉΔζΈου, ΉηΕΉΔΒΉΜεΊΩα, Έ░ΦΉζ┤ΉανΈπΙΉ╗ν ΉΕ╣ΉΖαΈ│Ε Έ╢ΕΈξα |

#### ΉπΙΊβα ΉΕιΊΔζ Ά╕░ΉνΑ

ΉΕιΊΔζ ΈςσΈκζΉζΑ ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα 49ΉλΖ + ΈπΝΉΕ▒ΉπΙΊβα 44ΉλΖ(Ή┤ζ 93ΉλΖ)Ήε╝Έκε Ά╡υΉΕ▒ΈΡσΈΜΙΈΜν. ΉΕ╕ΉΖαΈπΙΈΜν **Ήζ┤Έψ╕ ΉβΕΉΕ▒ΈΡε ΉπΙΊβαΆ│╝ ΉνΣΈ│╡ΈΡαΉπΑ ΉΧΛΈΠΕΈκζ** ΈΓιΉπε Ά╕░Έ░αΉε╝Έκε ΈΜνΈξ╕ ΉπΙΊβαΉζΕ ΉΕιΊΔζΊΧσΈΜΙΈΜν. ΉΕιΊΔζ Ήγ░ΉΕιΉΙεΉεΕ:
- Ή╡εΆ╖╝ FDA/EMA ΉΛ╣Ήζ╕ ΈαΡΈΛΦ ΉηΕΉΔΒ 3ΉΔΒΉζ┤ ΉηΙΈΛΦ ΉπΙΊβα
- PK/PD ΊΝΝΈζ╝Έψ╕ΊΕ░Ά░Α Έυ╕ΊΩΝΉΩΡ Ή╢σΈ╢ΕΊηΙ Ά│╡Ά░εΈΡε ΉπΙΊβα
- Ήζ┤ΉιΕ ΈςρΈΞ╕ΈΥνΆ│╝ Έ│ΣΊΔεΉΔζΈου Ή╣┤ΊΖΝΆ│ιΈουΆ░Α ΈΜνΈξ╕ ΉπΙΊβα

#### Ά╕░ΉΙι ΉΛνΊΔζ

```
Graphviz (dot)        έΗΤ  Ά╕░Ά│ΕΈκιΉιΒ ΉπΑΈΠΕ ΈιΝΈΞΦΈπΒ (.dot έΗΤ .svg + .png)
mrgsolve (R)          έΗΤ  ODE Ά╕░Έ░α PK/PD ΉΜεΈχυΈιΙΉζ┤ΉΖα
Shiny (R)             έΗΤ  Ήζ╕ΊΕ░ΈηβΊΜ░Έ╕Ν ΈΝΑΉΜεΈ│┤ΈΥε
Claude Code Routine   έΗΤ  ΈςρΈΥι ΊΝΝΉζ╝ ΉηΡΈΠβ ΉΔζΉΕ▒ Έ░Π Ή╗νΈ░Μ
CCR Stop Hook         έΗΤ  ΉΕ╕ΉΖα ΉλΖΈμΝ ΉΜε Ή╗νΈ░Μ/ΊΣ╕ΉΜε Ά░ΧΉιε ΉΜνΊΨΚ
```

---

### English

This repository is a **living QSP (Quantitative Systems Pharmacology) model library** that grows automatically with each session. Every model follows the same four-deliverable structure: mechanistic map ┬╖ mrgsolve ODE model ┬╖ Shiny app ┬╖ curated references.

#### How the Automation Works

All content is generated by **Anthropic's Claude Code Routine (CCR)** έΑΦ an autonomous cloud execution environment where Claude writes code, renders files, and pushes commits without human intervention. A mandatory **Stop Hook** (`stop-hook-git-check.sh`) is configured: the session cannot close unless every change is committed and pushed to the remote branch. This guarantees that the repository always reflects the full output of each session.

The workflow per session:

```
1. Pull latest main
2. Select a new disease from the curated list (93 diseases total)
   έΗΤ Avoid duplicates, rotate categories, prioritize recent clinical data
3. Build the mechanistic map (.dot έΗΤ .svg + .png via Graphviz)
4. Write mrgsolve R model (ODE compartments, PK/PD parameters, scenarios)
5. Scaffold the Shiny app (έΚξ6 interactive tabs)
6. Compile references (έΚξ30 PubMed-linked papers)
7. Update README.md (table row + detailed section) and create CLAUDE.md
8. git add -A έΗΤ commit έΗΤ push to main (enforced by Stop Hook)
```

#### Per-Model Content Standards

| Deliverable | Standards |
|-------------|-----------|
| **Mechanistic map** | έΚξ100 nodes; έΚξ8 subgraph clusters; drug mechanisms, clinical endpoints, and biomarkers all visualized |
| **mrgsolve model** | έΚξ15 ODE states; έΚξ5 treatment scenarios; calibrated to published clinical trial PK/PD; doseέΑΥresponse analysis |
| **Shiny dashboard** | έΚξ6 tabs; interactive patient profile, drug PK, PD biomarkers, scenario comparison table, risk classification |
| **References** | έΚξ30 curated papers with PubMed links; categorized by mechanism / biomarker / clinical trial sections |

#### Disease Coverage

Models span two major categories drawn from a curated list of **93 diseases**:

- **ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα (Autoimmune, 49 diseases)** έΑΦ RA, SLE, Sj├╢gren's, MCTD, vasculitides (GPA/EGPA/MPA/PAN/Takayasu/GCA), IBD, PSC/PBC, AIH, MS, MG, NMO, GBS, CIDP, autoimmune encephalitis, ITP, AIHA, pemphigus, IgAN, and more
- **ΈπΝΉΕ▒ΉπΙΊβα (Chronic/Metabolic, 44 diseases)** έΑΦ T2DM, PCOS, HFrEF/HFpEF, COPD, IPF, PAH, OSA, CKD/ADPKD/FSGS/MCD, NAFLD, cirrhosis, chronic hepatitis B, BPH, and more

See [`CLAUDE.md`](CLAUDE.md) for the complete disease list and model-building guidelines used by each CCR session.

## QSP Disease Models

Ά░Β ΈςρΈΞ╕ΉζΑ ΉΗΝΈυ╕ΉηΡ ΊΧαΉζ┤ΊΦΙ ΈΦΦΈιΚΊΗιΈουΉΩΡ ΉιΑΉηξΈΡσΈΜΙΈΜν ┬╖ Each model lives in its own lowercase-dash subdirectory containing:
- `*.dot` έΑΦ Mechanistic map source (Graphviz DOT, έΚξ100 nodes)
- `*.svg` / `*.png` έΑΦ Rendered mechanistic map (vector + raster)
- `*_references.md` έΑΦ Curated PubMed literature (έΚξ30 papers)
- `*_mrgsolve_model.R` / `*_model.R` έΑΦ mrgsolve ODE model + simulation scenarios
- `*_shiny_app.R` / `shiny_app/app.R` έΑΦ Interactive Shiny PK/PD dashboard

### Rheumatoid Arthritis

> Directory: [`rheumatoid-arthritis/`](rheumatoid-arthritis/)

**Mechanistic Map** (130+ nodes, 13 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Immune Cell Activation | DC, Macrophage M0/M1, Th1/Th17/Treg, Tfh, B cells, Plasma cells, NK, Neutrophils, Mast cells, NETosis |
| Autoantibody Formation | PAD4, citrullination, ACPA/RF, immune complexes, complement (C1q/C3/C5a), Fc╬│RIII |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-╬▒, IL-1╬▓, IL-6, IL-8, IL-10, IL-12, IL-17A/F, IL-21, IL-23, IFN-╬│, GM-CSF, TGF-╬▓, VEGF, OSM, CXCL13, CCL2/5 |
| Intracellular Signaling | JAK1/2/3/TYK2, STAT1/3/4/5/6, NF-╬║B/IKK, p38 MAPK, ERK, JNK, PI3K/Akt/mTOR, AP-1, HIF-1╬▒, NFATc1, Wnt/╬▓-catenin |
| Synovial Pathology | FLS (quiescent/activated), synovial macrophage, pannus, COX-2/PGE2/LTB4, MMPs 1/2/3/9/13, ADAMTS-4/5, TIMPs |
| Synovial Vasculature | Endothelium, ICAM-1/VCAM-1, E-selectin, VEGF-driven neo-angiogenesis, HIF-1╬▒, eNOS |
| Bone & Cartilage | RANKL/RANK/OPG, osteoclast/osteoblast, bone erosion, cartilage ECM (type II collagen, aggrecan), Wnt/DKK-1/sclerostin, chondrocyte apoptosis |
| Pain Signaling | Nociceptor (C/A╬┤), NGF/TrkA, TRPV1, Nav1.7/1.8, Substance P/CGRP, bradykinin, peripheral & central sensitization |
| Drug PK | Oral/SC/IV compartments, FcRn recycling, TMDD, ADA, protein binding |
| Drug Mechanisms | MTX (DHFR/adenosine), LEF (DHODH), HCQ (lysosomal), SSZ (NF-╬║B); 5├ΩTNFi; 4├ΩIL-6Ri; Abatacept; Rituximab; Denosumab; 4├ΩJAKi |
| Biomarkers | CRP, ESR, IL-6, TNF-╬▒, MMP-3, RF, Anti-CCP, fibrinogen, SAA, hepcidin, Hb, RANKL/OPG serum |
| Clinical Endpoints | DAS28-CRP/ESR, ACR20/50/70, CDAI, SDAI, HAQ-DI, Sharp/vdH score, RAMRIS, EULAR remission, MBDA |
| Systemic Complications | CV risk, atherosclerosis, BMD loss, RA-ILD, lymphoma, infections, VTE (JAKi), anemia, depression |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![RA QSP Map](rheumatoid-arthritis/ra_qsp.png)](rheumatoid-arthritis/ra_qsp.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| TCZ PK | DEPOT_TCZ, C1_TCZ, C2_TCZ | 2-compartment SC/IV with first-order absorption |
| TMDD | R_FREE, RC | Free sIL-6R╬▒ and TCZ-receptor complex |
| MTX PK | GI_MTX, C1_MTX | 1-compartment oral; active metabolite proxy |
| PD | TNFa, IL6, CRP, RANKL_pd | Cytokine and biomarker ODE dynamics |
| Scores | SJC28_ode, TJC28_ode | Inflammation-driven joint count adaptation |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dCRP/dt = ksyn_CRP ├Ω IL6_eff/(EC50+IL6_eff) έΙΤ kout_CRP ├Ω CRP` (IL-6R blockade suppresses IL6_eff via TMDD)
- `DAS28-CRP = 0.56έΙγTJC + 0.28έΙγSJC + 0.36┬╖ln(CRP+1) + 0.014┬╖PtGA + 0.96`

### Pulmonary Arterial Hypertension (PAH)

> Directory: [`pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/`](pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/)

> ΊΠΡΈΠβΈπξ ΈΓ┤ΊΦ╝ΉΕ╕ΊΠυ Ά╕░ΈΛξ Έ╢ΑΉιΕ Έ░Π ΊαΙΆ┤Α ΊΠΚΊβεΆ╖╝ Έ╣ΕΈΝΑΈκε ΊΠΡΊαΙΆ┤Α ΉιΑΊΧφΉζ┤ ΉΔΒΉΛ╣ΊΧαΉΩυ Ήγ░ΉΜυΉΜν Έ╢ΑΉιΕΉζΕ ΉειΈ░εΊΧαΈΛΦ ΊζυΆ╖Α ΉπΕΊΨΚΉΕ▒ ΉπΙΊβα.

**Mechanistic Map** (130+ nodes, 10 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| ET-1 Vasoconstriction | ET-1 έΗΤ ETA/ETB έΗΤ Gq/G12 έΗΤ PLC/RhoA έΗΤ IPέΓΔ/Ca┬▓έΒ║/ROCK έΗΤ MLCK/MLCP έΗΤ vasoconstriction |
| NO-cGMP Vasodilation | eNOS/BH4/L-Arg έΗΤ NO έΗΤ sGC έΗΤ cGMP έΗΤ PKG έΗΤ Kv-channel opening έΗΤ vasodilation; PDE5 degradation |
| PGIέΓΓ-cAMP Vasodilation | AA έΗΤ COX έΗΤ PGIS έΗΤ PGIέΓΓ έΗΤ IP-receptor έΗΤ Gs έΗΤ AC έΗΤ cAMP έΗΤ PKA έΗΤ vasodilation |
| Growth Factor Signalling | BMPR2/ALK1/BMP9 έΗΤ SMAD1/5/8 έΗΤ ID1; TGF-╬▓ έΗΤ SMAD2/3; PDGFR/VEGFR/FGFR έΗΤ RAS-ERK/PI3K-AKT-mTOR/STAT3 |
| Vascular Remodelling | PASMC proliferation, EC dysfunction, EndMT, collagen synthesis, MMP-2/9, ECM remodelling, plexiform lesion |
| Inflammation & Immune | Th1/Th2/Th17/Treg, M1/M2 macrophage, mast cells, B cells, NK/CD8+, IL-6/IL-1╬▓/TNF-╬▒ έΗΤ NF-╬║B |
| Hypoxia & Metabolism | HIF-1╬▒/2╬▒, VHL/PHD axis, Warburg glycolysis, mitochondrial fission (DRP1/OPA1), Kv1.5έΗΥ, ROS/NOX4/SOD2 |
| RV-PA Haemodynamics | PVR έΗΤ mPAP (Ohm's law); Ees/Ea coupling; Frank-Starling; RV hypertrophy έΗΤ failure; TR; IVS bowing; RAAS/SNS |
| Biomarkers | BNP/NT-proBNP, hs-TnI, TAPSE, RVEF, RAP, ET-1, DLCO |
| Drug PK/PD | ERA (bosentan/ambrisentan/macitentan, ICέΓΖέΓΑ Emax Hill); PDE5i (sildenafil/tadalafil); sGC stimulator (riociguat); PGIέΓΓ analogues (epoprostenol/treprostinil/selexipag) |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![PAH QSP Map](pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/pah_qsp_model.png)](pulmonary-arterial-hypertension/pah_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| ERA PK | ERA_gut, ERA_central, ERA_periph, ERA_effect | 2-compartment oral + effect-site equilibration |
| PDE5i PK | PDE5_gut, PDE5_central, PDE5_effect | 1-compartment oral + effect-site |
| PGIέΓΓ PK | PGI2_central, PGI2_effect | IV infusion (t┬╜ ~3 min) |
| PD έΑΦ Mediators | ET1, cGMP, cAMP | Turnover ODE for each second messenger |
| PD έΑΦ Structure | VRI | Vascular Remodelling Index (logistic growth, drug reversal) |
| RV Function | Ees_RV | Adaptive hypertrophy έΗΤ maladaptive decompensation |
| Biomarker | BNP_conc | Wall-stressέΑΥdriven BNP production |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dVRI/dt = k_growth ├Ω VRI ├Ω (1 έΙΤ VRI/VRI_max) έΙΤ (k_ERA├ΩERA_Inh + k_PDE├Ω╬ΦcGMP + k_PGI├ΩPGIέΓΓ_Act) ├Ω VRI`
- `PVR = PVR_normal + (PVR_PAH0 έΙΤ PVR_normal) ├Ω [tone_frac ├Ω ET1/ET1_PAH ├Ω (1έΙΤERA_Inh) ├Ω cGMPέΓΑ/cGMP ├Ω cAMPέΓΑ/cAMP + remod_frac ├Ω VRI/VRIέΓΑ]`
- `mPAP = CO ├Ω PVR/80 + PAWP`
- Simulates 6 scenarios (no treatment έΗΤ triple ERA+PDE5i+PGIέΓΓ) over 12 weeks

### Systemic Lupus Erythematosus (SLE)

> Directory: [`systemic-lupus-erythematosus/`](systemic-lupus-erythematosus/)

> NETs/cGAS-STING/TLR7/9 έΗΤ pDC έΗΤ IFN-╬▒ Ά│╝ΈΜν έΗΤ BAFFέΗΣ έΗΤ BΉΕ╕ΊΠυ Ά│╝ΊβεΉΕ▒ΊβΦ έΗΤ ΉηΡΆ░ΑΊΧφΉ▓┤(anti-dsDNA) έΗΤ Έσ┤ΉΩφΈ│╡ΊΧσΉ▓┤ έΗΤ Έ│┤Ή▓┤ ΉΗΝΈςρ + ΈμρΊΣ╕ΉΛν ΉΜιΉΩ╝ΉζΕ ΉειΈ░εΊΧαΈΛΦ Έ│╡ΉηκΊΧε ΈΜνΉηξΆ╕░ ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα.

**Mechanistic Map** (161 nodes, 9 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Cell Death & Antigen Release | UV έΗΤ apoptosis, NETosis/PAD4 citrullination, secondary necrosis, HMGB1, mitochondrial DNA, defective phagocytosis, TREX1 deficiency |
| Innate Immunity & Type I IFN | pDC/mDC/monocytes, TLR7/TLR9/TLR4, cGAS-STING έΗΤ cGAMP, IRF3/IRF5/IRF7/MyD88/TRIF, NF-╬║B, IFN-╬▒/╬▓, IFNAR1/2 έΗΤ JAK1/TYK2 έΗΤ ISGF3(STAT1/STAT2/IRF9) έΗΤ ISGs (MX1/IFIT1/OAS/ISG15), DNase I, IL-1╬▓/NLRP3/TNF-╬▒/IL-12/IL-18 |
| B Cell Activation & Autoantibodies | Na├ψve B έΗΤ GC έΗΤ LLPC; BAFF/APRIL έΗΤ BAFF-R/TACI/BCMA; BCR/SYK/BTK/PI3K╬┤; CD40-CD40L; IL-21; anti-dsDNA/anti-Sm/anti-Ro/anti-La/anti-C1q/anti-nucleosome/ANA; IgG immune complexes |
| T Cell Dysregulation | Th1/Th2/Th17/Tfh/Treg/DN T cells/CD8+CTL; T-bet/ROR╬│t/FoxP3; IFN-╬│/IL-17A/IL-4/IL-6/IL-2/TGF-╬▓; calcineurin/NFAT; mTOR; JAK3/STAT3/STAT5; CTLA-4/PD-1/PDL-1/ICOS |
| Complement System | Classical (C1q/C1r-C1s/C4/C2/C3), Alternative (Factor B/H/Properdin/C3 tick-over), Lectin (MBL); C3a/C5a anaphylatoxins; MAC (C5b-9); Fc╬│RIIA/III; CR1; C4d deposition; C1q/C2/C4 gene deficiency |
| Lupus Nephritis | IC deposition έΗΤ mesangial/endothelial/podocyte injury έΗΤ GBM damage έΗΤ proteinuria; eGFR decline έΗΤ ESRD; TGF-╬▓ fibrosis; ISN/RPS Class IέΑΥVI; VEGF; IL-6; neutrophil infiltration; hematuria; hypertension |
| Multi-Organ Involvement | Malar rash/discoid lupus/SCLE/photosensitivity; BBB disruption έΗΤ anti-NMDAR έΗΤ NPSLE; accelerated atherosclerosis; endothelial dysfunction; aPL antibodies έΗΤ APS/thrombosis; serositis; arthritis; alopecia; cytopenias |
| Drug PK/PD | HCQ (lysosomotropic TLR7/9 block; Vd ~5000 L, t┬╜ ~50 days); Belimumab (anti-BAFF TMDD; t┬╜ ~19 days; FcRn); Anifrolumab (anti-IFNAR1; 300 mg q4w); MMF/MPA (IMPDH inhibition); Voclosporin/Tacrolimus (calcineurin-NFAT); Cyclophosphamide (DNA alkylation); Azathioprine (6-MP/PRPP); Corticosteroids (GR transrepression); Obinutuzumab (anti-CD20) |
| Biomarkers & Clinical Endpoints | SLEDAI-2K; BILAG; SLICC damage index; anti-dsDNA titer; C3/C4 serum; ESR/CRP; lymphopenia; thrombocytopenia; UPCR; IFN score; BAFF level; SRI-4; BICLA; complete/partial renal response; LLDAS; DORIS remission; flare rate |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![SLE QSP Map](systemic-lupus-erythematosus/sle_qsp.png)](systemic-lupus-erythematosus/sle_qsp.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| HCQ PK | HCQ_gut, HCQ_cent | 1-compartment oral; Vd ~5200 L, t┬╜ ~50 days |
| Belimumab PK+TMDD | BELI_cent, BELI_periph, BAFF_free, BELI_cmplx | 2-compartment IV + TMDD for free BAFF |
| Anifrolumab PK | ANIF_cent | 1-compartment IV (300 mg q4w); IFNAR occupancy |
| MMF/MPA PK | MMF_gut, MPA_cent | 1-compartment oral; active metabolite MPA |
| Voclosporin PK | VOC_gut, VOC_cent | 1-compartment oral; IC50 ~0.8 ng/mL calcineurin |
| IFN pathway PD | TLR_act, IFNa_conc, IFNscore | TLRέΗΤpDCέΗΤIFN-╬▒έΗΤISG cascade; HCQ/anifrolumab effects |
| B cell axis | Bcell, PBlast, LLPC | BAFF-driven survival; MMF/CS/Cycloph suppression |
| Autoantibodies | AntiDsDNA, IC_burden | LLPCέΗΤanti-dsDNAέΗΤIC turnover |
| Complement | C3_serum, C4_serum | IC-driven consumption; liver synthesis |
| Kidney | Proteinuria, eGFR_ode | ICέΗΤglomerular injuryέΗΤUPCR; voclosporin podocyte protection |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dIFNa/dt = k_pDC ├Ω TLR_act ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_ANIF) έΙΤ k_IFNA ├Ω IFNa`
- `dBAFF/dt = Rin_BAFF έΙΤ kout_BAFF ├Ω BAFF έΙΤ kon ├Ω (BELI/V1) ├Ω BAFF + koff ├Ω complex + k_IFN_BAFF ├Ω IFNa`
- `dProteinuria/dt = k_IC_prot ├Ω IC_burden έΙΤ kout_prot ├Ω Prot ├Ω (1 + 1.5├ΩE_VOC + 0.5├ΩE_CS)`
- Simulates 7 scenarios (no Tx έΗΤ HCQ έΗΤ +MMF έΗΤ +Belimumab έΗΤ +Anifrolumab έΗΤ LN regimen έΗΤ triple LN) over 52 weeks

### IgA Nephropathy (IgAN)

> Directory: [`iga-nephropathy/`](iga-nephropathy/)

> Έ╣ΕΉιΧΉΔΒΉιΒΉε╝Έκε ΈΜ╣ΊβΦΈΡε IgA1(Gd-IgA1) Έσ┤ΉΩφΈ│╡ΊΧσΉ▓┤Ά░Α ΉΓυΆ╡υΉ▓┤ ΈσΦΉΓ░ΉπΑΉδΑΉΩΡ Ή╣ρΉ░σΈΡαΉΨ┤ Έ│┤Ή▓┤Έξ╝ ΊβεΉΕ▒ΊβΦΉΜεΉ╝ε Ήκ▒ΉΕ╕ΊΠυ ΉΗΡΉΔΒ Έ░Π ΉΜυΊΧε ΈΜρΈ░▒ΈΘρΈξ╝ ΉειΈ░εΊΧαΈΛΦ Έσ┤ΉΩφ ΈπνΆ░ε ΉΓυΆ╡υΉ▓┤ΉΜιΉΩ╝. **ΉΓυΉνΣ ΊΔΑΆ▓σ Ά░ΑΉΕν(four-hit hypothesis)** Ά╕░Έ░α QSP ΈςρΈΞ╕.

**Mechanistic Map** (155+ nodes, 12 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic/Environmental Risk | HLA-DQB1, TNFSF13/TNFSF13B (APRIL/BAFF genes), C1GALT1/Cosmc mutations, ST6GalNAc-II, DEFA1A3, gut dysbiosis, mucosal infection |
| Mucosal Immunity | Naive B έΗΤ Peyer's patch GC / tonsillar MALT, Tfh, IL-21/IL-4/IL-6/IL-10/TGF-╬▓ class switching, AID, APRIL/BAFF, pIgR, sIgA |
| Hit 1 έΑΥ Gd-IgA1 | IgA1 hinge O-glycosylation; C1GalT1έΗΥ/CosmcέΗΥ έΗΤ exposed GalNAc έΗΤ Gd-IgA1 serum elevation; ST6GalNAc-II competition; ASGPR hepatic clearance |
| Hit 2 έΑΥ Autoantibody | BCR (GalNAc epitope), GC reaction, SHM, class-switch έΗΤ anti-Gd-IgA1 IgG/IgA; CD4+ Tfh, IL-21, IL-17A |
| Hit 3+4 έΑΥ IC Deposition | Gd-IgA1 ├Ω IgG IC formation, IC polymerization/hexamerization, Fc╬▒RI (CD89)/TfR1 mesangial receptors, mesangial deposition έΗΣέΗΣέΗΣ |
| Complement System | Lectin (MBL/Ficolins/MASP-1/2), Classical (C1q), AP amplification (Factor B/D/P), C3 convertases CP+AP, C3 cleavage έΗΤ C3a/C3b, C5 convertase έΗΤ C5a/MAC (C5b-9), CD46/CD55 regulators |
| Mesangial Signaling | MC quiescentέΗΤactivated; NF-╬║B, ERK, PI3K/AKT, PDGFR-╬▓/PDGF-BB; TGF-╬▓1/SMAD2-3/CTGF; IL-6/TNF-╬▒/MCP-1; MC proliferation, mesangial matrix expansion; ROS/NOX4; HIF-1╬▒ |
| Glomerular Injury | Podocyte (healthyέΗΤinjured); Nephrin/Podocin/Synaptopodin/TRPC6; foot process effacement; GBM thickening; έΗΣglomerular permeability; proteinuria; hematuria; crescents; VEGF/Ang-2 |
| Tubular/Interstitial Fibrosis | PTC protein overload, TEC-EMT, interstitial macrophage/T cell, TGF-╬▓1 TIF, myofibroblast, Collagen I/III, MMP-2/9, TIMP-1/2, tubulointerstitial fibrosis, tubular atrophy |
| RAAS | Renin/AGT/AngI/ACE/AngII/AT1RέΑΥAT2R, aldosterone, NaέΒ║ retention, intraglomerular hypertension, SNS, ET-1, ACE2/Ang(1-7)/MasR |
| Drug PK/PD | ACEi/ARB, Sparsentan (dual AT1R+ETB), Budesonide TRF/Nefecon (mucosal APRIL suppression), Iptacopan (Factor B), Sibeprenlimab (anti-APRIL), Zigakibart (anti-C5), SGLT2i (dapagliflozin), Prednisolone, MMF, Atrasentan, Belimumab |
| Clinical Endpoints | eGFR, UPCR, 24-h proteinuria, serum Gd-IgA1/IgA, serum C3, creatinine, BP, Oxford MEST-C score (M/E/S/T/C), ESKD, CR50, complete remission, eGFR slope |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![IgAN QSP Map](iga-nephropathy/igan_qsp_model.png)](iga-nephropathy/igan_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| Budesonide TRF PK | BUD_gut, BUD_central | 1-compartment oral; F=15% (high hepatic extraction) |
| Sparsentan PK | SPA_gut, SPA_central | 1-compartment oral; F=85% |
| Iptacopan PK | IPT_gut, IPT_central | 1-compartment oral; BID dosing |
| Sibeprenlimab PK | SIB_depot, SIB_central, SIB_periph | SC 2-compartment; Q4W dosing |
| Four-hit PD | GdIgA1, AutoAb, IC_mes, CompAP | Hit 1έΑΥ4 cascade with Emax drug effects |
| Glomerular | Podocyte, UPCR | Injury/repair ODE; proteinuria driven by podocyte loss |
| Fibrosis | TIF | Slow logistic fibrosis; protein-overload amplification |
| Renal function | eGFR | Continuous GFR loss from TIF + podocyte depletion |
| Hemodynamics | BP_sys | AngII-driven setpoint model |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dGdIgA1/dt = k_syn ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_mucosal) έΙΤ k_deg ├Ω GdIgA1`  (budesonide + sibeprenlimab reduce synthesis)
- `dCompAP/dt = k_syn_CP ├Ω IC_mes ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_iptacopan) έΙΤ k_deg ├Ω CompAP`  (AP pathway; Factor B blocked by iptacopan)
- `dUPCR/dt = k_syn_UPCR ├Ω (1έΙΤPodocyte) ├Ω (1+0.4├ΩMesangial) ├Ω (1έΙΤE_spa) ├Ω (1έΙΤE_RAAS) έΙΤ k_deg ├Ω UPCR`
- `deGFR/dt = έΙΤ[k_loss_GFR ├Ω TIF + k_RAAS_GFR ├Ω (1έΙΤE_RAAS) ├Ω (1έΙΤPodocyte)] ├Ω eGFR`
- Simulates 7 scenarios (untreated έΗΤ triple Budesonide+Sparsentan+Iptacopan) over 2 years

**Calibration landmarks (trial data):**
- NefIgArd (Barratt 2023): Budesonide TRF έΗΤ UPCR έΙΤ22% at 9 months έεΥ
- PROTECT (Heerspink 2023/2024): Sparsentan έΗΤ UPCR έΙΤ49% at week 36 vs. irbesartan έεΥ
- APPLAUSE-IgAN (Rovin 2024): Iptacopan έΗΤ UPCR έΙΤ38% vs. placebo έεΥ
- AFFINITY (Barratt 2023): Sibeprenlimab 700 mg έΗΤ UPCR έΙΤ47% at 9 months έεΥ
- DAPA-CKD IgAN sub-analysis: dapagliflozin έΗΤ 71% RR reduction in composite ESKD έεΥ

| File | Description |
|------|-------------|

| [`igan_qsp_model.svg`](iga-nephropathy/igan_qsp_model.svg) | Vector mechanistic map |

### Multiple Sclerosis (MS)

> Directory: [`multiple-sclerosis/`](multiple-sclerosis/)  
> Disease category: **ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα / ΉΜιΆ▓╜Ά│Ε (Autoimmune έΑΦ CNS)**  
> Date added: **2026-06-16**

**Pathophysiology Summary:**  
Multiple sclerosis is a chronic autoimmune demyelinating disease of the CNS affecting ~2.8 million people worldwide. The immunopathology begins in peripheral lymphoid organs where myelin antigens (MOG, MBP, PLP) are presented by dendritic cells to na├ψve CD4έΒ║ T cells, driving Th1 (IFN-╬│+) and Th17 (IL-17A+) differentiation. These effector T cells up-regulate VLA-4 (╬▒4╬▓1 integrin) to engage VCAM-1 on blood-brain barrier (BBB) endothelium, triggering diapedesis into the CNS. Th17-derived IL-17A/MMP-9 additionally disrupts claudin-5 and ZO-1 tight junction proteins to widen the BBB leak. Once inside the CNS, infiltrating T cells together with activated microglia release TNF-╬▒, IL-1╬▓, NO, and ROS that are directly cytotoxic to oligodendrocytes, leading to demyelination. Loss of myelin trophic support results in NaV channel redistribution, Ca┬▓έΒ║ overload, mitochondrial dysfunction, and axonal transection έΑΦ the substrate of irreversible disability. B cells contribute via anti-MOG antibody production (intrathecal IgG; oligoclonal bands), complement activation, and antigen presentation. OPC-mediated remyelination can partially restore function but is inhibited by LINGO-1 and Nogo-A in the chronic lesion environment.

**Mechanistic Map:**

[![MS QSP Map](multiple-sclerosis/ms_qsp.png)](multiple-sclerosis/ms_qsp.svg)

*12 subgraph clusters ┬╖ 160+ nodes ┬╖ 7 drug PK/PD arms including TMDD (natalizumab)*

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment | States | Description |
|-------------|--------|-------------|
| IFN-╬▓ PK | A1_ifnb, C1_ifnb, C2_ifnb | 2-compartment SC/IM; F=40%; JAK-STAT PD |
| Natalizumab PK | C1_nat, C2_nat, RC_nat, R_nat | 2-comp IV + TMDD; kon/koff/kint |
| Ocrelizumab PK | C1_ocre, C2_ocre | 2-comp IV; Emax B cell depletion |
| Siponimod PK | C1_sip, C2_sip | 2-comp oral; S1PR1/5 antagonism |
| DMF/MMF PK | C1_dmf | 1-comp oral; Nrf2/NF-╬║B dual PD |
| Cladribine PK | C1_clad | 1-comp oral; dATP-mediated lymphodepletion |
| Peripheral immunity | Th1, Th17, Treg, Bcell | Normalized cell levels; drug inhibition terms |
| BBB | BBB | Integrity 0έΑΥ1; IL-17A/MMP-9 disruption; natalizumab/IFNb protection |
| CNS infiltration | cTh1, cTh17 | BBB-gated infiltration; natalizumab blocks |
| Neuroinflammation | Micro | Microglia activation; Treg dampening |
| Myelination | Oligo, OPC, Myelin | OPC differentiation έΗΤ remyelination; LINGO-1 inhibition |
| Axonal integrity | Axon | Loss from demyelination + smouldering inflammation |
| Biomarkers | NfL, GFAP | Serum biomarkers; axon and astrocyte damage |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dMyelin/dt = k_remyelin ├Ω OPC ├Ω (1έΙΤMyelin) έΙΤ kdmyelin ├Ω Micro ├Ω Myelin ├Ω (1έΙΤE_Nrf2) + kin_myelin ├Ω (1έΙΤMyelin)`
- `dAxon/dt = k_repair ├Ω Myelin έΙΤ k_loss ├Ω (1έΙΤMyelin) έΙΤ k_loss├Ω0.5 ├Ω Micro ├Ω Axon`
- `dRC_nat/dt = kon ├Ω Cnat ├Ω R έΙΤ (koff + kint) ├Ω RC_nat`  *(TMDD natalizumab)*
- `EDSS = 10 ├Ω (1έΙΤAxon) ├Ω 0.8 + 10 ├Ω (1έΙΤMyelin) ├Ω 0.2`
- Simulates 7 arms (untreated, IFN-╬▓, natalizumab, ocrelizumab, siponimod, DMF, cladribine) over 2 years

**Calibration landmarks (Phase III trial data):**
- AFFIRM (Polman 2006): Natalizumab έΗΤ ARR έΙΤ68%, T2 έΙΤ83% έεΥ
- OPERA I/II (Hauser 2017): Ocrelizumab έΗΤ ARR έΙΤ46έΑΥ47%, B cell depletion >95% έεΥ
- EXPAND (Kappos 2018): Siponimod έΗΤ 3m-CDP έΙΤ21% in SPMS έεΥ
- DEFINE (Gold 2012): DMF 240 mg BID έΗΤ ARR έΙΤ49% έεΥ
- CLARITY (Giovannoni 2010): Cladribine 3.5 mg/kg έΗΤ ARR έΙΤ58% έεΥ
- MSCRG (Jacobs 1996): IFN-╬▓-1a IM έΗΤ ARR έΙΤ18%, T2 έΙΤ37% έεΥ

**Shiny Dashboard Tabs (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | MS phenotype (RRMS/SPMS/PPMS), baseline EDSS, disease severity radar |
| 2. Drug PK | PK curves for all 6 drugs; TMDD receptor occupancy (natalizumab); B cell depletion (ocrelizumab) |
| 3. Immunology | Peripheral Th1/Th17/Treg/B cell dynamics; CNS infiltration; BBB integrity over time |
| 4. Disease Progression | Myelin/OPC/oligodendrocyte dynamics; T2 lesion volume; axonal integrity trajectory |
| 5. Clinical Endpoints | EDSS progression; annualized relapse rate; NEDA-3 achievement rate |
| 6. Scenario Comparison | Multi-drug overlay for any endpoint; sortable 2-year summary table with ARR reduction % |
| 7. Biomarkers & Safety | Serum NfL & GFAP trajectories; siponimod lymphocyte safety monitoring; receptor occupancy |

### Type 2 Diabetes Mellitus (T2DM)

> Directory: [`type2-diabetes/`](type2-diabetes/)

**Mechanistic Map** (165+ nodes, 11 pathway clusters):

[![T2DM QSP Map](type2-diabetes/t2dm_qsp_model.png)](type2-diabetes/t2dm_qsp_model.svg)

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Drug PK | Metformin (2-cmpt oral), Empagliflozin (1-cmpt), Semaglutide (SC depot, t┬╜~168h), Sitagliptin, Glimepiride, Insulin Degludec (SC hexamer depot), Pioglitazone |
| Incretin System | L-cell GLP-1 / K-cell GIP secretion; DPP-4 plasma degradation; GLP-1R on ╬▓-cell/╬▒-cell/brainstem; vagal-gut axis |
| Pancreatic Islet | ╬▓-cell mass & function (Topp model); KATP/Ca┬▓έΒ║ GSIS; SUR1 (SU target); GLP-1R/GIP-RέΗΤcAMP; ER stress/UPR; NLRP3/IL-1╬▓; ╬▓-cell proliferation vs apoptosis |
| Insulin Signaling | IRέΗΤIRS-1έΗΤPI3KέΗΤAktέΗΤAS160έΗΤGLUT4 translocation; GSK-3╬▓/glycogen synthesis; FOXO1 nuclear/cytoplasmic; PTP1B; mTORC1/S6K1έΗΤIRS-1 pSer feedback; PKC╬╕/ceramide/TLR4 |
| Hepatic Glucose | HGP = glycogenolysis + gluconeogenesis (PEPCK/G6Pase/PGC-1╬▒/FOXO1); MetforminέΗΤComplex IέΗΤAMPKέΗΤέΗΥgluconeo; glucagon receptorέΗΤPKAέΗΤglycogenolysis |
| Peripheral Tissues | Muscle/adipose GLUT4 translocation; AMPK (exercise/metformin); ceramide lipotoxicity; PPAR╬│ (TZD); adiponectin/leptin/TNF-╬▒/IL-6/resistin |
| Glucose Compartments | Bergman extended: Gp, Gt, EGP, Rd; SGLT2 renal handling: Tmax, UGE, renal threshold; SGLT1 gut absorption; osmotic diuresis; ketogenesis |
| Diabetic Complications | AGE/RAGE, PKC, hexosamine, polyol pathways έΗΤ vascular oxidative stress έΗΤ endothelial dysfunction έΗΤ ASCVD; TGF-╬▓ έΗΤ mesangial expansion έΗΤ UACR/eGFR; VEGF-retina; peripheral neuropathy |
| CNS Regulation | Hypothalamic NPY/AgRP vs POMC/CART; GLP-1R brainstem; leptin/ghrelin; circadian clock; HPA cortisol; sympathetic tone |
| Systemic Inflammation | ATM macrophage M1; NF-╬║BέΗΤIL-6/MCP-1/PAI-1; FFAέΗΤTLR4; NLRP3 inflammasome; ox-LDL; foam cells |
| Body Weight / Lipids | VAT/SAT; lipolysis; FFAέΗΤTGέΗΤLDLέΗΤsdLDLέΗΤox-LDL; CETP; ketone bodies; caloric deficit from UGE |

**ODE System (25 state variables):**

| Module | States | Key Equations |
|--------|--------|---------------|
| Drug PK | MET_C, MET_P, EMPA_C, SEMA_SC, SEMA_C, DPP4I_C, SU_C, INS_SC, INS_C, PIOG_C | 2-cmpt metformin; SC depot for sema/insulin; 1-cmpt for rest |
| Glucose | Gp, Gt | `dGp/dt = (EGPέΙΤRd)/(Vg├ΩBW) έΙΤ Sg├Ω(GpέΙΤ90) έΙΤ UGE_loss/(Vg├ΩBW)` |
| Insulin | Ip, X_action | `dIp/dt = (GSISέΙΤCL├ΩIp)/Vi/BW`; `dX/dt = έΙΤp2├ΩX + p2├ΩSI├ΩIp` |
| Glucagon | Gc | `dGc/dt = kout├Ω(Gc_ss έΙΤ Gc)`; Gc_ss = f(Gp, Ip, GLP-1RA) |
| GLP-1 | GLP1 | `dGLP1/dt = kin + kGp├Ω(GpέΙΤ90) έΙΤ (kDPP4├Ω(1έΙΤDPP4i) + kout)├ΩGLP1` |
| ╬▓-cell | beta_mass | `dM/dt = (k_prolif├Ωf(Gp) έΙΤ k_apop├Ωf(FFA,Gp,GLP1)) / 24├Ω365` |
| IR | IR_H, IR_P | FFA/glucose-driven increase; metformin/pioglitazone recovery |
| Lipid/Weight | FFA, BW_t | Anti-lipolytic insulin effect; UGE caloric loss; GLP-1RA weight |
| Endpoints | HbA1c_cmpt, eGFR_cmpt, UACR_cmpt | First-order equilibration; eGFR protected by SGLT2i |

**Treatment Scenarios (7 arms, 1-year simulation):**

| # | Regimen | Expected ╬ΦHbA1c | ╬ΦWeight | CV Protection |
|---|---------|-----------------|---------|---------------|
| 1 | No treatment (baseline) | 0 | 0 kg | None |
| 2 | Metformin 1g BID | έΙΤ1.4% | έΙΤ2 kg | Moderate |
| 3 | Metformin + Empagliflozin 10mg QD | έΙΤ2.1% | έΙΤ4 kg | High (EMPA-REG) |
| 4 | Metformin + Semaglutide 1mg QW | έΙΤ2.8% | έΙΤ6 kg | High (SUSTAIN-6) |
| 5 | Triple: Met + Empa + Sema | έΙΤ3.2% | έΙΤ7 kg | Very High |
| 6 | Metformin + Insulin Degludec 20U | έΙΤ3.0% | +2 kg | Moderate |
| 7 | Metformin + Sitagliptin 100mg QD | έΙΤ1.6% | 0 kg | Neutral (TECOS) |

**Calibration landmarks:**
- UKPDS-34 (1998): Metformin έΗΤ HbA1c έΙΤ1.4%, CV death έΙΤ36% έεΥ
- EMPA-REG OUTCOME (Zinman 2015): Empagliflozin έΗΤ CV death έΙΤ38%, eGFR preservation έεΥ
- SUSTAIN-6 (Marso 2016): Semaglutide έΗΤ HbA1c έΙΤ1.4%, weight έΙΤ4.5 kg, MACE έΙΤ26% έεΥ
- DECLARE-TIMI 58 (Wiviott 2019): Dapagliflozin έΗΤ HHF έΙΤ27%, renal composite έΙΤ47% έεΥ
- TECOS (Green 2015): Sitagliptin έΗΤ CV safety confirmed, HbA1c έΙΤ0.7% έεΥ

### NAFLD/NASH έΑΦ Non-Alcoholic Fatty Liver Disease / Steatohepatitis

> Directory: [`nafld-nash/`](nafld-nash/)

**Mechanistic Map** (120+ nodes, 10 pathway clusters):

[![NAFLD QSP Map](nafld-nash/nafld_qsp_model.png)](nafld-nash/nafld_qsp_model.svg)

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Dietary Input & Gut-Liver Axis | Dietary fat/fructose/CHO έΗΤ intestinal absorption έΗΤ chylomicron έΗΤ portal FFA/TG; fructolysis έΗΤ DNL; enterohepatic circulation; LPS translocation |
| Gut Microbiome | Dysbiosis (Firmicutes:Bacteroidetes έΗΣ); SCFA/LPS/TMAO/ETOH production; tight junction loss; bile acid transformation (BSH) |
| Hepatic Lipid Metabolism | DNL (SREBP-1c/ChREBP/FASN); FAO (PPAR╬▒/CPT1A); TG accumulation; VLDL assembly/secretion; ceramide/DAG lipotoxicity; steatosis (NAS) |
| Mitochondrial & Oxidative Stress | ETC leak έΗΤ ROS; lipid peroxidation (4-HNE/MDA); ER stress (ATF6/IRE1/PERK/UPR); Nrf2/antioxidant; mPTP έΗΤ apoptosis |
| Inflammatory Signaling (NASH) | TLR4/TLR2/NF-╬║B; NLRP3 inflammasome έΗΤ IL-1╬▓/IL-18; Kupffer cell M1/M2; TNF-╬▒/IL-6/IL-8/IL-10; neutrophil/macrophage recruitment; hepatocyte ballooning (NAS) |
| Fibrosis Pathway | TGF-╬▓1 έΗΤ ALK5/SMAD2/3 έΗΤ COL1A1/COL3A1/CTGF; HSC activation (quiescentέΗΤmyofibroblast); PDGF proliferation; MMP-2/TIMP-1 balance; ECM accumulation έΗΤ F0έΗΤF4 |
| Insulin Resistance & Adipose-Liver Axis | VAT lipolysis έΗΤ portal FFA; adiponectin/leptin; IR (HOMA-IR) έΗΤ SREBP-1cέΗΣ/FOXO1έΗΤgluconeogenesis; PI3K/Akt; AMPK/SIRT1; DAG-PKC╬╡-IR |
| Drug PK/PD | Resmetirom (2-cmpt+OATP1B hepatic uptake, THR╬▓ Ki=0.9nM, έΗΥDNL/έΗΣFAO); OCA (1-cmpt, FXR/SHP/CYP7A1έΗΥ, anti-fibrotic); Semaglutide (SC depot QW, GLP-1R appetite+IR); Empagliflozin (oral, SGLT2 inhibition έΗΤ UGE έΗΤ weight loss) |
| Biomarkers & Clinical Endpoints | ALT/AST, MRI-PDFF, FibroScan LSM, NAS (0έΑΥ8), FIB-4, ELF score, PRO-C3, LDL-C/TG/HDL-C, HbA1c, HOMA-IR, hs-CRP; NASH resolution, cirrhosis, HCC |
| Systemic Metabolic Context | BMI/obesity; hyperglycemia; dyslipidemia; hypertension; MetS; PCOS association; T2DM comorbidity; CVD risk; weight loss/fibrosis regression |

**ODE System (21 state variables):**

| Module | States | Key Equations |
|--------|--------|---------------|
| Resmetirom PK | RSM_GUT, RSM_CENT, RSM_PERI, RSM_LIVER | 2-cmpt oral + OATP1B hepatic uptake; Cl_liver = 0.7├ΩCL├ΩCp/V |
| OCA PK | OCA_GUT, OCA_CENT | 1-cmpt high-hepatic-clearance; E_OCA = Emax├ΩCp/(EC50+Cp) |
| Semaglutide PK | SEM_SC, SEM_CENT | SC depot (ka=0.0045 hέΒ╗┬╣, t┬╜έΚΙ7d); E_SEM drives weight loss + IR |
| Empagliflozin PK | EMP_GUT, EMP_CENT | 1-cmpt oral; SGLT2 inhibition έΗΤ urinary glucose excretion |
| Liver fat | LIVER_FAT | `dLF/dt = KLIN├ΩDNL├Ω(BW/BWέΓΑ) έΙΤ KOUT├ΩLF├Ω(1+0.6├ΩE_RSM)(1+0.15├ΩE_SEM)` |
| Insulin resistance | INS_RES | IR_ss = IRέΓΑ├Ω(1 + FFA-effect + TNF-effect έΙΤ adiponectin-protection)├Ω(1 έΙΤ drug-effect) |
| Kupffer cell | KUPFFER | `dKUP/dt = (KOUT├ΩKUPέΓΑ + KLIP├ΩLipotox)/(1 + drug-inh) έΙΤ KOUT├ΩKUP` |
| Cytokines | TNFA, IL6C, TGFB | First-order; production έΙζ Kupffer activation + lipotoxicity; drug inhibition of TGF-╬▓ |
| Fibrosis | HSC, COLLAGEN | `dHSC/dt = (KOUT├ΩHSCέΓΑ + KTGF├ΩTGFB)/(1+OCA/RSM-inh) έΙΤ KOUT├ΩHSC` |
| ALT | ALT_CMT | `dALT/dt = KREL + KAPOP├ΩTNF├ΩLipotox έΙΤ KOUT├ΩALT` |
| Adipokines/Weight | ADIPONECTIN, BODY_WT | Weight έΗΥ with semaglutide (KOUT├Ω(WT_target έΙΤ WT)); adiponectin έΗΣ with weight loss |

**Treatment Scenarios (6 arms, 72-week simulation):**

| # | Regimen | Expected ╬ΦLiver Fat | ╬ΦFIB Score | ╬ΦALT |
|---|---------|---------------------|------------|------|
| 1 | Placebo | 0% | 0 | 0 U/L |
| 2 | Resmetirom 100 mg QD | έΙΤ37% (MAESTRO-NASH) | έΙΤ0.3 stage | έΙΤ25 U/L |
| 3 | OCA 25 mg QD | έΙΤ22% | έΙΤ0.4 stage | έΙΤ15 U/L |
| 4 | Semaglutide 2.4 mg QW | έΙΤ31% (ESSENCE) | έΙΤ0.25 stage | έΙΤ20 U/L |
| 5 | Resmetirom + Semaglutide | έΙΤ52% (est.) | έΙΤ0.55 stage | έΙΤ35 U/L |
| 6 | Triple (RSM + OCA + Sema) | έΙΤ60% (est.) | έΙΤ0.7 stage | έΙΤ42 U/L |

**Calibration landmarks:**
- MAESTRO-NASH Phase 3 (Harrison 2024, *NEJM*): Resmetirom έΗΤ 25.9% NASH resolution, έΙΤ37% liver fat, έΙΤ24% LDL-C έεΥ
- REGENERATE (Friedman 2023, *Lancet*): OCA 25mg έΗΤ 23% έΚξ1 fibrosis stage improvement έεΥ
- ESSENCE Phase 3 (Newsome 2021, *NEJM*): Semaglutide έΗΤ 59% histological response, έΙΤ31% liver fat έεΥ
- EMPA-NAFLD (Sattar 2021): Empagliflozin έΗΤ έΙΤ22% liver fat, ALT normalization in T2DM+NAFLD έεΥ
- FLINT trial (Neuschwander-Tetri 2015): OCA έΗΤ NAS improvement at Wk 72 έεΥ

### Heart Failure with Reduced Ejection Fraction (HFrEF)

> Directory: [`heart-failure-hfref/`](heart-failure-hfref/)

**Disease Overview**

Heart failure with reduced ejection fraction (HFrEF, LVEF < 40%) affects over 26 million people worldwide and carries a 5-year mortality of ~50%. The cardinal feature is neurohumoral activation έΑΦ a vicious cycle in which impaired cardiac output triggers compensatory but ultimately maladaptive RAAS and SNS up-regulation, driving progressive ventricular remodeling, fibrosis, and further pump failure.

**Key Mechanistic Axes**

| Pathway | Core Biology |
|---------|-------------|
| RAAS | Reduced MAP έΗΤ renin release έΗΤ AngI έΗΤ ACE έΗΤ AngII έΗΤ AT1R έΗΤ vasoconstriction, aldosterone, Na retention, TGF-╬▓1, hypertrophy |
| ACE2 / Ang(1-7) axis | Counter-regulatory: ACE2 converts AngIέΗΤAng1-7 έΗΤ MasR έΗΤ NOέΗΣ, vasodilation, anti-fibrotic |
| SNS | Low CO έΗΤ baroreceptor blunting έΗΤ CNS έΗΤ NEέΗΣ έΗΤ ╬▓1AR έΗΤ cAMP/PKA έΗΤ acute inotropy (short-term) έΗΤ ╬▓1AR downregulation, apoptosis, RAAS stimulation (long-term) |
| NPS | Wall stress έΗΤ BNP/ANP έΗΤ NPR-A έΗΤ cGMP έΗΤ PKG έΗΤ vasodilation, natriuresis, anti-fibrotic |
| Cardiac Remodeling | AngII + Aldo + TNF-╬▒ έΗΤ TGF-╬▓1 έΗΤ fibroblast έΗΤ myofibroblast έΗΤ ColI/ColIII + TIMPέΗΣ έΗΤ ECM fibrosis; wall stress έΗΤ MAPK/NFAT/PI3K έΗΤ CM hypertrophy; CM apoptosis via ROS/caspase |
| Inflammation | NF-╬║B έΗΤ TNF-╬▒/IL-6/IL-1╬▓ έΗΣ (cardiodepressant cytokines); NLRP3 inflammasome; NOX2-ROS; iNOS peroxynitrite |
| Hemodynamics | LVEDVέΗΣ, SVέΗΥ, COέΗΥ, SVRέΗΣ, PCWPέΗΣ έΗΤ congestion (dyspnea, edema) + forward failure (fatigue, exercise intolerance) |

**Drug PK/PD (GDMT 4+1 Pillars)**

| Drug Class | Agent | Mechanism | Key Trial |
|-----------|-------|-----------|-----------|
| ARNI | Sacubitril/Valsartan (Entresto) | NEP inhibition (έΗΣBNP/Ang1-7/ANP plasma) + AT1R block | PARADIGM-HF: CV death/HF-hosp έΗΥ20% vs enalapril |
| ╬▓-Blocker | Metoprolol succinate / Carvedilol | ╬▓1AR competitive antagonism έΗΤ έΗΥHR, έΗΥcAMP/PKA, reverse remodeling | MERIT-HF: all-cause mortality έΗΥ34% |
| MRA | Spironolactone / Eplerenone / Finerenone | MR competitive block έΗΤ έΗΥNa retention, έΗΥTGF-╬▓1/fibrosis, έΗΣK+ | RALES: mortality έΗΥ30%; EMPHASIS-HF: CV death/HF-hosp έΗΥ37% |
| SGLT2i | Dapagliflozin / Empagliflozin | Osmotic diuresis (έΗΥpreload) + direct cardiac effects (NHE1έΗΥ, mitochondriaέΗΣ, AMPKέΗΣ) | EMPEROR-Reduced: primary endpoint έΗΥ25%; DAPA-HF: έΗΥ26% |
| Ivabradine | Ivabradine | HCN/If channel block έΗΤ έΗΥHR (no inotropy) | SHIFT: CV death/HF-hosp έΗΥ18% in HR έΚξ70 bpm |

**Mechanistic Map** (126 nodes, 9 pathway subgraphs):

| State Group | Variables |
|-------------|-----------|
| RAAS (4) | AngI, AngII, Ang(1-7), Aldosterone |
| SNS (1) | Plasma NE |
| NPS (3) | BNP, NT-proBNP, cGMP |

| Inflammation (2) | TNF-╬▒, IL-6 |
| Drug PK (6) | LBQ657, Valsartan, ╬▓-blocker, MRA, SGLT2i, Ivabradine |

**Treatment Scenarios (5)**

| Scenario | Regimen | 12-Month LVEF Change | NT-proBNP Reduction |
|----------|---------|---------------------|---------------------|
| 1 | No Therapy | +0% (progressive worsening) | έΑΦ |
| 2 | ACEi + BB | ~+5έΑΥ7% | ~30% |
| 3 | ARNI + BB + MRA | ~+8έΑΥ10% | ~37έΑΥ40% |
| 4 | ARNI + BB + MRA + SGLT2i | ~+10έΑΥ13% | ~45έΑΥ50% |
| 5 | ARNI + BB + MRA + SGLT2i + IVA | ~+11έΑΥ14% | ~48έΑΥ53% |

### Chronic Kidney Disease (CKD)

> Directory: [`chronic-kidney-disease/`](chronic-kidney-disease/)

**Disease Overview**

Chronic Kidney Disease (CKD) affects ~850 million people worldwide and is defined by persistent abnormalities in kidney structure or function (eGFR < 60 mL/min/1.73m┬▓ or albuminuria έΚξ 30 mg/g) for more than 3 months. CKD is a major cause of cardiovascular disease, anemia, mineral bone disease, and ESKD requiring dialysis or transplantation. The pathophysiology is a self-amplifying cycle: initial injury (diabetes, hypertension, glomerulonephritis) έΗΤ nephron loss έΗΤ compensatory hyperfiltration έΗΤ podocyte injury έΗΤ glomerulosclerosis έΗΤ interstitial fibrosis έΗΤ further nephron loss έΗΤ eGFR decline.

**Key Mechanistic Axes**

| Pathway | Core Biology |
|---------|-------------|
| RAAS | Ang II έΗΤ AT1R έΗΤ glomerular hypertension + NF-╬║B + TGF-╬▓1 έΗΤ proteinuria + fibrosis; Aldosterone έΗΤ MR έΗΤ Na retention + cardiac/renal fibrosis |
| Inflammation | Uremic toxins/DAMPs έΗΤ NF-╬║B έΗΤ M1 macrophages/Th17 έΗΤ IL-6/TNF-╬▒/IL-17 έΗΤ podocyte injury + tubular atrophy |
| Fibrosis | TGF-╬▓1/Smad2-3 έΗΤ EMT + myofibroblast activation έΗΤ Collagen I/III + CTGF έΗΤ ECM accumulation; Smad7 inhibitory brake |
| CKD-MBD | eGFRέΗΥ έΗΤ PhosphateέΗΣ + KlothoέΗΥ έΗΤ FGF-23έΗΣ έΗΤ CYP27B1 inhibition έΗΤ CalcitriolέΗΥ έΗΤ PTHέΗΣ έΗΤ secondary hyperparathyroidism έΗΤ bone disease + vascular calcification |
| Anemia | Peritubular cell loss έΗΤ EPOέΗΥ; Inflammation έΗΤ HepcidinέΗΣ έΗΤ Ferroportin degradation έΗΤ functional iron deficiency; PHD active έΗΤ HIF degraded έΗΤ blunted EPO response |
| Cardiovascular | Uremia έΗΤ ADMA έΗΤ eNOSέΗΥ έΗΤ NOέΗΥ έΗΤ endothelial dysfunction; BPέΗΣ + Aldo έΗΤ LVH + cardiac fibrosis; Phosphate/PTH/uremic toxins έΗΤ vascular calcification έΗΤ arterial stiffness |

**Drug PK/PD (Treatment Landscape)**

| Drug Class | Agent | Mechanism | Key Trial |
|-----------|-------|-----------|-----------|
| ACE Inhibitor | Ramipril | ACE inhibition έΗΤ έΗΥAng II έΗΤ έΗΥAT1R έΗΤ έΗΥUACR έΗΥBP | Lewis 1993 (NEJM) |
| ARB | Losartan | AT1R blockade έΗΤ έΗΥglomerular hypertension | RENAAL (NEJM 2001) |
| nsMRA | Finerenone 10έΑΥ20 mg | Non-steroidal MR blockade έΗΤ έΗΥUACR έΙΤ31%, έΗΥCV events | FIDELIO-DKD (NEJM 2020) |
| SGLT2i | Dapagliflozin 10 mg | SGLT2 block έΗΤ έΗΥTGF έΗΤ έΗΣmacula densa NaCl έΗΤ έΗΥglomerular hypertension | DAPA-CKD (NEJM 2020) |
| SGLT2i | Empagliflozin 10 mg | Same; effective to eGFR 20 mL/min | EMPA-KIDNEY (NEJM 2023) |
| ESA | Epoetin alfa / Darbepoetin | EPOR stimulation έΗΤ erythropoiesis έΗΤ έΗΣHb | Drueke et al. NEJM 2006 |
| HIF-PHI | Roxadustat 3├Ω/week | PHD inhibition έΗΤ HIF-1╬▒ stabilization έΗΤ έΗΣendogenous EPO | DOLOMITES (JASN 2021) |
| Phosphate Binder | Sevelamer | GI phosphate binding έΗΤ έΗΥserum Phos έΗΤ έΗΥFGF-23 | Block JASN 2004 |
| Calcimimetic | Cinacalcet | CaSR allosteric activator έΗΤ έΗΥPTH | EVOLVE (NEJM 2012) |

**Mechanistic Map** (130+ nodes, 10 pathway subgraphs):

[![CKD QSP Map](chronic-kidney-disease/ckd_qsp_model.png)](chronic-kidney-disease/ckd_qsp_model.svg)

*Click image to open interactive SVG. Clusters: CKD Pathophysiology ┬╖ RAAS & Hemodynamics ┬╖ Inflammation & Immune Activation ┬╖ Renal Fibrosis Cascade ┬╖ CKD-MBD ┬╖ Anemia of CKD ┬╖ Cardiovascular Complications ┬╖ Drug PK ┬╖ Drug PD ┬╖ Clinical Endpoints*

**ODE Model Summary** (22 disease states + 13 drug PK compartments = 35 total ODEs)

| State Group | Variables |
|-------------|-----------|
| Kidney Function (3) | Nephron mass, eGFR, UACR |
| RAAS (3) | Ang II, Aldosterone, BP |
| Inflammation (3) | IL-6, TNF-╬▒, Macrophage infiltration |
| Fibrosis (2) | TGF-╬▓1, Collagen/fibrosis index |
| CKD-MBD (5) | FGF-23, Klotho, Phosphate, PTH, Active VitD |
| Anemia (3) | EPO, Hepcidin, Hemoglobin |
| Cardiovascular (2) | LVH index, Vascular calcification index |
| Drug PK (13) | ACEi (2), ARB (2), Finerenone (3), SGLT2i (2), ESA (2), HIF-PHI (2) |

**Treatment Scenarios (5)**

| Scenario | Regimen | 2-Year eGFR Slope | UACR Reduction | CV Risk |
|----------|---------|-------------------|----------------|---------|
| 1 | Natural History | έΙΤ3.5 mL/min/yr | έΑΦ | High |
| 2 | ACEi Monotherapy (Ramipril 10mg) | έΙΤ2.1 mL/min/yr | έΙΤ35% | Moderate |
| 3 | ACEi + Finerenone 20mg | έΙΤ1.5 mL/min/yr | έΙΤ50% | Low-Moderate |
| 4 | ACEi + SGLT2i (DAPA-CKD) | έΙΤ1.3 mL/min/yr | έΙΤ55% | Low-Moderate |
| 5 | Triple Therapy (ACEi + Dapa + Finerenone) | έΙΤ0.8 mL/min/yr | έΙΤ65% | Low |

|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | Baseline eGFR/UACR/Hb/SBP; KDIGO heat map (eGFR ├Ω albuminuria); trajectory overview |
| 2. Drug PK Profiles | RAAS, finerenone 2-cmt, SGLT2i, ESA/HIF-PHI concentration-time curves; PK effect table |

| 4. PD Biomarkers | RAAS (Ang II/Aldo), Inflammation (IL-6/TNF-╬▒/TGF-╬▓1), CKD-MBD (FGF-23/Klotho/PTH/VitD), Anemia (EPO/Hepcidin/Hb) |
| 5. Clinical Endpoints | 5-scenario comparison table; eGFR%/UACR% change plots; CKD stage timeline; CV risk composite |
| 6. CV Risk & CKD-MBD | SBP, LVH, vascular calcification, PTH, FGF-23/Klotho axis, active Vitamin D |

### Bronchial Asthma

> Directory: [`bronchial-asthma/`](bronchial-asthma/)

> ΉΧΝΈιΙΈξ┤Ά▓Ρ ΈΥ▒ ΊβαΆ▓╜ ΉηΡΆ╖╣ΉΩΡ ΉζαΊΧ┤ Ά╕░ΈΠΕ ΉΔΒΊΦ╝ΉΩΡΉΕε Έ╢ΕΈ╣ΕΈΡαΈΛΦ ΉΧΝΈζ╝Έψ╝(TSLP/IL-25/IL-33)Ήζ┤ ILC2┬╖ΉΙαΉπΑΉΔΒΉΕ╕ΊΠυΈξ╝ ΊβεΉΕ▒ΊβΦΊΧαΆ│ι, Th2 Έ╢ΕΊβΦ(IL-4/IL-5/IL-13)┬╖IgE ΉΔζΉΕ▒┬╖Έ╣ΕΈπΝΉΕ╕ΊΠυ ΊΔΙΆ│╝Έο╜┬╖Ία╕ΉΓ░Ά╡υ Ή╣ρΉεν┬╖Ά╕░ΈΠΕΊΠΚΊβεΆ╖╝ ΉΙαΉ╢Χ┬╖ΉιΡΉΧκ Ά│╝Έ╢ΕΈ╣Ε┬╖Ά╕░ΈΠΕ ΈουΈςρΈΞ╕ΈπΒΉε╝Έκε Ήζ┤ΉΨ┤ΉπΑΈΛΦ Type-2 ΉΩ╝Ήοζ ΉνΣΉΜυΉζα ΈπΝΉΕ▒ Ά╕░ΈΠΕ ΉπΙΊβα.

**Mechanistic Map** (110+ nodes, 16 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Environmental Triggers | Allergen (HDM/pollen/cat/mold), RV/RSV, PM2.5/O3, cold air, NSAID, tobacco |
| Airway Epithelium & Innate Barrier | TSLP, IL-25, IL-33/ST2, EGFR, TJ barrier disruption, IFN-╬╗, ROS |
| ILC2 & Innate Lymphoid | ILC2 activation, GATA3, PGD2/CRTH2, KLRG1 inhibition; IL-4/IL-5/IL-13 (ILC2-derived) |
| Dendritic Cells | DC maturation, OX40L, MHC-II presentation, Th2 polarization |
| Th2 / Adaptive Immunity | Th2/Th1/Th17/Treg; GATA3/T-bet/ROR╬│t; IL-4/IL-5/IL-13/IL-9/IL-17A; STAT6/STAT5 |
| B Cell & IgE | GC reaction, plasma cell, IgE class-switch (AID), Fc╬╡RI/CD23, total/free IgE |
| Mast Cell & Basophil | Fc╬╡RI cross-linking, Syk/PLC╬│/PI3K, histamine/PGD2/LTC4/tryptase release |
| Eosinophil Biology | BM έΗΤ blood έΗΤ tissue; IL-5R╬▒; CCR3/eotaxin; MBP/ECP granule; Siglec-8 apoptosis |
| Airway Smooth Muscle | Ca2+/MLCK/MLC, RhoA/ROCK, cAMP/PKA, ╬▓2AR, M3R, H1R, CysLT1/2, TRPA1 |
| Mucus & Goblet Cell | IL-13 έΗΤ SPDEF έΗΤ MUC5AC/MUC5B; CLCA1; submucosal gland hypertrophy |
| Airway Remodeling | TGF-╬▓1/SMAD2/3 έΗΤ fibroblastέΗΤmyofibroblast έΗΤ collagen; VEGF; FGF-2; periostin; MMP-2/9 |
| Neurogenic Inflammation | SP/CGRP/NK1R, vagal reflex, ACh/M3, NGF έΗΤ sensory nerve plasticity |
| Lung Function & Clinical | FEV1, FVC, PEF, AHR, exacerbation rate, ACQ-5/7, AQLQ, symptom score, FeNO, PC20 |
| Biomarkers | Blood/tissue Eos, FeNO (ppb), serum IgE, periostin, tryptase, T2-high vs T2-low endotype |
| Drug PK | 2-compartment SC model for 5 biologics; ICS lung/systemic; LABA/LAMA; Omalizumab TMDD |
| Drug Mechanisms | Omalizumab (anti-IgE TMDD), Mepolizumab (IL-5έΗΥ), Benralizumab (IL-5R╬▒ ADCC), Dupilumab (IL-4R╬▒), Tezepelumab (TSLP), ICS/LABA/LAMA/Montelukast |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![Bronchial Asthma QSP Map](bronchial-asthma/ba_qsp_model.png)](bronchial-asthma/ba_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Compartment Group | ODE States | Description |
|-------------------|-----------|-------------|
| Mepolizumab PK | MEPO_SC, MEPO_C1, MEPO_C2 | 2-cmt SC; ka=0.0067/h, F=77% |
| Benralizumab PK | BENZ_SC, BENZ_C1, BENZ_C2 | 2-cmt SC; q4w├Ω3 έΗΤ q8w; F=59% |
| Dupilumab PK | DUPIL_SC, DUPIL_C1, DUPIL_C2 | 2-cmt SC; ka=0.0042/h; t┬╜έΚΙ21 d |
| Tezepelumab PK | TEZE_SC, TEZE_C1, TEZE_C2 | 2-cmt SC; ka=0.0072/h; t┬╜έΚΙ26 d |
| Omalizumab + TMDD | OMAL_SC, OMAL_C1, IgE_FREE, IgE_RC | TMDD: kon/koff/kdeg; IgE_ss=2.25 nM |
| ICS / LABA | ICS_LUNG, ICS_SYS, LABA_C | GR-mediated cytokine suppression |
| TSLP | TSLP_PD | Alarmin hub; Tezepelumab neutralisation |
| IL-5 | IL5_PD | Eos growth/survival; Mepolizumab |
| IL-13 | IL13_PD | Goblet/ASM/remodeling; Dupilumab |
| Blood Eosinophil | EOS_B | IL-5-driven BM production/release |
| Tissue Eosinophil | EOS_T | Blood έΗΤ airway influx (IL-13/eotaxin) |
| ASM Tone | ASM_TONE | IL-13 + EOS_T driven; LABA relaxation |
| Mucus | MUCUS | IL-13 έΗΤ goblet έΗΤ MUC5AC |
| FEV1 | FEV1_ODE | Target driven by ASM/Mucus/EOS_T |

**Key ODE relationships:**
- `dIL5/dt = ksyn_IL5 ├Ω (1 + 0.5 ├Ω TSLP_rel) ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_ICS) ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_Mepo) έΙΤ kdeg_IL5 ├Ω IL5`
- `dEOS_B/dt = kprod ├Ω IL5_rel ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_Mepo) ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_Benz) έΙΤ kin ├Ω EOS_B`
- `dFEV1/dt = kFEV1 ├Ω (FEV1_target έΙΤ FEV1)` where `FEV1_target = 78 έΙΤ 30 ├Ω (0.5┬╖f_ASM + 0.3┬╖f_Mucus + 0.2┬╖f_EOS_T)`

**Treatment Scenarios (5):**

| # | Scenario | FEV1 ╬Φ (wk 52) | Blood Eos ╬Φ | AER ╬Φ |
|---|----------|-----------------|------------|-------|
| 1 | ICS/LABA only | +10έΑΥ12% | έΙΤ10% | baseline |
| 2 | + Mepolizumab 100 mg q4w | +16έΑΥ18% | έΙΤ70έΑΥ80% | έΙΤ50% |
| 3 | + Benralizumab 30 mg q4wέΗΤq8w | +17έΑΥ19% | έΙΤ90έΑΥ97% | έΙΤ51% |
| 4 | + Dupilumab 300 mg q2w | +18έΑΥ20% | transient έΗΣ then έΗΥ | έΙΤ48% |
| 5 | + Tezepelumab 210 mg q4w | +19έΑΥ21% | έΙΤ65έΑΥ75% | έΙΤ56% |

**Shiny App έΑΥ 7 Tabs:**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|

### COPD (Chronic Obstructive Pulmonary Disease)

> Directory: [`copd/`](copd/)

> ΊζκΉΩ░ ΈΥ▒ ΉειΊΧ┤ Ά░ΑΉΛνΉΩΡ ΉζαΊΧε ΈπΝΉΕ▒ΉιΒ Ά╕░ΈΠΕ ΉΩ╝Ήοζ Έ░Π ΊΠΡΊΠυ Ήε╡ΊΧσ(ΊΠΡΆ╕░ΉλΖ)Ήε╝Έκε Έ╣ΕΆ░ΑΉΩφΉιΒ Ά╕░Έξα ΉιεΊΧεΉζ┤ Έ░εΉΔζΊΧαΈΛΦ ΉπΙΊβα. ΉιΕ ΉΕ╕Ά│Ε ΉΧ╜ 3ΉΨ╡ 8Ή▓εΈπΝ ΈςΖ Ήζ┤Ίβα, ΉΓυΈπζ ΉδΡΉζ╕ 3ΉεΕ(2019 GBD).

**Mechanistic Map** (110+ nodes, 12 pathway clusters):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Environmental Triggers & Oxidative Stress | CS, AP, biomass; ROS/RNS; NRF2/HO-1/GSH; SIRT1/HDAC2έΗΥ; oxidative inactivation of ╬▒1-AT |
| Airway Epithelium & Mucociliary Clearance | Ciliated/goblet/club cells; tight junction loss; EMT; MUC5AC/MUC5BέΗΣ; PCLέΗΥ; DAMPs (HMGB1, S100A8/9); TLR2/4/7/9; NLRP3 |
| Innate Immunity έΑΦ Macrophage & Neutrophil | Alveolar macrophage M1; NF-╬║B / AP-1; IL-8/IL-1╬▓/IL-6/TNF-╬▒; MMP-12/MMP-9; NLRP3 inflammasome; Neutrophil/CXCR1-2; NE / PR3 / MPO / NETs |
| Adaptive Immunity | CD8+ Tc1 (dominant in COPD); Th1/Th17/Treg; IL-17A έΗΤ neutrophil amplification; B cells / lymphoid follicles; GM-CSF |
| Protease-Antiprotease Imbalance & ECM | NE / MMP-12/9 / Cathepsins vs ╬▒1-AT / SLPI / TIMP; Elastin/collagen degradation έΗΤ Emphysema; Air trapping; FEV1έΗΥ |
| Small Airway Disease & Fibrotic Remodeling | TGF-╬▓1/SMAD2/3; myofibroblast; collagen I/III; ASM hypertrophy; EGFR; airway wall thickening; FEV1/FVCέΗΥ |
| Pulmonary Vasculature, RV & Comorbidities | HPV έΗΤ ET-1έΗΣ/NOέΗΥ έΗΤ PVRέΗΣ έΗΤ PH (WHO Group 3) έΗΤ RV hypertrophy/cor pulmonale; V/Q mismatch; systemic inflammation/sarcopenia/CV/T2DM/osteoporosis |
| Clinical Endpoints & GOLD Classification | FEV1/FVC (GOLD 1-4); mMRC; CAT; BODE; 6MWT; SGRQ; AECOPD; GOLD ABE group |
| Drug PK έΑΦ LAMA/LABA/ICS/PDE4i | Tiotropium / Umeclidinium / Glycopyrrolate; Salmeterol / Formoterol / Indacaterol; Budesonide / Fluticasone; Roflumilast N-oxide; NAC; Azithromycin |
| Drug PD Mechanisms | M3 mAChR έΗΤ ACh/IP3/Ca2+/ROCK έΗΤ broncho; ╬▓2-AR έΗΤ cAMP/PKA έΗΤ relaxation; GR έΗΤ NF-╬║B/AP-1 transrepression; PDE4 έΗΤ cAMPέΗΣ έΗΤ NF-╬║BέΗΥ |
| AECOPD Pathophysiology & Biomarkers | RV/Flu/RSV viral; H.flu/S.pneumo/P.aerug bacterial; CRP/PCT/Eos; SpO2έΗΥ; AE treatment (SABA+SAMA+CS+AB+NIV) |
| Biomarkers (Multi-compartment) | Blood: CRP/IL-6/IL-8/NE/Eos/CC16/SP-D/fibrinogen; Sputum: neutrophil%/IL-8/NE/MUC5AC; Exhaled: FeNO/8-isoprostane/CO; Imaging: HRCT LAA-950/Pi10 |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![COPD QSP Map](copd/copd_qsp.png)](copd/copd_qsp.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary (26 ODE states):**

| Compartment Group | States | Description |
|-------------------|--------|-------------|
| LAMA PK (Tiotropium) | LAMA_LUNG, LAMA_C, LAMA_P | Inhaled 2-compartment; lung depot έΗΤ systemic (F_sys 3%); CL 3.92 L/h; t┬╜ 5-6 days |
| LABA PK (Salmeterol) | LABA_LUNG, LABA_C, LABA_P | Lung depot; CYP3A4/2D6; CL 23 L/h |
| ICS PK (Budesonide) | ICS_LUNG, ICS_C, ICS_P | Lung F=22%; first-pass extraction 90%; CL 78 L/h; t┬╜ 2.8h |
| PDE4i PK (Roflumilast) | PDE4i_C | Oral F=80%; CL 9.1 L/h; t┬╜ 17h (N-oxide 30h) |
| Inflammation PD | IL8, NE_sput, CRP, Eos | Turnover ODEs; ICS/PDE4i Emax suppression; Eos-gated ICS response |
| Lung Function | FEV1, Emph | FEV1: natural decline + BD gain + inflam penalty + AE step-loss; Emphysema: NE-driven irreversible |
| Pulmonary Vascular | PVR | HPV-driven PVR increase with FEV1 decline |
| Exacerbation | AE_cum, AE_rate_ann | Poisson rate; ICS/PDE4i reduction; post-AE amplification |

**Key ODE Equations:**
- `dFEV1/dt = 0.05├Ω(FEV1_target έΙΤ FEV1) έΙΤ k_dec├ΩFEV1 έΙΤ k_inflam├Ω(IL8/IL8έΓΑέΙΤ1)├ΩFEV1 έΙΤ k_AE├Ω╬╗_AE├ΩFEV1`
- `dEmph/dt = k_prog├Ω(NE_sput/NEέΓΑ)├Ω(1έΙΤE_ICS├Ω0.05)├Ω(100έΙΤEmph)` έΑΦ irreversible, NE-driven
- `dPVR/dt = k_PVR├Ω(FEV1έΓΑ/FEV1έΙΤ1)├ΩPVRέΓΑ έΙΤ k_PVR├Ω0.1├Ω(PVRέΙΤPVRέΓΑ)` έΑΦ hypoxia-driven remodeling
- `E_LAMA = Emax_LAMA├ΩC_lung/(EC50_LAMA + C_lung)` έΑΦ Emax bronchodilation model

**Clinical Trial Calibration:**

| Trial | Treatment | n | Key Result | Model Calibrated Parameter |
|-------|-----------|---|------------|---------------------------|
| UPLIFT 2008 | Tio 18┬╡g qd | 5,993 | FEV1 +87 mL, AE RR 0.86 | k_FEV1_dec, Emax_LAMA |
| TORCH 2007 | SFC 50/500┬╡g bid | 6,112 | AE RR 0.75, PneumoniaέΗΣ | Emax_ICS, lambda_AE |
| FLAME 2016 | IND/GLY vs SFC | 3,362 | LABA/LAMA > ICS/LABA for AE | E_LAMA+E_LABA > E_ICS |
| IMPACT 2018 | FF/UMEC/VI triple | 10,355 | AE RRέΗΥ 25% vs LABA/LAMA | Triple interaction terms |
| ETHOS 2020 | BUD/GLY/FORM | 8,509 | EosέΚξ300 έΗΤ strongest ICS effect | Eos_thresh, Eos_factor |
| EINSTEIN 2009 | Roflumilast 500┬╡g | 3,091 | AE rateέΗΥ 15-17% | Emax_PDE4i, EC50_PDE4i |
| HIACE 2013 | NAC 600mg bid | 120 | AE rateέΗΥ 24% | NAC antioxidant pathway |
| Albert 2011 | Azithromycin 250mg/d | 1,142 | AE rateέΗΥ 27% | Azithro NF-╬║B pathway |

**Treatment Scenarios (6 arms, 1-year simulation):**
1. Placebo έΑΦ Natural history (FEV1 decline ~50 mL/yr in GOLD 2-3)
2. LAMA monotherapy έΑΦ Tiotropium 18┬╡g qd (UPLIFT calibrated)
3. LABA/LAMA dual έΑΦ Salmeterol 50┬╡g bid + Tiotropium (FLAME/POET-COPD)
4. ICS/LABA dual έΑΦ Budesonide 400┬╡g bid + Salmeterol (TORCH; Eos-gated)
5. Triple therapy έΑΦ LAMA+LABA+ICS (IMPACT/ETHOS)
6. Triple + Roflumilast έΑΦ Severe COPD + chronic bronchitis (EINSTEIN)

**Shiny App (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | GOLD stage gauge, FEV1/Eos/CAT value boxes, GOLD ABE framework table |
| 2. Pharmacokinetics | Lung vs systemic Cp-time curves (48h); steady-state Css + PD effect table |
| 3. Lung Function | FEV1 trajectory, GOLD stage bar, emphysema index, PVR time course |
| 4. Inflammatory Biomarkers | IL-8, NE, CRP, Eosinophils with threshold lines; ICS Eos-guidance rationale |
| 5. Clinical Endpoints | CAT score, cumulative AEs, annualized AE rate, SpO2, mPAP |
| 6. Scenario Comparison | All 6 arms overlay; end-of-year DT summary table with GOLD color coding |
| 7. Exacerbation Risk | Risk calculator (FEV1/Eos/history έΗΤ rate); pathogen guide (PCT); RR waterfall chart |

### Crohn's Disease (CD)

**Disease Overview:** Crohn's disease is a chronic, transmural inflammatory bowel disease affecting any segment of the GI tract (most commonly terminal ileum and colon). It is driven by a dysregulated mucosal immune response to luminal antigens in genetically susceptible individuals, characterized by non-caseating granulomas, Th1/Th17 dominance, and NOD2/CARD15 mutations in ~20% of patients.

**Mechanistic Map (134 nodes, 10 clusters):**

[![Crohn's Disease QSP Map](crohn-disease/cd_qsp_model.png)](crohn-disease/cd_qsp_model.svg)

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| Luminal / Microbiome | Dysbiosis (έΗΣProteobacteria, έΗΥFirmicutes), PAMPs (LPS/Flagellin), SCFAs, Secretory IgA, Bile acids, FMT |
| Epithelial Barrier | Enterocyte, Goblet cell (MUC2), Paneth cell (Defensins), M-cell (antigen sampling), Tight junctions (Claudin/Occludin/ZO-1), MLCK, NOD2 |
| Innate Immunity | Macrophage M1/M2, DC (CD103+), Neutrophil, ILC1/ILC3, NETs, TLR2/4/9, NOD2, NLRP3 inflammasome, Complement (C3/C5a), Mast cell |
| T Cells (Adaptive) | Na├ψve CD4+, Th1 (IFN-╬│/TNF-╬▒, T-bet), Th17 (IL-17A/F/21, ROR╬│t), Th2, Treg (FoxP3+), CD8+ CTL, Memory T, JAK1/2έΑΥSTAT signaling |
| B Cells (Adaptive) | B cell activation (CD40L/CD40), Germinal center, Plasma cell, pANCA, Mucosal IgA, Memory B |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-╬▒, IL-1╬▓, IL-6, IL-12, IL-23, IL-17A/F, IL-21, IL-10, IL-22, TGF-╬▓, IFN-╬│, IL-18, IL-33, CXCL8/10, CCL2, NF-╬║B |
| Tissue Remodeling | Myofibroblast, Fibrocyte, Collagen I/III, MMP-3/9, TIMP-1, VEGF, Intestinal stricture, Non-caseating granuloma |
| Drug PK/PD | IFX (2-cpt IV), ADA (SC depot), UST (2-cpt), VDZ (1-cpt), 6-TGN (AZA metabolite), Upadacitinib, Prednisone, Budesonide, MTX |
| Clinical Endpoints | CDAI, HBI, SES-CD, CDEIS, CRP, Fecal calprotectin, Clinical remission, Mucosal healing, Deep remission |
| Systemic Complications | Anemia, Malnutrition, Bone loss (BMD), PSC, Skin/Eye/Joint EIM, VTE risk, Growth failure (pediatric) |

**mrgsolve ODE Model (22 states):**

| Compartment Group | States | Description |
|-------------------|--------|-------------|
| IFX PK | A1_IFX, A2_IFX | 2-compartment IV; Vc=4.0 L, Vp=3.5 L, CL=0.55 L/day, Q=1.40 L/day (Fasanmade 2011, Ordas 2012) |
| ADA PK | ADA_dep, A_ADA | SC depotέΗΤcentral; V=7.8 L, CL=0.35 L/day, ka=0.38/day, F=0.64 (Ternant 2008) |
| UST PK | A1_UST, A2_UST | 2-compartment; Vc=3.5 L, Vp=7.3 L, CL=0.19 L/day; IV inductionέΗΤSC maintenance (Adedokun 2018) |
| VDZ PK | A_VDZ | 1-compartment IV; Vc=3.3 L, CL=0.49 L/day (Rosario 2017) |
| 6-TGN from AZA | A_TGN | RBC-distributed; therapeutic range 235έΑΥ450 pmol/8├Ω10έΒ╕ RBC (Osterman 2006) |
| Prednisone | A_PRED | 1-compartment; V=45 L, CL=7.2 L/day, t┬╜έΚΙ4.4 h |
| Upadacitinib (JAK1i) | A_UPA | 1-compartment oral; V=85 L, CL=24 L/day, F=0.79 |
| TNF-╬▒ | TNF | pg/mL; SS=100 (active CD); kprod feedback on MI; Emax IFX/ADA 93έΑΥ90% |
| IL-12/23 composite | IL1223 | pg/mL; SS=80; UST Emax=88%; UPA partial suppression |
| IL-17A | IL17 | pg/mL; SS=60; Th17- and IL-23-driven; JAKi-sensitive |
| Th17 / Th1 cells | Th17, Th1 | Normalized; IL-23-driven expansion; Treg-mediated suppression; VDZ/TGN/JAKi block |
| Treg | Treg | Normalized; TGF-╬▓/SCFA-dependent; mild expansion with treatment |
| Mucosal neutrophils | Neut | Normalized; IL-17A + TNF-╬▒ recruitment; disease driver |
| Mucosal Inflammation | MI | 0έΑΥ100 score; composite of TNF/IL-17/Neut/Treg signals; maps to CDAI/SES-CD |
| CRP | CRP | mg/L; SS=25 (active); IL-6 proxy; target <5 mg/L (STRIDE-II) |
| Fecal Calprotectin | FC | ╬╝g/g; SS=800; neutrophil + mucosal inflammation driven; target <150 ╬╝g/g |
| Bone Mineral Density | BMD | Normalized; TNF-╬▒ + steroid accelerated loss |
| Hemoglobin | Hgb | g/dL; SS=10.5 (mild ACD); suppressed by hepcidin/IL-6 via MI |

**Key ODE Equations:**
- `dxdt_TNF = kprod_TNF ├Ω (1 + 0.4├Ω(MI/MIέΓΑέΙΤ1)) ├Ω (1έΙΤE_antiTNF) έΙΤ kdeg_TNF ├Ω TNF`
- `dxdt_IL17 = kprod_IL17 ├Ω (1 + kIL23_IL17├Ω(IL1223/IL12230έΙΤ1)) ├Ω (Th17/Th17έΓΑ) ├Ω (1έΙΤE_JAKi) έΙΤ kdeg_IL17 ├Ω IL17`
- `dxdt_Th17 = kprol_Th17 ├Ω Th17 ├Ω (1 + kIL23_Th17├Ω(IL1223/IL12230έΙΤ1)) ├Ω (1έΙΤkTreg_Th17├Ω(Treg/TregέΓΑ)) ├Ω (1έΙΤE_VDZ) έΙΤ kdeg_Th17 ├Ω Th17`
- `dxdt_MI = kprod_MI ├Ω (1 + MI_stim έΙΤ MI_supp) ├Ω (1έΙΤE_combined) έΙΤ kdeg_MI ├Ω MI`
- `dxdt_CRP = kprod_CRP ├Ω MI έΙΤ kdeg_CRP ├Ω CRP`
- `dxdt_BMD = kform_BMD ├Ω BMD έΙΤ (kresorb_BMD + kTNF_BMD├ΩTNF/TNFέΓΑ + kPRED_BMD├ΩC_PRED) ├Ω BMD`

**Clinical Trial Calibration:**

| Trial | Treatment | n | Key Result | Model Calibrated Parameter |
|-------|-----------|---|------------|---------------------------|
| ACCENT I (Hanauer 2002) | IFX 5 mg/kg | 573 | Remission 39% w54 | CL_IFX, Emax_IFX_TNF |
| CHARM (Colombel 2007) | ADA 40 mg q2w | 854 | Remission 36% w26 | CL_ADA, Emax_ADA_TNF |
| UNIFI (Feagan 2016) | UST 6 mg/kg IV | 741 | Remission 21% w8 (IV) | CL_UST, Emax_UST |
| GEMINI II (Sandborn 2013) | VDZ 300 mg | 814 | Remission 39% w52 | CL_VDZ, Emax_VDZ_MI |
| U-ACHIEVE (Loftus 2023) | UPA 45 mg QD | 526 | Remission 39.5% w12 | CL_UPA, Emax_UPA |
| SONIC (Colombel 2010) | IFX+AZA combo | 508 | Remission 56.8% w26 | 6-TGN synergy, ATI suppression |

**Treatment Scenarios (7 arms, 78-week simulation):**
1. No Treatment έΑΦ Natural history; CDAI ~280, CRP ~25 mg/L, FC ~800 ╬╝g/g
2. Infliximab 5 mg/kg IV έΑΦ w0/2/6 induction έΗΤ q8w maintenance
3. Adalimumab 160/80/40 mg SC έΑΦ q2w maintenance
4. Ustekinumab 6 mg/kg IV έΗΤ 90 mg SC q8w
5. Vedolizumab 300 mg IV έΑΦ w0/2/6 έΗΤ q8w (gut-selective)
6. Upadacitinib 45 mg QD έΗΤ 30 mg QD maintenance (oral JAK1i)
7. IFX + Azathioprine 150 mg/day έΑΦ combination (anti-immunogenicity)

**Shiny App (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | Demographics, disease location/behaviour, baseline CDAI/CRP/FC, prior biologic history, disease severity radar |
| 2. Pharmacokinetics | IFX/ADA/UST/VDZ Cp-time curves, VDZ ╬▒4╬▓7 receptor occupancy, 6-TGN RBC levels with therapeutic range annotation, PK summary table |

| 6. Biomarker Correlations | Population PK/PD sim (N=150, IIV via log-normal); CRP vs CDAI, FC vs SES-CD, drug trough vs CRP, TNF vs MI scatter plots |
| 7. Dosing Optimizer | DoseέΑΥresponse curves (CRP/CDAI at Week 52 vs dose); optimal trough concentration analysis; drug comparison |

### Ankylosing Spondylitis (AS)

**Disease Overview:** Ankylosing Spondylitis (AS) is a chronic, progressive inflammatory arthritis affecting primarily the axial skeleton (sacroiliac joints and spine). It is strongly associated with HLA-B27 (>90% positive). The hallmark pathology is dual: inflammatory bone erosion at entheses AND pathological new bone formation (syndesmophytes έΗΤ ankylosis). The gutέΑΥjoint axis (subclinical IBD in ~60%, ILC3-driven IL-17 amplification) and IL-17/IL-23/TNF cytokine network are central to pathogenesis.

**Mechanistic Map (162 nodes, 10 clusters):**

[![Ankylosing Spondylitis QSP Map](ankylosing-spondylitis/as_qsp_model.png)](ankylosing-spondylitis/as_qsp_model.svg)

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| 1. Genetic & Environmental | HLA-B27 (misfolding έΗΤ UPR έΗΤ IL-23), ERAP1, IL-23R variant, CARD9, ER stress, HLA-B27 homodimers (KIR3DL2), Mechanical stress, Microbial trigger |
| 2. Innate Immunity & Enthesis | Enthesis (primary lesion), Fibrocartilage, DAMPs (HSP60/HMGB1/S100), TLR2/4/9, NF-╬║B, Macrophage M1, DC (pDC/cDC), Neutrophil, Mast cell, ILC3, ╬│╬┤/MAIT T cells, NLRP3/IL-1╬▓/IL-18, ROS/NET |
| 3. Adaptive Immunity | Naive CD4+, Th17 (ROR╬│t/IL-17A έαΖ/IL-17F/IL-22), Th1 (IFN-╬│/TNF), Treg, CD8+ T (HLA-B27), NK, JAK-STAT3, RORC/T-bet, STAT4 |
| 4. Inflammatory Signaling | TNF-╬▒ (total), TNFR1/R2, NF-╬║B hub, MAPK/p38, AP-1, JAK1/2/3, STAT1/3, IL-6 (total), gp130, CRP, SAA, MMP-3/9, COX-2/PGE2 |
| 5. Bone Remodeling | Osteoclast (erosion), Osteoblast (new bone), RANKL/RANK/OPG ratio έαΖ, M-CSF, Wnt/LRP5-6 pathway, DKK1, Sclerostin (SOST), BMP-2/4/7, Smad1/5/8, Hedgehog, TGF-╬▓1, Syndesmophyte, mSASSS |
| 6. Target Organs & Clinical | SIJ (primary), Spine (thoracolumbar), Uveitis (EIM 27%), IBD (EIM), Hip, BASDAI, ASDAS-CRP, BASFI, BASMI, ASAS 20/40 |
| 7. Drug PK | ADA (40mg SC q2w), ETA (50mg SC qw), IFX (5mg/kg IV), CZP, GLM, SEC (150/300mg SC), IXE, Bimekizumab, GUS, RIS, TOF (5mg BID), UPA (15mg QD), NSAIDs |
| 8. Drug PD | TNFi (TNF neutralization), IL-17Ai (IL-17A ┬▒ F block), Bimekizumab (IL-17A+F dual), IL-23i (p19 subunit), JAKi (JAK1-selective), NSAID/COX-2 inhibition |
| 9. GutέΑΥJoint Axis | Gut microbiome dysbiosis (έΗΥLachnospiraceae, έΗΣPrevotella), gut ILC3, Gut DC IL-23 production, Subclinical IBD (60%), Portal circulation, Molecular mimicry |
| 10. PK/PD Outputs | Free TNF/IL-17/IL-23, Disease activity (composite), BASDAI/ASDAS-CRP simulated, mSASSS progression, ASAS20/40, Trial calibration (ATLAS/MEASURE/COAST-V/SELECT-AXIS/GUIDE) |

**mrgsolve ODE Model (22 states):**

| Compartment Group | States | Description |
|-------------------|--------|-------------|
| Adalimumab PK | ADA_SC, ADA_C | 1-cmpt SC; ka=0.019/h, F=0.64, CL=9.6 mL/h, V=7600 mL, t┬╜έΚΙ14 d |
| Etanercept PK | ETA_SC, ETA_C | 1-cmpt SC; ka=0.048/h, F=0.76, t┬╜έΚΙ4 d |
| Secukinumab PK | SEC_SC, SEC_C, SEC_P | 2-cmpt SC; ka=0.015/h, F=0.73, CL=4.8 mL/h, Vc=3600, Vp=2800, Q=1.2 mL/h, t┬╜έΚΙ27 d |
| Tofacitinib PK | TOF_C | 1-cmpt oral; ka=1.5/h, F=0.74, CL=3500 mL/h, V=87000 mL, t┬╜έΚΙ3 h |
| Upadacitinib PK | UPA_C | 1-cmpt oral; ka=1.2/h, F=0.79, CL=8500 mL/h, V=96000 mL, t┬╜έΚΙ15 h |
| NSAID PK | NSAID_C | 1-cmpt oral; naproxen proxy, t┬╜έΚΙ12έΑΥ14 h |
| Cytokine PD | TNF, IL17A, IL23, IL6 | pg/mL; IL-17/IL-23 cross-drive; JAKi partial suppression of all; TNFi Emax=85%, IL-17Ai Emax=90% |
| Acute Phase | CRP | mg/L; IL-6-driven hepatic production; t┬╜έΚΙ19 h; ASDAS component |
| Bone remodeling | RANKL, OPG | AU; TNF upregulates RANKL, downregulates OPG; TNFi partially reverses |
| Osteoclast | OC | Activity (AU); driven by RANKL/OPG ratio ├Ω TNF; TNFi inhibits |
| Bone formation | BF | Syndesmophyte index; IL-17A + Wnt/BMP driven; TNF-DKK1 paradox modeled |
| Structural outcome | Erosion, mSASSS | Cumulative scores; mSASSS rate: IL-17Ai > TNFi inhibition |
| Composite disease | DiseaseAct | 0έΑΥ1 continuous; Kout model; maps to BASDAI/ASDAS |

**Key ODE Equations:**
- `dxdt_TNF = kprod_TNF ├Ω TNF_base ├Ω IL17_amp ├Ω HLA_factor έΙΤ kdeg_TNF ├Ω TNF ├Ω (1 + Inh_TNFi + 0.3├ΩInh_JAKi)`
- `dxdt_IL17A = kprod_IL17 ├Ω IL17_base ├Ω (1 + 0.6├ΩIL23_drv) ├Ω HLA_factor έΙΤ kdeg_IL17 ├Ω IL17A ├Ω (1 + Inh_IL17i + 0.2├ΩInh_JAKi)`
- `dxdt_BF = kform_BF ├Ω (1 + 0.5├ΩIL17A/IL17_base) ├Ω (1 έΙΤ 0.4├ΩInh_TNFi) έΙΤ kdeg_BF ├Ω BF` έΗΡ TNF-DKK1 paradox
- `dxdt_mSASSS = 0.00015 ├Ω BF ├Ω (1 έΙΤ 0.5├ΩInh_IL17i έΙΤ 0.3├ΩInh_TNFi)` έΗΡ IL-17Ai > TNFi for bone
- `BASDAI_sim = BASDAI_ss ├Ω DiseaseAct / 0.68`

**Clinical Trial Calibration:**

| Trial | Drug | n | Primary Endpoint | Observed | Model |
|-------|------|---|-----------------|---------|-------|
| ATLAS wk 24 | Adalimumab 40mg q2w | 208 | ASAS20 | 59% vs 22% PBO | έεΥ |
| MEASURE 1 wk 16 | Secukinumab 150mg | 371 | ASAS20 | 61% vs 29% PBO | έεΥ |
| GO-RAISE wk 24 | Golimumab 50mg q4w | 356 | ASAS20 | 59% vs 22% PBO | έεΥ (ADA proxy) |
| COAST-V wk 16 | Ixekizumab 80mg q4w | 341 | ASAS20 | 52% vs 18% PBO | έεΥ (SEC proxy) |
| SELECT-AXIS 1 wk 14 | Upadacitinib 15mg QD | 187 | ASAS40 | 52% vs 26% PBO | έεΥ |
| GUIDE | Guselkumab 100mg q8w | 474 | ASAS20 | active vs PBO | έεΥ (IL-23i class) |

**Treatment Scenarios (7 arms, 52-week simulation):**
1. Placebo έΑΦ Natural history; BASDAI ~6.8, ASDAS ~3.9, CRP ~15 mg/L
2. Adalimumab 40mg SC q2w έΑΦ TNFi; Inh_TNFi Emax=0.85
3. Etanercept 50mg SC qw έΑΦ TNFi (shorter t┬╜=4d); similar efficacy
4. Secukinumab 150mg SC (loading wk0έΑΥ4 then q4w) έΑΦ IL-17Ai; superior mSASSS suppression
5. Tofacitinib 5mg BID oral έΑΦ JAK1/3; ASAS40 ~40%; rapid onset (t┬╜ 3h)
6. Upadacitinib 15mg QD oral έΑΦ JAK1-selective; superior vs tofacitinib on bone
7. NSAID (naproxen equivalent) έΑΦ Symptom relief only; partial CRP reduction

**Shiny App (7 tabs):**

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| 1. Patient Profile | Demographics (WT, sex, HLA-B27), BASDAI/CRP/IL-17A baseline, prior TNFi history, disease severity classification, drug suitability radar chart |
| 2. Drug PK | ConcentrationέΑΥtime profiles (╬╝g/mL for biologics, ng/mL for JAKi), 2-cmpt SEC peripheral compartment, PK parameter table, Cmax/Tmax/AUC summary |
| 3. Disease Activity | BASDAI & ASDAS-CRP dual-axis plot, threshold annotations (BASDAI<4, ASDAS<2.1), CRP dynamics, TNF-╬▒ and IL-17A suppression side-by-side |
| 4. Structural Progression | mSASSS cumulative plot, bone formation vs erosion trajectories, RANKL:OPG ratio, TNF-DKK1 paradox bone interpretation |
| 5. Clinical Endpoints | ASAS20/40 probability over time, BASDAI50 milestone, response table at wk 4/12/16/24/52, trial benchmark comparison (ATLAS/MEASURE) |
| 6. Scenario Comparison | All 7 drugs overlay (BASDAI, TNF, mSASSS), Week-24 DT summary with BASDAI/ASDAS/CRP/ASAS20/40 by scenario |
| 7. Biomarker Dashboard | Selectable biomarkers (TNF, IL-17A, IL-23, IL-6, CRP, RANKL, OPG), drug efficacy inhibition % plot, osteoclast & bone formation time course |

### Atrial Fibrillation (AF)

> Directory: [`atrial-fibrillation/`](atrial-fibrillation/)

**Disease Summary**

Atrial fibrillation is the most common sustained cardiac arrhythmia, affecting >37 million people worldwide. AF arises from complex interactions among electrical remodeling (shortened ERP, conduction slowing), Ca┬▓έΒ║ handling disturbances (RyR2 leak έΗΤ DADs), structural fibrosis (AngII/TGF-╬▓1/SMAD), inflammation (NLRP3/IL-1╬▓/ROS), and autonomic nervous system dysregulation. The resulting wavelength shortening allows reentry circuits and focal pulmonary vein triggers to maintain AF ("AF begets AF"). Atrial stasis creates a prothrombotic state (Virchow's triad: stasis + endothelial dysfunction + hypercoagulability) that drives stroke risk. Management involves rate control (beta-blockers), rhythm control (antiarrhythmics), anticoagulation (DOACs), and upstream RAAS therapy.

**Key Pathways Modeled**

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| Risk Factors | HTN, HF, obesity, OSA, T2DM, genetic variants (PITX2, ZFHX3), atrial stretch |
| Electrical Remodeling | Nav1.5 (INa), Cav1.2 (ICaL), Kv1.5 (IKur), IKACh (Kir3.1/3.4), hERG (IKr), Cx40/43 gap junctions, ERP shortening, wavelength shortening, reentry circuits, focal PV triggers |
| Ca┬▓έΒ║ Handling | SERCA2a/PLN, RyR2 leak, NCX1, CaMKII oxidation, SR Ca┬▓έΒ║ overload, SOICR έΗΤ DADs/EADs |
| Structural Remodeling | AngII/AT1R/ACE, TGF-╬▓1/TGF╬▓R/SMAD2/3, myofibroblast, collagen I/III, MMP/TIMP, LAA enlargement, atrial fibrosis |
| Inflammation & ROS | NLRP3/caspase-1/IL-1╬▓, NF-╬║B, NOX2/mitochondrial ROS, superoxide/peroxynitrite, eNOS uncoupling, CRP |
| Autonomic NS | ╬▓1AR/cAMP/PKA, M2R/IKACh, ganglionated plexi, NE/ACh, sympatho-vagal remodeling |
| Thromboembolism | LAA stasis, TF/FVIIa/FXa/thrombin/fibrin cascade, platelet activation, protein C/AT-III, stroke |
| Drug PK | Amiodarone (3-cmt, t┬╜ ~40-55d, fat depot V2=4200L), Apixaban (2-cmt, t┬╜ 12h), Metoprolol (2-cmt, t┬╜ 3.5h), Flecainide, Rivaroxaban, Dabigatran, Warfarin, Digoxin |
| Drug PD | Class IέΑΥIV antiarrhythmics, IKur/IKACh blockade (atrial-selective), FXa/FIIa/VKA inhibition, ERP prolongation, QTc monitoring |
| Clinical Endpoints | AF burden (%), ERP (ms), QTc (ms), HR (bpm), NT-proBNP, CRP, LA diameter, stroke risk (%/year), fibrosis score |

**Drug PK/PD (Treatment Landscape)**

| Drug Class | Agent | Mechanism | Key Trial / Calibration |
|-----------|-------|-----------|------------------------|
| Class III Antiarrhythmic | Amiodarone 200mg/day (after loading) | IKr + ICaL + INa + IKACh block έΗΤ ERPέΗΣ + rate έΗΥ | Roy et al. NEJM 2000; AFFIRM arm |
| Class II (Rate Control) | Metoprolol 50mg BID | ╬▓1AR blockade έΗΤ HRέΗΥ | AFFIRM (NEJM 2002; PMID:12466506); RACE (NEJM 2002; PMID:12466507) |
| Direct FXa Inhibitor | Apixaban 5mg BID | Competitive FXa inhibition έΗΤ έΗΥthrombin generation | ARISTOTLE (NEJM 2011; PMID:21870978); RRR 21% vs warfarin |
| Direct Thrombin Inhibitor | Dabigatran 150mg BID | Direct FIIa inhibition | RE-LY (NEJM 2009; PMID:19717844) |
| Direct FXa Inhibitor | Rivaroxaban 20mg QD | Competitive FXa inhibition | ROCKET-AF (NEJM 2011; PMID:21830957) |
| Vitamin K Antagonist | Warfarin (INR 2έΑΥ3) | VKORC1 inhibition έΗΤ έΗΥF II/VII/IX/X synthesis | AVERROES (NEJM 2011; PMID:21309657) |
| Early Rhythm Control | Multiple agents | Earlier sinus rhythm έΗΤ structural prevention | EAST-AFNET 4 (NEJM 2020; PMID:32865375) |

| S6 | Rhythm + anticoag έΑΦ Amiodarone + Apixaban (SoC) | ~30% | ~1.0%/yr | ~74 bpm |

### Myasthenia Gravis (MG)

**ΉνΣΉοζ Ά╖╝Έυ┤ΈιξΉοζ** | Autoimmune / Neuromuscular Junction

**Mechanistic Map**

[![MG QSP Map](myasthenia-gravis/mg_qsp_model.png)](myasthenia-gravis/mg_qsp_model.svg)

*Click image to open interactive SVG. 16 pathway clusters: Thymus & Immune Priming ┬╖ B Cell & Plasma Cells ┬╖ Autoantibody (AChR/MuSK/LRP4) ┬╖ FcRn-IgG Homeostasis ┬╖ NMJ Structure ┬╖ ACh Neurotransmission ┬╖ Complement Cascade ┬╖ NMJ Damage ┬╖ Pyridostigmine PK/PD ┬╖ Corticosteroid/IS PK ┬╖ Biologic Drug PK ┬╖ Drug PD on Immune System ┬╖ Non-drug Interventions (PLEX/IVIG/Thymectomy) ┬╖ Muscle Physiology ┬╖ Clinical Endpoints ┬╖ Biomarker Panel*

**Key Pathways Modeled**

| Cluster | Key Nodes |
|---------|-----------|
| Thymus & Immune Priming | Thymoma, Thymic Hyperplasia, Myoid Cells (AChR+), Thymic DC, AIRE dysfunction, Naive T, Tfh (CXCR5+), Th1/Th17, Treg failure, Thymic GC reaction, HLA-DR3 |
| B Cell & Plasma Cells | Naive B, GC-B (affinity maturation/CSR), Memory B, SL-PC, LL-PC (BM niche), CD20+ B (Rituximab target), BCR specificity, CD40L-CD40, IL-21 signaling |
| Autoantibodies | Anti-AChR IgG (~85%, IgG1/3), Anti-MuSK IgG (~5-8%, IgG4), Anti-LRP4 (~1-3%), Titin/RyR Ab, IGG pool, NMJ-bound Ab |
| FcRn & IgG Homeostasis | FcRn (FCGRT/╬▓2m), endosome pH cycling, IgG recycling vs lysosomal degradation; Efgartigimod + Rozanolixizumab block FcRn έΗΤ 75% IgG reduction |
| NMJ Structure | ╬▒-motor neuron, axon terminal, presynaptic/postsynaptic membranes, junctional folds, AChR clusters (~10^7/NMJ, ╬╡-subunit adult), MuSK, LRP4, Agrin, Rapsyn, ColQ, Dystrophin complex |
| ACh Neurotransmission | CHT1/choline uptake, ChAT, VAChT, synaptic vesicles, Nav1.6 AP, VGCC (P/Q-type Cav2.1), SNARE complex, exocytosis, ACh-AChR binding (2 sites, ╬▒-subunit), AChE hydrolysis (kcat~1.4├Ω10έΒ┤/s); Pyridostigmine reversible carbamylation |
| Classical Complement | C1q recognition έΗΤ C1r/C1s έΗΤ C4b/C2a (C3 convertase) έΗΤ C3a/C3b έΗΤ C5 convertase έΗΤ C5 cleavage (eculizumab/ravulizumab/zilucoplan target) έΗΤ C5a (inflammation) + C5b έΗΤ C6-C9 έΗΤ MAC (C5b-9) έΗΤ NMJ pore |
| NMJ Damage | Ab crosslinking έΗΤ AChR internalization, complement MAC έΗΤ junctional fold destruction, ACh binding blockade (MuSK-Ab), AChR density έΗΥ, NMJ safety factor έΗΥ (normal 3-5├Ω), EPP amplitude έΗΥ έΗΤ subthreshold έΗΤ muscle AP failure έΗΤ fatigable weakness |
| Drug PK | Pyridostigmine (1-cmt oral, F~18%, Vd=1.3L/kg, ke=0.37/h); Prednisolone (2-cmt, F=82%, CL=0.3L/h/kg, CYP3A4); AZAέΗΤ6-MPέΗΤ6-TGN (TPMT/HGPRT, t┬╜(TGN)~5d); Eculizumab (2-cmt IV, Vss=7.7L, t┬╜=11d); Efgartigimod (2-cmt + FcRn binding, CL=0.15L/h) |
| Non-drug Interventions | Plasmapheresis (PLEX): acute IgG removal (days); IVIG: FcRn saturation έΗΤ έΗΥIgG t┬╜; Thymectomy: removes intrathymic GC source (MGTX: +5-year CSR benefit) |
| Muscle EC Coupling | Nicotinic ion channel opening έΗΤ muscle AP (Nav1.4) έΗΤ DHPR (T-tubule) έΗΤ RyR1 (SR Ca┬▓έΒ║ release) έΗΤ Troponin-C έΗΤ Tropomyosin shift έΗΤ Myosin-Actin crossbridge έΗΤ Contraction; SERCA Ca┬▓έΒ║ reuptake |
| Clinical Endpoints | QMG (0-39), MG-ADL (0-24), MGAS, MGFA class I-V, Myasthenic Crisis (FVC<50%), Ptosis, Diplopia, Dysphagia, Dysarthria, Respiratory failure; CSR, MMS |
| Biomarkers | Anti-AChR titer (nmol/L, RIA), Anti-MuSK (CBA/ELISA), Total IgG, SFEMG jitter (┬╡s), RNS decrement (>10%), sC5b-9, Blood Tfh %, CH50, Thymus CT |

**Drug PK/PD Summary**

| Drug | Class | Mechanism | Calibration Trial |
|------|-------|-----------|-------------------|
| Pyridostigmine 60mg q6h | AChEI (symptomatic) | Reversible AChE carbamylation έΗΤ έΗΣcleft ACh έΗΤ έΗΣNMJ safety factor | Huang et al. 2017 (PopPK); Breyer-Pfaff 1990 |
| Prednisolone 0.5έΑΥ1.5mg/kg/d | Corticosteroid | GR nuclear έΗΤ έΗΥNF-╬║B/IL-2/IL-17 έΗΤ έΗΥTfh/GC-B/SLPC | Palace et al. Neurology 1998 |
| Azathioprine 2έΑΥ3mg/kg/d | Antimetabolite (IMPDH/DNA) | 6-TGN έΗΤ IMPDH inhibition + DNA incorporation έΗΤ έΗΥlymphocyte proliferation | TPMT pharmacogenomics |
| Eculizumab 900mg q2w IV | Anti-C5 (complement) | Blocks C5 cleavage έΗΤ έΗΥC5a + έΗΥMAC έΗΤ NMJ protection | REGAIN (Howard et al. Lancet Neurol 2017; έΙΤ4.2 QMG vs placebo) |
| Ravulizumab 3000mg q8w IV | Anti-C5 (long-acting) | Same as eculizumab; recycled by FcRn έΗΤ t┬╜~49d | CHAMPION-MG (Vu et al. NEJM Evid 2022) |
| Zilucoplan 0.3mg/kg SC qd | Anti-C5 (peptide) | Subcutaneous C5 inhibitor; rapid onset | RAISE (Howard et al. JAMA Neurol 2023) |
| Efgartigimod 10mg/kg IV qw | Anti-FcRn | Competes for FcRn έΗΤ έΗΥIgG recycling έΗΤ ~75% total IgG έΗΥ in 4 wk | ADAPT (Howard et al. Lancet Neurol 2021) |
| Rozanolixizumab 1mg/kg SC qw | Anti-FcRn (mAb) | FcRn blockade έΗΤ IgG catabolism έΗΣ | MycarinG (Bril et al. Lancet Neurol 2023) |
| Rituximab 375mg/m┬▓ IV ├Ω4 | Anti-CD20 | ADCC + CDC + apoptosis έΗΤ B cell depletion; esp. effective in MuSK-MG | Tandan et al. Muscle Nerve 2017 (systematic review) |
| Thymectomy (VATS/robot) | Surgery | Removes intrathymic GC; long-term έΗΥSL-PC/LL-PC source | MGTX (Wolfe et al. NEJM 2016): QMG έΙΤ2.85, CSRέΗΣ at 5yr |

**ODE Model Summary** (20 compartments)

| State Group | Variables |
|-------------|-----------|
| Pyridostigmine PK (2) | GUT\_PYR, CENT\_PYR έΗΤ C\_PYR έΗΤ AChE\_INH (Emax, EC50=50ng/mL, ╬│=1.5) |
| Prednisolone PK (3) | GUT\_PRED, CENT\_PRED, PERIPH\_PRED έΗΤ GR activation έΗΤ immunosuppression |
| Azathioprine/6-TGN (3) | GUT\_AZA έΗΤ SIXMP (TPMT/HGPRT) έΗΤ SIXTGN (t┬╜~5d) έΗΤ IMPDH inh |
| Eculizumab PK (2) | CENT\_ECUL, PERIPH\_ECUL έΗΤ C5 inhibition (EMAX=0.99, EC50=100ng/mL) |
| Efgartigimod PK (2) | CENT\_EFGAR (free) + FCRN\_EFGAR (bound) έΗΤ FcRn occupancy έΗΤ έΗΣIgG degradation |
| Immune compartment (4) | TFH, GCB (logistic growth ├Ω Tfh), SLPC (t┬╜~17h), LLPC (t┬╜ years) έΗΤ suppressed by GR/6-TGN |
| AChR-Ab pool (1) | ACHR\_AB\_C: secreted by SL+LL PC, degraded via FcRn (K\_AB\_EFF = f[FcRn\_OCC]) |
| NMJ AChR density (1) | ACHR\_DEN: synthesized (K\_ACHR\_IN) έΙΤ degraded (K\_ACHR\_D) έΙΤ Ab-mediated downregulation |
| Complement activity (1) | COMP\_ACT: driven by ACHR\_AB\_C, decays, inhibited by eculizumab |
| NMJ Safety Factor (1) | NMJ\_SF = f(AChR\_DEN ├Ω 0.8 + ACh\_Avail ├Ω 0.2) έΗΤ drives QMG/MG-ADL |

**Treatment Scenarios (7)**

| Scenario | Regimen | QMG at 52wk | AChR-Ab | NMJ Safety Factor |
|----------|---------|:-----------:|:-------:|:-----------------:|
| S1 | Natural history (untreated) | ~30 (severe) | High (έΗΣ) | <0.5 (severelyέΗΥ) |
| S2 | Pyridostigmine 60mg q6h | ~22 (moderate) | Unchanged | ~0.85 (έΗΣAChE inh) |
| S3 | Pyridostigmine + Prednisolone | ~15 (mild-mod) | Moderate έΗΥ | ~0.80 |
| S4 | Pyridostigmine + Pred + AZA | ~10 (mild) | Substantial έΗΥ | ~0.90 |
| S5 | Eculizumab + Pyridostigmine | ~8 (mild) | Unchanged | ~0.95 (MACέΗΥ) |
| S6 | Efgartigimod + Pyridostigmine | ~8 (mild) | ~75% έΗΥ | ~0.92 |
| S7 | Rituximab + Pyridostigmine | ~9 (mild) | GCB/SL-PC έΗΥέΗΥ | ~0.88 |
