## Primary Biliary Cholangitis (PBC)

**Date added:** 2026-06-17 | **Directory:** [`primary-biliary-cholangitis/`](primary-biliary-cholangitis/)

[![PBC Mechanistic Map](primary-biliary-cholangitis/pbc_qsp_model.png)](primary-biliary-cholangitis/pbc_qsp_model.svg)

### Disease Overview

Primary Biliary Cholangitis (PBC) is a chronic, autoimmune, cholestatic liver disease characterized by progressive destruction of small intrahepatic bile ducts. It predominantly affects women (9:1 F:M ratio) and is hallmarked by anti-mitochondrial antibodies (AMA έΚξ1:40; έΚξ95% sensitivity) directed against the pyruvate dehydrogenase complex E2 subunit (PDC-E2). Without treatment, PBC progresses from bile duct inflammation (florid duct lesion) through ductopenia to biliary fibrosis, cirrhosis, and liver failure requiring transplantation.

### Key Pathophysiological Cascade

```
Genetic susceptibility (HLA-DRB1, IL12A/IL12RB2, STAT4)
+ Environmental triggers (xenobiotics, infection/molecular mimicry)
         έΗΥ
pDC έΗΤ TLR7/9 έΗΤ IFN-╬▒ έΗΤ Type I IFN signaling
         έΗΥ
CD4+ Th1 έΗΤ IFN-╬│ ┬╖ CD8+ CTL έΗΤ Perforin/Granzyme B
         έΗΥ
BEC apoptosis (FasL/TRAIL/CTL) + Impaired GSH secretion έΗΤ PDC-E2 apotope
         έΗΥ
AMA (IgM έΗΤ IgG class switch) ┬╖ BEC senescence έΗΤ SASP
         έΗΥ
Ductopenia (vanishing bile duct syndrome) έΗΤ ALPέΗΣέΗΣ
         έΗΥ
Cholestasis: Hydrophobic BA poolέΗΣ έΗΤ NLRP3/IL-1╬▓ έΗΤ Hepatocyte damage
         έΗΥ
TGF-╬▓1 / HSC activation έΗΤ Collagen I/III έΗΤ Fibrosis (Metavir F0έΗΤF4)
         έΗΥ
Portal hypertension ┬╖ Cirrhosis ┬╖ HCC (>15├Ω risk)
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug | Target | Mechanism | Key Trial | ALP Response |
|------|--------|-----------|-----------|:------------:|
| **UDCA** 13-15 mg/kg/d | FXR (partial) / BSEP / AE2 | Enriches hydrophilic BA pool; bicarbonate umbrella; BSEP/MRP2 induction; hepatoprotection | Lindor 1994, NEJM | 30-40% έΗΥ |
| **Obeticholic acid (OCA)** 5-10 mg/d | FXR agonist (100├Ω vs UDCA) | FXR έΗΤ FGF19έΗΣ έΗΤ CYP7A1έΗΥ; BSEPέΗΣ έΗΤ BA exportέΗΣ; ASBTέΗΥ έΗΤ BA reabsorptionέΗΥ | POISE (Nevens 2016, NEJM) | 38% έΗΥ |
| **Elafibranor** 80 mg/d | PPAR╬▒/╬┤ dual agonist | BA detoxification (UGT1A3έΗΣ glucuronidation; SULT2A1έΗΣ sulfation; CYP4A11έΗΣ ╧Κ-oxidation); anti-inflammatory; ABCG5/8έΗΣ | ELATIVE (Kowdley 2024, Lancet) έΑΦ **FDA Jun 2024** | **51% ALP normalization** |
| **Seladelpar** 10 mg/d | PPAR╬┤ selective | BA sulfationέΗΣ; GGTέΗΥ; pruritusέΗΥ (autotaxinέΗΥ); HMGCRέΗΥ | RESPONSE (Bowlus 2024, Lancet) έΑΦ **FDA Aug 2024** | **25% ALP normalization** |
| **Bezafibrate** 400 mg/d | pan-PPAR (╬▒>╬┤>╬│) | Broad BA detoxification; anti-fibrotic | BEZURSO (Corpechot 2018, NEJM) | **67% ALP normalization** |

### Clinical Endpoints

| Endpoint | Definition | Clinical Significance |
|----------|-----------|----------------------|
| ALP response | ALP <1.67├ΩULN + Bilirubin έΚνULN at 12m | Primary endpoint POISE; GLOBE-derived threshold |
| ALP normalization | ALP έΚνULN | Primary endpoint ELATIVE/RESPONSE |
| Paris II criteria | ALP <1.5├ΩULN + AST έΚν2├ΩULN + Bilirubin έΚνULN | Best validated biochemical surrogate |
| GLOBE score | 5-year transplant-free survival | Validated in 4,800 patients |
| UK-PBC score | 5/10-year liver-related mortality | Complementary to GLOBE |
| Pruritus NRS | 0-10 numeric rating scale | Key symptom endpoint; OCA limits |

### ODE Model Architecture (20 states)

| State Group | Variables | Biological Meaning |
|-------------|-----------|-------------------|
| Drug PK (10) | UDCA/OCA/ELF/SEL/BEZ (gut + central) | 1-compartment with EHC for UDCA |
| Immunology (3) | AMA, Th1, BEC_dmg | Core disease drivers |
| Bile acid axis (2) | BA_toxic, FGF19 | FXR-FGF19-CYP7A1 feedback loop |
| Biomarkers (4) | ALP, BILI, GGT, IgM | Primary clinical endpoints |
| Disease state (1) | Fibrosis (Metavir 0-4) | Long-term progression |

### Treatment Scenarios (7)

| Scenario | Regimen | ALP at M12 | ALP Normalization | Pruritus Effect |
|----------|---------|:----------:|:-----------------:|:---------------:|
| S1 | No treatment | ~3.5├ΩULN | 0% | Moderate |
| S2 | UDCA monotherapy | ~2.1├ΩULN | ~15% | Mild benefit |
| S3 | UDCA + OCA 5mg | ~1.5├ΩULN | ~30% | Worsened (dose-limiting) |
| S4 | UDCA + OCA 10mg | ~1.3├ΩULN | ~38% | Severely worsened |
| S5 | UDCA + Elafibranor 80mg | ~1.1├ΩULN | **~51%** | Improved |
| S6 | UDCA + Seladelpar 10mg | ~1.4├ΩULN | **~25%** | Improved |
| S7 | UDCA + Bezafibrate 400mg | ~1.0├ΩULN | **~55%** | Neutral |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| έΣι Patient Profile | Baseline ALP/Bilirubin/GGT/fibrosis stage; disease overview; drug information table; 4 KPI value boxes |

| έΣλ PD Biomarkers | ALP/Bilirubin/GGT (all ├ΩULN); IgM; FGF19 induction by OCA; Pruritus NRS (with OCA warning) |
| έΣμ Disease Biology | AMA titer; Th1 cell activity; BEC damage index (0-1); Toxic BA pool; Metavir fibrosis score |
| έΣν Clinical Endpoints | Paris II response; ALP normalization flag; GLOBE surrogate score; 12-month summary table |
| έΣξ Scenario Comparison | 7-scenario ALP/fibrosis/pruritus comparison plots; month-12 results DataTable |

## Hypertrophic Cardiomyopathy (HCM)

> **Category:** ΈπΝΉΕ▒ΉπΙΊβα / ΉΜυΊαΙΆ┤Α ┬╖ Chronic Disease / Cardiovascular
> **Directory:** [`hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/`](hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/)
> **Date added:** 2026-06-17

### Disease Overview

Hypertrophic cardiomyopathy (HCM) is the most prevalent inherited cardiac disease (~1:500 globally), caused primarily by pathogenic variants in sarcomere protein genes έΑΦ most commonly **MYH7** (╬▓-myosin heavy chain) and **MYBPC3** (cardiac myosin-binding protein C), together accounting for ~80% of genotype-positive cases. The hallmark pathology is unexplained left ventricular hypertrophy with non-dilated ventricle, typically asymmetric septal hypertrophy (ASH).

### Mechanistic Map

[![HCM QSP Model](hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/hcm_qsp_model.png)](hypertrophic-cardiomyopathy/hcm_qsp_model.svg)

*Click image to open the full-resolution SVG. 200+ nodes, 12 subgraph clusters.*

### Pathophysiology Summary

```
Sarcomere Gene Mutations (MYH7/MYBPC3/TNNT2/TNNI3/TPM1/MYL2)
         έΗΥ
έΗΥ SRX fraction (MYBPC3 stabilizes SRX) + έΗΣ DRX fraction
         έΗΥ
έΗΣ Duty Ratio (myosin heads in power stroke)
    έΗΤ Hypercontractility έΗΤ Venturi effect έΗΤ SAM έΗΤ LVOT obstruction
    έΗΤ έΗΣ ATP hydrolysis / MVOέΓΓ έΗΤ Microvascular ischemia
         έΗΥ
Calcineurin-NFAT + CaMKII/HDAC4/MEF2 + ERK1/2 (mechano-signaling)
         έΗΥ
Fetal gene reactivation έΗΤ Asymmetric LVH (IVSέΗΣέΗΣ, LV massέΗΣ)
         έΗΥ
TGF-╬▓1/SMAD2/3 έΗΤ FibroblastέΗΤMyofibroblast έΗΤ Collagen I/IIIέΗΣ
         έΗΥ
Interstitial fibrosis (ECVέΗΣ) + Replacement fibrosis (LGE+)
         έΗΥ
έΗΥ LV compliance έΗΤ LVEDPέΗΣ έΗΤ LA pressureέΗΣ έΗΤ AF (25έΑΥ30% lifetime)
         έΗΥ
RyR2 diastolic leak (DADs) + Myocyte disarray (reentry) + Scar substrate
         έΗΥ
VT έΗΤ VF έΗΤ Sudden Cardiac Death (SCD, 0.5έΑΥ1%/yr; έΚξ6% 5-yr = ICD)
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug | Class | Mechanism | Key Trial | Primary Effect |
|------|-------|-----------|-----------|:-------------:|
| **Mavacamten** 2.5έΑΥ15 mg QD | Cardiac myosin inhibitor | Shifts myosin from DRX έΗΤ SRX state (stabilizes super-relaxed); έΗΥ duty ratio; έΗΥ ATPase activity; CYP2C19-metabolized | EXPLORER-HCM (NEJM 2020) | LVOT έΗΥ36 mmHg |
| **Aficamten** | Next-gen cardiac myosin inhibitor | Competitive cardiac myosin ATPase inhibitor; shorter t┬╜ (~7h vs 6έΑΥ9d); more titratable | SEQUOIA-HCM (Lancet 2024) | LVOT έΗΥ36 mmHg |
| **Metoprolol / Bisoprolol** | ╬▓έΓΒ-Blocker | έΗΥ HR έΗΤ έΗΥ dynamic LVOT obstruction + έΗΥ contractility; έΗΥ Ca┬▓έΒ║ leak (PKA/PLB pathway) | Empirical use (no RCT) | HRέΗΥ, symptomέΗΥ |
| **Verapamil** | Non-DHP CCB | ICaL blockade έΗΤ HRέΗΥ + contractilityέΗΥ + LVOT gradientέΗΥ | Small RCTs | SymptomέΗΥ |
| **Disopyramide** | Class Ia antiarrhythmic | NaέΒ║ channel blockade έΗΤ έΗΥ SAM έΗΤ έΗΥ LVOT gradient; negative inotrope | Sherrid 2005 (JACC) | LVOT έΗΥ40% |
| **Furosemide/Torsemide** | Loop diuretic | Volume reduction έΗΤ έΗΥ LVEDP έΗΤ έΗΥ LA pressure έΗΤ έΗΥ congestion | Supportive | SymptomέΗΥ |
| **Surgical Myectomy / ASA** | Septal Reduction Therapy (SRT) | Direct removal/ablation of obstructing septum έΗΤ LVOTέΗΥέΗΥέΗΥ | Ommen 2005 (JACC) | LVOT έΗΥέΗΥέΗΥ |
| **NOAC / Warfarin** | Anticoagulation | Thrombin/FXa inhibition έΗΤ stroke prevention in AF | ARISTOTLE, RE-LY | Stroke riskέΗΥ |

### ODE Model Architecture (18 State Variables)

| Compartment Group | Variables | Biology |
|-------------------|-----------|---------|
| Mavacamten PK (3) | A_gut_m, A_c_m, A_p_m | 3-compartment PK; CYP2C19 EM/PM/UM adjustment |
| Beta-blocker PK (1) | A_bb | 1-compartment; metoprolol equivalents |
| Calcium dynamics (2) | Ca_cyt, Ca_SR | Cytosolic Ca┬▓έΒ║ (nM); SR Ca┬▓έΒ║ load (╬╝M) |
| Signaling (3) | Calcineurin, NFAT_nuc, ERK_act | Calcineurin-NFAT hypertrophy axis; ERK1/2 stress |
| Structural remodeling (4) | IVS, LVmass_rel, TGFb1, Collagen | IVS (mm); LV mass (relative); fibrosis drivers |
| Hemodynamics (3) | LVOT, LVEDP, HR_state | Key clinical hemodynamic endpoints |
| Biomarkers (2) | NT_proBNP, TroponinI | Wall stress biomarker; myocardial injury |
| AF risk (1) | AF_hazard | Cumulative AF incidence hazard |

### Treatment Scenarios (7)

| Scenario | Regimen | Key Effect at 52 Weeks |
|----------|---------|------------------------|
| S1 | Untreated HCM | Progressive LVOTέΗΣ, NT-proBNPέΗΣ, IVSέΗΣ |
| S2 | Mavacamten 5 mg QD (CYP2C19 EM) | LVOT έΗΥ~18 mmHg, NT-proBNP έΗΥ~35%, NYHA improved |
| S3 | Mavacamten 10 mg QD (EM) | LVOT έΗΥ~26 mmHg, NT-proBNP έΗΥ~50% |
| S4 | Mavacamten 2.5 mg QD (CYP2C19 PM) | Similar exposure to 10mg EM (έΗΣexposure due to έΗΥCL) |
| S5 | Beta-blocker 200 mg QD (metoprolol) | HRέΗΥ~28%, LVOT έΗΥ~12 mmHg (rate-dependent) |
| S6 | Mavacamten 5 mg + BB 100 mg | Additive: LVOT έΗΥ~22 mmHg, HRέΗΥ, symptom improvement |
| S7 | Post-SRT (Myectomy, IVS reset=11mm) | LVOT normalises (<10 mmHg), long-term fibrosis persists |

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| έΣι Patient Profile | Patient demographics, genotype, HCM phenotype, baseline hemodynamic parameters; mechanistic map thumbnail |

| έΣλ Cardiac Mechanics | LVOT gradient, LVEDP, LVEF, cardiac output, HR έΑΦ all over simulation period; 4 real-time value boxes |
| έΣμ Hypertrophy & Fibrosis | IVS thickness, collagen content, TGF-╬▓1, NFAT nuclear fraction, estimated CMR ECV (%) |
| έΣν Clinical Endpoints | NT-proBNP, Troponin I, NYHA class, peak VOέΓΓ; monthly results datatable |
| έΣξ Scenario Comparison | 7-scenario head-to-head comparison; primary outcome selector; 52-week summary table |
| έΣο Risk Assessment | HCM Risk-SCD calculator (O'Mahony 2014 formula); AF cumulative hazard; ICD indication tracker; risk factor contribution chart |

## Graves' Disease

> **Directory:** [`graves-disease/`](graves-disease/)

**ICD-10:** E05.0 ┬╖ **Category:** Autoimmune Endocrine Disease ┬╖ **Prevalence:** ~0.5% (F:M = 7έΑΥ10:1)

### Pathophysiology

Graves' disease is the most common cause of hyperthyroidism (~80% of cases). Thyroid-stimulating autoantibodies (TSAb) bind and constitutively activate the TSH receptor (TSHR) on thyroid follicular cells, bypassing normal HPT axis regulation.

| Module | Key Components |
|--------|---------------|
| **HPT Axis** | Hypothalamus έΗΤ TRH έΗΤ Pituitary έΗΤ TSH; dual T4/T3 Hill-kinetics negative feedback; circadian pulsatility; TSH suppression by high fT4/fT3 |
| **Autoimmune Pathogenesis** | CD4+/CD8+ T cells; Th1/Th2/Th17/Treg polarization; B-cell germinal center reaction; plasma cells έΗΤ TSAb (stimulating) / TBAb (blocking) / TBII; CTLA-4/HLA-DR3 genetic risk; CD40έΑΥCD40L costimulation |
| **Thyroid Follicular Cell** | TSHR/Gs-╬▒/cAMP/PKA/CREB signaling; NIS-mediated iodide uptake; DUOX2/HέΓΓOέΓΓ; TPO organification; MIT+DIT coupling έΗΤ T3/T4 synthesis; colloid storage; WolffέΑΥChaikoff effect + escape; goiter (VEGF/bFGF) |
| **Hormone PK/PD** | TBG/albumin/transthyretin binding; D1 (T4έΗΤT3 ~60%), D2 (local brain T3), D3 (T4έΗΤrT3 inactivation); TR-╬▒/TR-╬▓ nuclear signaling; enterohepatic recirculation (~20%) |
| **Drug PK** | MMI (F=93%, t┬╜=4-6h, high thyroid concentration); PTU (F=75%, t┬╜=1-2h, 75% protein-bound); ┬╣┬│┬╣I (FέΚΙ100%, NIS-mediated thyroid uptake ~60-80%); Propranolol (F=26%, first-pass, t┬╜=4h); LT4 replacement |
| **Drug PD** | MMI έΗΤ irreversible TPO inhibition + immunosuppression (TRAbέΗΥ); PTU έΗΤ TPO + D1 inhibition; ┬╣┬│┬╣I έΗΤ ╬▓-radiation thyroid cell death έΗΤ atrophy έΗΤ hypothyroidism; Propranolol έΗΤ ╬▓έΓΒ-blocker (HRέΗΥ) + D1 inhibition; Rituximab έΗΤ anti-CD20 B-cell depletion έΗΤ TRAbέΗΥ (delayed); Teprotumumab έΗΤ IGF-1R blockade έΗΤ GOέΗΥ |
| **Graves' Ophthalmopathy** | TSHR+IGF-1R on orbital fibroblasts; TRAb activation έΗΤ HAS1/HAS2 (hyaluronanέΗΣ) + PPAR-╬│ adipogenesis; orbital inflammation (TNF-╬▒/IL-6/Th1); EOM fibrosis έΗΤ proptosis + diplopia; CAS score; optic nerve compression |
| **Target Organ Effects** | Cardiovascular: tachycardia (HRέΗΣ20-40 bpm), AF risk (5-15%), έΗΣcardiac output, έΗΥSVR; Bone: osteoclastέΗΣ έΗΤ BMD loss (cortical > trabecular) έΗΤ fracture riskέΗΣ; CNS: anxiety/tremor/insomnia/hyperreflexia; Metabolic: BMRέΗΣ20-60%, weight loss, heat intolerance |
| **Clinical Endpoints** | TSH (suppressed <0.01), fT4έΗΣ, fT3έΗΣ, TRAb (>1.75 IU/L diagnostic), RAIUέΗΣ; Burch-Wartofsky score (thyroid storm); CAS score (GO); Hertel exophthalmometry; BMD Z-score |

### Model Specifications

| Feature | Detail |
|---------|--------|
| ODE Compartments | **18** (HPT axis + thyroid mass + T4/T3/fT4/fT3/rT3 pools + TRAb + B cells + bone resorption + heart rate + GO score + TPO inhibition) |
| Treatment Scenarios | **6**: Untreated ┬╖ MMI 30mg/day ┬╖ Radioiodine 15 mCi ┬╖ MMI+Propranolol ┬╖ Block-and-Replace (MMI+LT4) ┬╖ Rituximab+MMI |
| Virtual Population | n=200 with lognormal TRAbέΓΑ and ICέΓΖέΓΑ_MMI variability |
| Calibration | MMI PK: Walter 2012 (J Clin Pharmacol); TRAb dynamics: Eisenberg 2008; HPT feedback: Leow 2007 |
| Key Trials | CATS trial (MMI vs PTU safety); MINGO trial (rituximab+MP vs MP); OPTIC trial (teprotumumab) |

### Key Equations

```
TSHR_act  = E_TSH ├Ω TSH/(EC50_TSH + TSH) + E_TRAb ├Ω TRAb/(EC50_TRAb + TRAb)
T4_synth  = ksyn_T4 ├Ω ThyMass ├Ω TSHR_act ├Ω (1 έΙΤ TPO_inh)
TSH_prod  = ksyn_TSH / mean[(fT4/fT4_norm)^n, (fT3/fT3_norm)^n]
dTRAb/dt  = kprod_TRAb ├Ω Bcell έΙΤ kel_TRAb ├Ω TRAb
dGO/dt    = kGO_TRAb ├Ω TRAb ├Ω (1 έΙΤ GCS) έΙΤ kGO_kel ├Ω GO
```

### Files

| File | Description |
|------|-------------|
| [`gd_qsp_model.dot`](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.dot) | Graphviz DOT source (9 clusters: HPT axis ┬╖ autoimmune ┬╖ thyroid follicular cell ┬╖ hormone PK ┬╖ drug PK ┬╖ drug PD ┬╖ ophthalmopathy ┬╖ target organs ┬╖ clinical endpoints) |
| [`gd_qsp_model.svg`](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.svg) | Vector mechanistic map |
| [`gd_qsp_model.png`](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.png) | Raster mechanistic map (150 dpi) |
| [`gd_references.md`](graves-disease/gd_references.md) | 43 curated references (10 sections); Morshed 2015 (Endocr Rev) ┬╖ Smith 2016 (NEJM) ┬╖ Douglas 2020 (NEJM teprotumumab) ┬╖ Ross 2016 (ATA guidelines) |
| [`gd_mrgsolve_model.R`](graves-disease/gd_mrgsolve_model.R) | 18-state mrgsolve ODE; 6 treatment scenarios; VPop n=200; sensitivity analysis; calibrated to Walter 2012 / Eisenberg 2008 |
| [`gd_shiny_app.R`](graves-disease/gd_shiny_app.R) | 6-tab shinydashboard: Patient Profile ┬╖ Drug PK ┬╖ Thyroid Hormone PD ┬╖ Cardiovascular & Bone ┬╖ Immune & Ophthalmopathy ┬╖ Scenario Comparison |

[![Graves' Disease QSP Map](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.png)](graves-disease/gd_qsp_model.svg)

## Idiopathic Pulmonary Fibrosis (IPF)

> **Directory:** [`idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/`](idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/)

**ICD-10:** J84.112 ┬╖ **Category:** ΈπΝΉΕ▒ΉπΙΊβα / Ία╕ΊζκΆ╕░ ΉΕυΉειΊβΦ ┬╖ **Prevalence:** 13έΑΥ20 per 100,000; incidence rising with age (peak 60έΑΥ70 yrs)

### Pathophysiology

Idiopathic pulmonary fibrosis is a progressive, irreversible, and fatal fibrotic interstitial lung disease characterized by the **usual interstitial pneumonia (UIP)** histological pattern. The prevailing hypothesis centers on **repetitive alveolar epithelial injury** followed by aberrant wound healing driven by TGF-╬▓1.

[![IPF QSP Model](idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/ipf_qsp_model.png)](idiopathic-pulmonary-fibrosis/ipf_qsp_model.svg)

| Module | Key Components |
|--------|---------------|
| **Alveolar Epithelium (AEC I/II)** | AEC-II injury/senescence (ROS, ER stress, telomere shortening, MUC5B variant, TERT/SFTPC mutations) έΗΤ DAMP release έΗΤ ╬▒v╬▓6 integrin + TSP-1 activate latent TGF-╬▓1; KL-6 and SP-D biomarkers; Wnt/╬▓-catenin blocks AEC-II repair; EGF/HGF support regeneration (reduced in IPF) |
| **TGF-╬▓1/SMAD Signaling** | TGF╬▓1 (central driver): TGF╬▓RI/II έΗΤ pSMAD2/3 έΗΤ SMAD4 nuclear complex έΗΤ CTGF/PAI-1/fibronectin/Col1A1/TIMP-1 transcription; SMAD7 (negative feedback); non-SMAD (PI3K/AKT/MAPK/Rho) έΗΤ fibroblast proliferation/migration; LOX (collagen crosslinking) έΗΤ matrix stiffness έΗΤ mechanotransduction έΗΤ more TGF-╬▓ |
| **Macrophage Biology** | DAMP έΗΤ TLR4/TLR9 έΗΤ NLRP3 inflammasome έΗΤ IL-1╬▓/IL-18; AM έΗΤ M1 (TNF-╬▒/IL-6/MMP-12) or M2 (IL-4/IL-13/IL-10) polarization; M2 έΗΤ TGF-╬▓1/CTGF/osteopontin; CCL-18 as M2 biomarker |
| **Fibroblast/Myofibroblast** | Quiescent έΗΤ activated (TGF-╬▓/PDGF) έΗΤ myofibroblast (╬▒-SMA+); IPF fibroblasts epigenetically reprogrammed (bcl-2έΗΣ, apoptosis-resistant); YAP/TAZ/FAK/Rho-ROCK; CXCL12/SDF-1 recruits circulating fibrocytes (CD45+/Collagen+); senescent fibroblasts (SASP) amplify TGF-╬▓ |
| **ECM Remodeling** | Collagen I/III overproduction; MMP-1/-2/-7/-9/-13 (degradation) vs TIMP-1/-2 (inhibition) έΑΦ TGF-╬▓ tips balance toward TIMPέΗΣ έΗΤ fibrosis; MMP-7 serum biomarker; periostin stabilizes collagen; HA activates TLR4; matrix stiffness έΗΤ YAP/TAZ mechanotransduction feedback loop |
| **Growth Factors & Angiogenesis** | PDGF-AA/BB έΗΤ PDGFR╬▒/╬▓ έΗΤ fibroblast proliferation; FGF-2 έΗΤ FGFR1/2 έΗΤ fibroblast survival; VEGF-A έΗΤ VEGFR2 έΗΤ abnormal neovascularization; ET-1 έΗΤ ETA/ETB έΗΤ myofibroblast differentiation; platelet activation έΗΤ TGF-╬▓ release |
| **Oxidative Stress** | NOX4 (TGF-╬▓-induced) + mitochondrial ROS έΗΤ AEC-II damage + TGF-╬▓ activation; Nrf2/GSH/SOD defense; mTORέΗΣ έΗΤ fibroblast proliferation; mtDNA damage έΗΤ NLRP3; autophagy impairment |
| **Drug PK έΑΦ Pirfenidone** | F=81%, ka=1.74/h, t┬╜=2.4h, CL=8.4 L/h, V1=20.4 L; food delays Tmax (3h fed vs 1h fasted); CYP1A2 (85%) + CYP2C9/3A4 (15%); renal elimination (80%); EC50 ~30 ┬╡g/mL (TGF-╬▓ inhibition) |
| **Drug PK έΑΦ Nintedanib** | F=4.7% (P-gp/BCRP efflux limits absorption), ka=0.8/h, t┬╜=10h, CL=22 L/h, V1=730 L; CYP3A4 + UGT glucuronidation; biliary elimination (93%); IC50 ~20 nM (FGFR1); BIBF1202 active metabolite |
| **Drug PD Targets** | Pirfenidone: TGF-╬▓1έΗΥ / TNF-╬▒έΗΥ / PDGFέΗΥ / FGFέΗΥ / ROSέΗΥ; Nintedanib: VEGFR-1/2/3 / PDGFR╬▒/╬▓ / FGFR-1/2/3 / Src/Lck/RET competitive TKI |
| **Clinical Endpoints** | FVC% predicted (primary), DLCO%, TLC%, 6MWD, AE-IPF, HRCT honeycombing/GGO score, GAP index (Gender-Age-Physiology), all-cause mortality |
| **Comorbidities** | GERD/microaspiration, OSA, pulmonary hypertension, emphysema (CPFE), lung cancer (2έΑΥ3├Ω risk), smoking (major risk) |

### Drug Mechanisms

| Drug | Dose | Mechanism | Key Trial | Primary Outcome |
|------|------|-----------|-----------|-----------------|
| **Pirfenidone** | 801 mg TID oral | Anti-fibrotic/anti-inflammatory: έΗΥTGF-╬▓1 secretion, έΗΥPDGF, έΗΥTNF-╬▒, antioxidant (έΗΣGSH) | ASCEND (NEJM 2014) | έΙΤ47.9% FVC decline reduction vs placebo (p<0.001) |
| **Nintedanib** | 150 mg BID oral | Triple tyrosine kinase inhibitor: FGFR-1/2/3, VEGFR-1/2/3, PDGFR╬▒/╬▓ | INPULSIS-1/2 (NEJM 2014) | έΙΤ50.1% FVC decline reduction vs placebo (p<0.001) |
| **Combination** | Both agents | Additive/complementary mechanisms (different targets) | INJOURNEY (2018) | Numerically greater FVC preservation vs monotherapy |
| **N-Acetylcysteine** | 600 mg TID | GSH precursor έΗΤ antioxidant | PANTHER-IPF (NEJM 2012) | No benefit over placebo (monotherapy) |
| **Nintedanib (SSc-ILD)** | 150 mg BID | FGFR/VEGFR/PDGFR inhibition in systemic sclerosis-ILD | SENSCIS (NEJM 2019) | FVC decline reduced έΙΤ44% |

### Model Specifications

| Feature | Detail |
|---------|--------|
| ODE Compartments | **17** (Pirfenidone PK ├Ω3 + Nintedanib PK ├Ω3 + AEC2 + TGF-╬▓ + M2 + ROS + Fibroblast + Myofibroblast + Collagen + MMP + TIMP + FVC + DLCO) |
| Treatment Scenarios | **5**: Placebo ┬╖ Pirfenidone 801 mg TID ┬╖ Nintedanib 150 mg BID ┬╖ Combination ┬╖ Pirfenidone Low Dose (267 mg TID) |
| Clinical Calibration | ASCEND: έΙΤ47.9% FVC decline reduction; INPULSIS: έΙΤ50.1% FVC decline reduction; Natural history ~200 mL/yr |
| PK Sources | Pirfenidone: Rubino 2009 (J Clin Pharmacol); Nintedanib: Stopfer 2011 (Clin Pharmacokinet) |
| Biomarkers Tracked | MMP-7 (serum, proxy), KL-6 (proxy, U/mL scale), Periostin (proxy), TGF-╬▓1, collagen, MMP:TIMP ratio |
| Dose-Response | 4-dose pirfenidone (267έΑΥ1068 mg TID) ├Ω 4-dose nintedanib (50έΑΥ200 mg BID) |

### Key Equations

```
dAEC2/dt   = k_rep ├Ω (1 έΙΤ AEC2) έΙΤ k_AEC ├Ω ROS ├Ω AEC2
dTGFb/dt   = [kprod + kact├Ω(1έΙΤAEC2) + 0.06├ΩM2 + 0.04├ΩMyofib] ├Ω (1έΙΤinh_P) έΙΤ kdeg├ΩTGFb
inh_P      = Emax_P ├Ω Cp / (EC50_P + Cp)          // Pirfenidone Hill inhibition
inh_N      = Emax_N ├Ω Cn_nM / (EC50_N + Cn_nM)    // Nintedanib Hill inhibition
dMYOFIB/dt = kdiff ├Ω FIBRO ├Ω TGFb ├Ω (1 έΙΤ 0.5├Ωinh_N) έΙΤ 0.006├ΩMYOFIB
dCOL/dt    = kprod_col ├Ω MYOFIB έΙΤ kdeg_col ├Ω MMP/(TIMP+0.1) ├Ω COL
dFVC/dt    = έΙΤk_FVC ├Ω (COLέΙΤ1)έΓΛ ├Ω FVC              // FVC loss from collagen excess
GAP Score  = G(sex) + A(age) + P(FVC%) + P(DLCO%)  // O'Mahony 2014
```

### Shiny App (6 Interactive Tabs)

| Tab | Content |
|-----|---------|
| έΣι Patient Profile | Patient FVC/DLCO input; GAP score calculator (O'Mahony 2014 formula); natural history FVC trajectory; severity classification table |
| έΣκ Drug PK | Pirfenidone 72h plasma Cp (┬╡g/mL) vs EC50; Nintedanib 72h Cn (nM) vs IC50; PK parameter table; population PK variability (n=50 Monte Carlo, CV~30%) |
| έΣλ Lung Function | FVC% and DLCO% time-course; real-time value boxes (52-wk FVC, DLCO, decline, treatment response %); spirometry severity zones; annualized decline rate |
| έΣμ Biomarkers | TGF-╬▓1 & myofibroblast trajectories; ECM collagen/MMP/TIMP dynamics; serum MMP-7/KL-6/Periostin proxies; ROS & AEC-II integrity; biomarker correlation heatmap |
| έΣν Scenario Comparison | 5-scenario head-to-head FVC plot; summary datatable (Week 0/13/26/39/52); treatment effect bar chart vs placebo; pirfenidone & nintedanib dose-response curves |
| έΣξ Mechanistic Map | Full IPF mechanistic map PNG (130+ nodes, 12 clusters); pathway interaction table; drug mechanism target summary |

### Systemic Sclerosis (SSc)

> Directory: [`systemic-sclerosis/`](systemic-sclerosis/)

**Date added:** 2026-06-17  
**Category:** ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα / Ά▓░ΊΧσΉκ░ΉπΒ (Autoimmune / Connective Tissue Disease)

**Disease Overview:**  
Systemic sclerosis (SSc) is a rare systemic autoimmune disease defined by three hallmark pathological processes: **(1) autoimmunity** έΑΦ T/B cell dysregulation producing disease-specific autoantibodies (anti-Scl-70, anti-centromere, anti-RNA Pol III); **(2) vasculopathy** έΑΦ Raynaud's phenomenon, endothelial injury, ET-1 overproduction, digital ulcers, SSc-associated PAH; **(3) fibrosis** έΑΦ TGF-╬▓/SMAD2-3-driven myofibroblast activation, ECM accumulation causing skin (mRSSέΗΣ), lung (ILD/FVCέΗΥ), kidney (SRC), and GI tract fibrosis.

| Subtype | Skin | Key Ab | Organ Risk |
|---------|------|--------|------------|
| dcSSc (diffuse) | Proximal limbs + trunk | Anti-Scl-70 | ILD, SRC, cardiac |
| lcSSc (limited/CREST) | Hands + face | Anti-centromere | PAH, GAVE |
| SSc sine scleroderma | None | Variable | Internal organs only |

**Mechanistic Map** (15 clusters, >100 nodes):

[![SSc QSP Map](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.png)](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_qsp_model.svg)

**mrgsolve Model Summary:**

| Layer | State Variables | Key Equations |
|-------|----------------|---------------|
| Drug PK | 5 drugs: Nintedanib (2-cpt), TCZ (2-cpt IV), MPA/MMF (1-cpt), Bosentan (1-cpt), Iloprost (inhaled 1-cpt) | Multi-compartment ODEs with Hill PD effects |
| Cytokines | TGF-╬▓1, IL-6, Th17, Bnv | Production/degradation + drug inhibition |
| Fibrosis | FAct, Myo, Col1, Col3, ECM | Sequential activation cascade |
| Skin | mRSS (0-51) | ECM-driven logistic growth |
| Lung ILD | FVC %, DLCO % | FVC loss rate = kFVC ├Ω ECM ├Ω (1 έΙΤ E_NINT) |
| Vascular | ET-1, NO, PGI2, Endo, PVR, 6MWD | Bosentan: έΛμ ETAR; Iloprost: έΗΣ PGI2 analog |

**Treatment Scenarios (6):**
1. Untreated (natural history)
2. Nintedanib 150 mg BID έΑΦ SENSCIS (NEJM 2019; έΙΤ41% FVC decline)
3. Tocilizumab 8 mg/kg IV q4w έΑΦ focuSSced (Lancet RM 2020)
4. MMF 3000 mg/day έΑΦ SLS II (Lancet RM 2016)
5. Bosentan 125 mg BID έΑΦ ERA for PAH (RAPIDS-2: έΙΤ48% digital ulcers)
6. Full combination: Nintedanib + Tocilizumab + MMF

| [`ssc_references.md`](systemic-sclerosis/ssc_references.md) | 50 PubMed references (10 sections) |

## Gout

> Directory: [`gout/`](gout/)

**Date added:** 2026-06-17  
**Category:** ΈπΝΉΕ▒ΉπΙΊβα / ΈΝΑΉΓυ (Chronic Disease / Metabolic)

**Disease Overview:**  
Gout is the most prevalent inflammatory arthritis worldwide, caused by chronic hyperuricemia (serum urate >6.8 mg/dL) leading to monosodium urate (MSU) crystal deposition in joints and periarticular tissues. The disease progresses through four stages: **(1) asymptomatic hyperuricemia**, **(2) acute gouty arthritis flares** (NLRP3-driven IL-1╬▓ release), **(3) intercritical gout**, and **(4) chronic tophaceous gout** (visible crystal deposits, joint destruction). Gout is strongly associated with metabolic syndrome, CKD, cardiovascular disease, and hypertension.

### Key Pathophysiological Cascade

```
Dietary purines + Fructose + Endogenous synthesis
         έΗΥ  [Xanthine Oxidase (XO)]
    Hypoxanthine έΗΤ Xanthine έΗΤ Uric Acid
         έΗΥ
   Serum Urate Pool  έΗΡέΗΤ  URAT1 (reabsorption, 88%)
                          OAT1/OAT3 (secretion)
                          ABCG2 (gut + renal secretion)
         έΗΥ [>6.8 mg/dL in synovial fluid]
    MSU Crystal Nucleation & Growth
         έΗΥ [Phagocytosis by macrophages/neutrophils]
   NLRP3 Inflammasome Assembly (Signal 1: NF-╬║B; Signal 2: cathepsin B)
         έΗΥ [Caspase-1 activation]
    Pro-IL-1╬▓ έΗΤ Mature IL-1╬▓ (+ IL-18, Gasdermin D/pyroptosis)
         έΗΥ
   Neutrophil recruitment έΗΤ NETosis έΗΤ Joint inflammation
         έΗΥ
    Acute Flare (pain NRSέΗΣ, swelling, warmth, CRPέΗΣ)
         έΗΥ [chronic course]
    Tophus formation έΗΤ Cartilage/bone erosion
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug Class | Agents | Target | Clinical Evidence |
|-----------|--------|--------|-------------------|
| XO Inhibitors | Allopurinol (oxypurinol) | XO competitive inhibition | CONFIRMS trial (Becker 2005/2010) |
| XO Inhibitors | Febuxostat | XO non-purine selective | CONFIRMS: 80mg έΗΤ~70% sUAέΗΥ |
| Uricosurics | Probenecid | URAT1 blockade | Classical agent |
| Uricosurics | Lesinurad | URAT1 + OAT4 | CLEAR 1&2: +add-on 37% target |
| Colchicine | Low-dose colchicine | Tubulin / NLRP3 assembly | AGREE trial (Terkeltaub 2010) |
| NSAIDs | Indomethacin | COX-1/COX-2 | Acute flare standard |
| IL-1 biologics | Anakinra (IL-1Ra) | IL-1 receptor | Refractory flares |
| IL-1 biologics | Canakinumab (anti-IL-1╬▓) | Neutralizes IL-1╬▓ | CANTOS / So 2010 |

### Mechanistic Map

[![Gout QSP Map](gout/gout_qsp_model.png)](gout/gout_qsp_model.svg)

> **13 subgraph clusters ┬╖ 120+ nodes ┬╖ 100+ edges**  
> Purine Metabolism ┬╖ XO-Inhibitor PK ┬╖ Uricosuric PK ┬╖ Renal Transport (URAT1/OAT/ABCG2) ┬╖ Systemic Urate Distribution ┬╖ Crystal Formation & Synovial Compartment ┬╖ NLRP3 Inflammasome ┬╖ Inflammatory Mediators ┬╖ Cellular Response ┬╖ Anti-inflammatory Drug PK ┬╖ IL-1 Biologic PK ┬╖ Clinical Endpoints ┬╖ Comorbidities & Genetics

### ODE Model Architecture (33 state variables)

| Compartment | States | Key Equations |
|-------------|--------|---------------|
| Urate Distribution | A_UA_cent, A_UA_peri, A_UA_syn | Production (XO) έΙΤ Renal CLr έΙΤ Gut ABCG2 έΙΤ Distribution |
| Crystal & Tophus | A_Crystal, A_Tophus | Crystal = k_form┬╖(sUAέΙΤsat)έΒ║ έΙΤ k_diss έΙΤ PMN clearance |
| Inflammasome | A_IL1b, A_TNFa, A_PMN, A_Pain | NLRP3 activation έΗΤ Caspase-1 έΗΤ IL-1╬▓; Neutrophil influx |
| Disease Outcomes | A_JointDmg, A_eGFR | Linear damage accumulation; Urate-nephropathy eGFR decline |
| Allopurinol/Oxypurinol | A_Allo_gut, A_Allo_cent, A_Oxy_cent, A_Oxy_peri | 2-cpt + metabolite; XO inhibition: I=C/(C+Ki) |
| Febuxostat | A_Febu_gut, A_Febu_cent, A_Febu_peri | 2-cpt; Ki=1 nM (potent non-purine XO inhibitor) |
| Probenecid | A_Prob_gut, A_Prob_cent, A_Prob_peri | 2-cpt; URAT1 IC50=5 mg/L |
| Lesinurad | A_Lesi_gut, A_Lesi_cent | 1-cpt; URAT1/OAT4 IC50=0.1 mg/L |
| Colchicine | A_Colch_gut, A_Colch_cent, A_Colch_peri | 2-cpt; NLRP3 assembly έΛμ Emax=85% |
| Indomethacin | A_Indo_gut, A_Indo_cent, A_Indo_tiss | 2-cpt; COX inhibition |
| Anakinra | A_Ana_SC, A_Ana_cent, A_Ana_peri | SC 2-cpt; IL-1Ra receptor blockade |
| Canakinumab | A_Cana_SC, A_Cana_cent, A_Cana_peri, A_IL1b_Cana | SC TMDD; IL-1╬▓ neutralization + catabolism |

### Treatment Scenarios (8)

| # | Scenario | Rationale |
|---|----------|-----------|
| 1 | Untreated hyperuricemia | Natural history baseline |
| 2 | Allopurinol 300 mg/day | Standard first-line ULT |
| 3 | Febuxostat 80 mg/day | Potent XO inhibitor (non-purine) |
| 4 | Allopurinol 300mg + Lesinurad 200mg | Dual mechanism combo (CLEAR studies) |
| 5 | Colchicine 1.2mg + 0.6mg (low-dose) | Acute flare: AGREE regimen |
| 6 | Indomethacin 50mg TID | Acute flare: NSAID regimen |
| 7 | Canakinumab 150mg SC | Refractory flares / biologic |
| 8 | Febuxostat 80mg + Colchicine prophylaxis 0.5mg/day | ULT + flare prevention |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ Demographics, diet/alcohol, CKD, ABCG2 Q141K polymorphism, drug dose sliders
2. **Serum Urate (sUA)** έΑΦ sUA trajectory, target attainment, XO inhibition %, crystal burden, tophus volume
3. **Inflammation & Pain** έΑΦ IL-1╬▓ dynamics, neutrophil influx, NRS pain score, flare duration
4. **Clinical Endpoints** έΑΦ eGFR trajectory, joint damage accumulation, flare risk, outcomes table
5. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ Up to 5 pre-defined treatment scenarios plotted side by side
6. **Biomarkers & Genetics** έΑΦ CRP proxy, ABCG2/URAT1/GLUT9 genetics, NLRP3 pathway summary, HLA-B*58:01
7. **References** έΑΦ Pivotal trials, guidelines, CPIC pharmacogenomics

## Sj├╢gren's Syndrome (pSS)

> **ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα / Ήβ╕Έ╢ΕΈ╣ΕΉΕι (Autoimmune / Exocrine Glands)**  
> ΈΣΡ Έ▓ΙΉπ╕Έκε ΊζΦΊΧε ΉιΕΉΜι ΉηΡΆ░ΑΈσ┤ΉΩφΉπΙΊβα (F:M = 9:1; ΉειΈ│ΣΈξι ~0.1έΑΥ0.4%)

### Mechanistic Map

[![pSS QSP Map](sjogrens-syndrome/ss_qsp_model.png)](sjogrens-syndrome/ss_qsp_model.svg)

> **12 subgraph clusters ┬╖ 180+ nodes ┬╖ 200+ edges**  
> Genetic Triggers ┬╖ Innate Immune Activation (pDC/TLR7/9/cGAS-STING/NETs/NLRP3) ┬╖ T-cell Compartment (Th1/Th17/Tfh/Treg) ┬╖ B-cell Activation & Autoantibody (Anti-SSA/SSB/M3R/AQP5 + BAFF/APRIL/GC) ┬╖ Salivary Gland Pathology (AQP5/M3R/Ca┬▓έΒ║/UWSF) ┬╖ Lacrimal/Ocular Surface ┬╖ Systemic Extraglandular Manifestations ┬╖ Lymphoproliferation & MALT Lymphoma (FFS score) ┬╖ Intracellular Signaling (JAK-STAT/NF-╬║B/PI3K/BTK) ┬╖ Drug PK Compartments ┬╖ Drug PD Mechanisms ┬╖ Biomarkers & Clinical Outcomes

### Pathophysiology Summary

```
Genetic susceptibility (HLA-DR3, IRF5, STAT4, BLK, TNFAIP3)
+ Environmental trigger (EBV/UV/oxidative stress)
         έΗΥ
Apotope release (Ro52/Ro60 on apoptotic blebs)
         έΗΥ
pDC: TLR7/9 + cGAS-STING έΗΤ IRF7/IRF3 έΗΤ Type I IFN (IFN-╬▒/╬▓)
         έΗΥ [ISG signature in 75% of pSS patients]
IFN-I έΗΤ BAFFέΗΣ (BEC/macrophage) + mDC maturation
         έΗΥ
T-cell priming: Th1 (IFN-╬│/TNF-╬▒) + Th17 (IL-17A/IL-21) + Tfh
         έΗΥ                                        έΗΥ
Glandular infiltration έΗΡέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑέΦΑ B-cell activation
(CD4+ periductal foci)              BAFF-R + CD40/CD40L + BCR
(focus score έΚξ1/4mm┬▓)              έΗΥ
         έΗΥ              GC formation έΗΤ Anti-SSA/Ro52(>95%) + Anti-SSB/La
Acinar apoptosis (FasL)  + Anti-M3R έΗΤ M3R blockade έΗΤ cAMP/Ca┬▓έΒ║ έΗΥ
AQP5 downregulation                 έΗΤ AQP5 internalization έΗΥ
         έΗΥ                                    έΗΥ
UWSF έΗΥ (<1.5 mL/15 min)     Lacrimal: Schirmer έΚν5 mm/5 min
Xerostomia (dental caries,    Keratoconjunctivitis sicca
dysphagia, oral candida)      MMP-9έΗΣ, tear osmolarityέΗΣ
         έΗΥ [chronic course; 40έΑΥ50├Ω lymphoma risk]
Ectopic GC (CXCL13/CXCL12) έΗΤ B-cell clonal expansion
         έΗΥ
MALT lymphoma έΗΤ DLBCL (MYC rearrangement)
FFS score: low C4 + ╬▓έΓΓ-MGέΗΣ + cryos + parotid enlargement
```

### Drug Mechanisms Modeled

| Drug | Target | Mechanism | Key Trial |
|------|--------|-----------|-----------|
| Hydroxychloroquine (HCQ) | TLR7/9 (lysosomal) | pHέΗΣ έΗΤ pDC inhibition έΗΤ IFN-IέΗΥ | JOQUER (Ann Rheum Dis 2014) |
| Pilocarpine (Salagen 5 mg QID) | M3-muscarinic receptor | Cholinergic agonist έΗΤ Ca┬▓έΒ║/cAMPέΗΣ έΗΤ UWSF/tearέΗΣ | Papas 2004 (J Rheumatol) |
| Cevimeline (Evoxac 30 mg TID) | M3R (selective) | Selective M3R agonist | Fife 2002 (J Rheumatol) |
| Rituximab (2├Ω1g IV) | CD20 (B cells) | CDC/ADCC έΗΤ B-cell depletion | TEARS trial (Devauchelle-Pensec 2014) |
| Ianalumab (300 mg SC q4w) | BAFF-R | B-cell depletion via BAFF-R blockade | TWINSS Phase 3 (Bowman 2022, Lancet) |
| Iscalimab (anti-CD40) | CD40 (B cell) | TέΑΥB interactionέΗΥ έΗΤ GC disruption | Fisher 2020 (Ann Rheum Dis) |
| Baricitinib (2έΑΥ4 mg QD) | JAK1/2 | IFN-I/IL-6 signalingέΗΥ έΗΤ ESSDAIέΗΥ | Bowman 2023 (Arthritis Rheumatol) |
| Topical CsA 0.05% | Calcineurin | NFATέΗΥ έΗΤ corneal T-cellέΗΥ | Sall 2000 (Ophthalmology) |
| Lifitegrast 5% drops | LFA-1/ICAM-1 | T-cell corneal adhesionέΗΥ | OPUS-3 (Holland 2017) |

### ODE Model Architecture (19 state variables)

| Compartment Group | States | Key Equations |
|-------------------|--------|---------------|
| HCQ PK (3-cmt) | DEPOT_HCQ, C1_HCQ, C2_HCQ | F=0.74, Ka=0.05/h, Vd=750 L/kg; t┬╜έΚΙ40 d (tissue accumulation) |
| Pilocarpine PK | DEPOT_PIL, C_PIL | 1-cmt oral; EC50_PIL=80 ng/mL έΗΤ UWSF increase |
| Rituximab PK | C1_RTX, C2_RTX | 2-cmt; CL=0.20 L/h; Hill: E=(CέΒ┐)/(EC50έΒ┐+CέΒ┐); EMAX=90% |
| Ianalumab PK | C1_IAN, C2_IAN | IgG1 mAb; CL=0.18 L/h; EC50=8 mcg/mL; EMAX=88% |
| Prednisolone PK | DEPOT_PRD, C_PRD | 1-cmt; GRέΗΤNF-╬║BέΗΥ; max 50% cytokine suppression |
| Type I IFN (PD) | IFN | KIN_IFN ├Ω STIM ├Ω (1έΙΤHCQ_inh) έΙΤ KOUT ├Ω IFN |
| BAFF (PD) | BAFF_pd | KIN ├Ω (1+(STIM_BAFέΙΤ1)├ΩIFN) ├Ω (1έΙΤPRD) έΙΤ KOUT├ΩBAFF |
| B cells (PD) | BCELL | KIN ├Ω (1+(STIM_BCέΙΤ1)├ΩBAFF) ├Ω (1έΙΤRTX_depέΙΤIAN_dep) έΙΤ KOUT├ΩBC |
| Plasma cells | PLASMA_C | Input from BC ├Ω (1έΙΤ0.3├ΩRTX) έΙΤ KOUT_PC ├Ω PC |
| Anti-SSA titer | AB_SSA | KIN ├Ω (1+(STIM_ABέΙΤ1)├ΩPC) έΙΤ KOUT_AB ├Ω AB; t┬╜έΚΙ96 d |
| Salivary function | SAL | KIN ├Ω SAL_tgt ├Ω (1+PIL_stim) έΙΤ KOUT ├Ω SAL |
| Lacrimal function | LAC | KIN ├Ω LAC_tgt ├Ω (1+0.4├ΩPIL_stim) έΙΤ KOUT ├Ω LAC |
| ESSDAI (proxy) | ESSDAI_pd | Driven by BCELL+IFN+AB; scaled to clinical 0έΑΥ123 |
| Lymphoma risk | LYMPHOMA | dLR/dt = k_LR ├Ω BCELL ├Ω BAFF (cumulative integrator) |

### Treatment Scenarios (5)

| # | Scenario | Key Effect | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-----------|-------------------|
| 1 | No treatment | Progressive glandular loss, lymphoma risk έΗΣ | Natural history |
| 2 | HCQ 400 mg/day | IFN-IέΗΥ via TLR7/9 block; modest ESSDAIέΗΥ | JOQUER 2014 |
| 3 | HCQ + Pilocarpine 5 mg QID | Symptomatic UWSFέΗΣ + SchirmerέΗΣ; no systemic effect | Papas 2004 |
| 4 | HCQ + Rituximab 2├Ω1g | B-cell depletion έΗΤ BAFFέΗΥ + Anti-SSAέΗΥ + ESSDAIέΗΥ | TEARS 2014 |
| 5 | HCQ + Ianalumab 300 mg q4w | BAFF-RέΑΥmediated B-cell depletion; ESSDAI response έΚξ3 | TWINSS 2022 (Lancet) |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ ESSDAI/ESSPRI info boxes; Schirmer & UWSF; ACR/EULAR classification criteria table
2. **Drug PK Profiles** έΑΦ HCQ steady-state, pilocarpine single-dose, rituximab 2-dose, ianalumab q4w concentration-time plots
3. **Disease Biomarkers** έΑΦ IFN-I index, BAFF pg/mL, B-cell pool %, Anti-SSA EU; biomarker summary table at weeks 24/52
4. **Glandular Function** έΑΦ UWSF, Schirmer, pilocarpine on/off comparison, glandular function table
5. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ ESSDAI, B cells, Anti-SSA, UWSF for all 5 scenarios; endpoint comparison table at week 24
6. **Lymphoma Risk** έΑΦ FFS score calculator, cumulative risk plot, CXCL13/B-cell ectopic GC dynamics, FFS component table

## Type 1 Diabetes Mellitus (T1DM)

> Directory: [`type1-diabetes/`](type1-diabetes/)

**Mechanistic Map** (12 clusters, 130+ nodes):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Susceptibility | HLA-DR3/DR4, PTPN22, CTLA4, IL2RA, INS-VNTR, IFIH1/MDA5; enterovirus/CVB, gut dysbiosis, early nutrition, vitamin D |
| Innate Immunity | pDC έΗΤ IFN-╬▒/╬▓ (Type I IFN); mDC maturation; macrophage M1; NK; NLRP3/IL-1╬▓; TLR3/7; RIG-I/MDA5/cGAS-STING; CXCL10 |
| Adaptive Immunity (T cells) | Naive CD4+έΗΤTh1/Tfh; Naive CD8+έΗΤCTLέΗΤMemory; TCR activation; IFN-╬│/TNF-╬▒/IL-2; Perforin/GrB; FasL/TRAIL; CTLA-4/PD-1 coinhibition; Treg (FoxP3+) |
| B Cells & Autoantibodies | Naive BέΗΤGC BέΗΤPlasma cell; BAFF/APRIL; IAA (1st Ab) + GADA + IA-2A + ZnT8A; multi-Ab staging (Stage 1έΑΥ3) |
| Beta-cell Insulitis & Destruction | Islet infiltration; MHC-I upregulation (IFN-╬│); ER stress (BiP/IRE1╬▒/PERK); ROS/RNS; mitochondrial dysfunction; Caspase-3 apoptosis; Bm decline |
| Beta-cell Biology & GSIS | GLUT2/GCK έΗΤ ATP/ADP έΗΤ KATP closure έΗΤ depolarisation έΗΤ VGCC έΗΤ Ca┬▓έΒ║ έΗΤ exocytosis; GLP-1R/GIP-R έΗΤ cAMP έΗΤ amplification; proinsulin έΗΤ C-peptide |
| Glucose Homeostasis | Gut Ra; plasma glucose [G]; hepatic EGP + GU + glycogen; muscle/adipose GLUT4; brain; renal SGLT2; glucagon (╬▒-cell); IR signalling (IRS1/PI3K/Akt); HbA1c; AGEs |
| Insulin PK (Therapeutic) | SC depot (hexamerέΗΤmonomer); central + peripheral compartments; hepatic/renal clearance; basal (Glargine/Degludec) + bolus (Aspart/Lispro/Fiasp); CSII pump; CGM έΗΤ APC/HCL |
| Disease-Modifying Immunotherapy | Teplizumab (anti-CD3, TN-10); Abatacept (CTLA4-Ig); Rituximab (anti-CD20); ATG+G-CSF; Baricitinib (JAK1/2, BANDIT); Low-dose IL-2; CAR-Treg; Islet Tx; SC-islets (VX-880) |
| Adjunctive Pharmacotherapy | SGLT2i (sotagliflozin/empagliflozin); GLP-1RA (semaglutide); Pramlintide (amylin); Metformin; ACEi; Statin |
| Chronic Complications | AGE/RAGE έΗΤ PKC/polyol/hexosamine έΗΤ ROS; Nephropathy (TGF-╬▓1/SMAD); Retinopathy (VEGF/pericyte loss); Neuropathy (axonal); CVD; Hypoglycaemia unawareness |
| Clinical Endpoints & Biomarkers | HbA1c (<7%); TIR 70έΑΥ180 (>70%); TBR <70 (<4%); TAR >180 (<25%); C-peptide AUC (MMTT); insulin TDD; eGFR/UACR; LDL-C; DQOL/PAID |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![T1DM QSP Map](type1-diabetes/t1dm_qsp_model.png)](type1-diabetes/t1dm_qsp_model.svg)

### ODE Compartments (20 states)

| Compartment | State | Description |
|-------------|-------|-------------|
| Beta-cell & Immune | Bm, CTL, Treg | Normalised beta-cell mass; pathogenic CTL; regulatory T cells |
| C-Peptide | Cpep | Endogenous secretion marker (pmol/L) |
| Glucose kinetics | Gp, Gt | Plasma and tissue glucose (mg/dL) |
| Insulin PK | SC1, SC2, Ic, Ip | SC hexamer, monomer depots; central + peripheral plasma |
| Insulin action | X_ins | Remote effect compartment (Akt/GLUT4 proxy) |
| Glucagon | Gcg | ╬▒-cell glucagon (pg/mL); EGP counter-regulation |
| HbA1c | HbA1c | Running-mean glycation proxy (ADAG equation) |
| Teplizumab PK | Ctep | IV anti-CD3 mAb (╬╝g/mL); CTLέΗΥ/TregέΗΣ MOA |
| CGM / APC | CGM_comp, APC_integral | Interstitial glucose (10-min lag); PID integral state |
| Meal absorption | Qsto1, Qsto2, Qgut | Dalla Man 3-compartment gut model |
| Mean glucose | MG_avg | 30-day running average for HbA1c / complication risk |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Key Modelled Effect | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|---------------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Untreated T1DM | Progressive BmέΗΥ, HbA1cέΗΣ >10%, DKA risk | Natural history |
| 2 | MDI (Basal + Bolus) | HbA1c target ~7%; TIR ~50έΑΥ60% | DCCT 1993 (intensive arm) |
| 3 | CSII (Insulin Pump) | HbA1c έΙΤ0.3% vs. MDI; TIR +8% | TREAT trial 2019 |
| 4 | Hybrid Closed-Loop (HCL/APC) | TIR +11%, TBR έΙΤ1%, HbA1c έΙΤ0.5% | NEJM Breton 2020 |
| 5 | Teplizumab (Stage 2 prevention) | Bm stabilised, T1DM onset delayed ~3 yrs | TN-10 (Herold NEJM 2019) |
| 6 | Teplizumab + MDI (Stage 3 onset) | C-peptide preserved; insulin TDD έΗΥ ~30% | AT-RISK 2023, Sims 2021 |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ Disease stage value boxes (HbA1c/C-peptide/Bm); autoantibody prevalence bar chart; T1DM natural history curve (╬▓-cell + glucose)
2. **Insulin PK** έΑΦ Insulin type selector (5 types); SC concentrationέΑΥtime plot; PK parameter table (Tmax, duration, CL, ka)
3. **Glucose & CGM** έΑΦ Full glucose trace with TIR band; Ambulatory Glucose Profile (percentiles); CGM metric table; glucose zone histogram
4. **Beta-cell & Immunity** έΑΦ Beta-cell mass trajectory; CTL & Treg dynamic panels; C-peptide AUC plot; kDest sensitivity analysis
5. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ 6-scenario HbA1c + Bm traces; CGM metric comparison table (TIR/TBR/TAR/GMI)
6. **Biomarkers & Complications** έΑΦ Cumulative complication risk (nephropathy/retinopathy/neuropathy); 10-yr risk table; HbA1c vs. complication probability curves
7. **About** έΑΦ Model description, clinical trial calibration table, technical references

## Psoriatic Arthritis (PsA)

> Directory: [`psoriatic-arthritis/`](psoriatic-arthritis/)

**Mechanistic Map** (14 clusters, 130+ nodes):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Risk | HLA-C*06:02 (PSORS1), HLA-B27 (axial/enthesitis), IL23R, TNFAIP3 (A20), PTPN22, LCE3B/C (barrier), Koebner phenomenon, Strep guttate trigger |
| Innate Immune Activation | pDC έΗΤ IFN-╬▒; mDC (cDC1); Macrophage M1/M2; Neutrophil (CXCL1/8-driven, Munro microabscess); Mast cell; ILC2/ILC3; NK cell (KIR3DL2/HLA-B27); DAMP (HMGB1/S100A8/9); TLR2/4/7/9; NLRP3/Caspase-1/IL-1╬▓/IL-18 |
| Adaptive Immunity | Th17 (ROR╬│t/STAT3), Th1 (T-bet/STAT4), Th22, Treg, CD8+ CTL, Tfh/B cell/Plasma cell, MAIT, ╬│╬┤ T; IL-23 έΗΤ STAT3 έΗΤ ROR╬│t έΗΤ Th17; IL-12 έΗΤ STAT4 έΗΤ T-bet έΗΤ Th1 |
| Cytokine Network | IL-17A/F ┬╖ IL-22 (KC hyperplasia) ┬╖ TNF-╬▒ ┬╖ IL-1╬▓ ┬╖ IL-6 ┬╖ IL-8/CXCL8 ┬╖ IL-18 ┬╖ IL-10 ┬╖ IL-36╬▒/╬▓/╬│ ┬╖ IFN-╬│ ┬╖ TGF-╬▓1 ┬╖ VEGF ┬╖ MMP-3 ┬╖ S100A8/9 ┬╖ CXCL10 ┬╖ CCL20 (CCR6έΗΤTh17) ┬╖ OSM |
| JAK-STAT / NF-╬║B / cAMP | JAK1/2/3/TYK2 έΗΤ STAT3/4/6/1; NF-╬║B/IKK/AP-1/p38 MAPK/ERK; PDE4 έΗΤ cAMP έΗΤ PKA έΗΤ NF-╬║BέΗΥ; PI3K/Akt έΗΤ mTOR (Th17 metabolics) |
| Skin Pathology | Keratinocyte έΗΤ KC activated (IL-17/IL-22/TNF/IL-36); LL-37/╬▓-defensin AMPs έΗΤ TLR7/9 auto-DNA loop; Acanthosis + parakeratosis έΗΤ PASI; Neutrophil Munro microabscess; VEGF angiogenesis; Hair follicle pDC reservoir |
| Enthesis Pathology | Fibrocartilage + mechanical stress έΗΤ Bone marrow ILC3/╬│╬┤T έΗΤ IL-17 local; IL-23 DAMP; Enthesophyte (new bone)/erosion; Dactylitis (sausage digit); Axial disease (sacroiliitis; HLA-B27 UPR έΗΤ IL-23) |
| Synovium & Joint | FLS quiescent έΗΤ activated (invasive pannus); RANKL έΗΤ osteoclast έΗΤ erosion; COX-2/PGE2 vasodilation/edema; SJC66/TJC68/DAPSA/MDA/PsARC endpoints; RF-/ACPA- seronegative ~65% |
| Bone Remodeling | RANKL/RANK/OPG; M-CSF; DKK1 (Wnt inhibitor, TNF/IL-17 έΗΣ); BMP2/4/6 + Wnt/╬▓-catenin έΗΤ osteoblast + periostitis; dual pathology: erosion + new bone; mTSS/SHS structural damage |
| GutέΑΥSkinέΑΥJoint Axis | Dysbiosis (AkkermansiaέΗΥ/FirmicutesέΗΣ) έΗΤ barrier permeability έΗΤ LPS έΗΤ TLR4 έΗΤ Macrophage M1; ILC3 gut trafficking; sIgA; IBD association (~7%); CRP/fibrinogen acute phase |
| Nail Disease & Comorbidities | NAPSI score (nail matrix enthesis); Uveitis (~7%); MetSyn; CV risk έΗΣ1.3├Ω; Depression/Anxiety 37%; Obesity έΗΤ LeptinέΗΣ/AdiponectinέΗΥ; NAFLD ~47% |
| Drug PK | ADA 2-cmt SC+TMDD; IXE/GUS 1-cmt SC+TMDD; UPA/APR oral 1-cmt; FcRn recycling (IgG); ka/CL/Vd/F parameters from population PK analyses |
| Drug Mechanisms | TNFi (ADA/ETN/IFX/CZP/GOL) ┬╖ IL-17Ai (IXE/SEC/BIM) ┬╖ IL-23i (GUS/RIS/TIL) ┬╖ IL-12/23i (UST/p40) ┬╖ JAKi (UPA/TOF/BAR/FIL: JAK1/2/3/TYK2) ┬╖ PDE4i (Apremilast: cAMPέΗΣέΗΤNF-╬║BέΗΥ) ┬╖ CTLA4-Ig ┬╖ NSAIDs ┬╖ MTX ┬╖ SSZ |
| Biomarkers & Endpoints | CRP ┬╖ ESR ┬╖ IL-17A/IL-6 serum ┬╖ Calprotectin (S100A8/9) ┬╖ MMP-3 ┬╖ VEGF; ACR20/50/70 ┬╖ PASI75/90/100 ┬╖ DAPSA (remission έΚν4/LDA έΚν14) ┬╖ MDA (5/7 criteria) ┬╖ VLDA ┬╖ CASPAR ┬╖ HAQ-DI ┬╖ SF-36/PsAID ┬╖ mTSS/SHS |

## Ulcerative Colitis (UC)

> Directory: [`ulcerative-colitis/`](ulcerative-colitis/)

**Mechanistic Map** (12 clusters, 204 nodes, 222 edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Risk | HLA-DQ, IL10 locus, IL23R, NOD2, TNFSF15, JAK2 variant, HNF4A, CDH1, IBD loci; Smoking (protective in UC), NSAIDs risk, antibiotics in early life, Western diet, HPA stress axis |
| Epithelial Barrier | Colonocyte, goblet cell (MUC2/MUC5AC), tight junctions (ZO-1, Occludin, Claudin-1), HBD-2 defensin, IEC apoptosis, ER stress/UPR, EGF/IGF-1 receptors, LGR5 crypt stem cell, Paneth cell metaplasia, tuft cellέΑΥIL-25 axis, MLCK activation |
| Gut Microbiome & Dysbiosis | F. prausnitziiέΗΥ, BifidobacteriumέΗΥ, RoseburiaέΗΥ, E. coli AIECέΗΣ, C. difficile; butyrate/SCFA; LPS/MAMPs έΗΤ TLR4; secretory IgA; mucus penetration; dysbiosis index; TLR2/NOD2έΑΥMDP sensing |
| Innate Immune Activation | Resident macrophage M1/M2, recruited monocyte, neutrophil influx (CXCL8 gradient), mDC, pDCέΑΥIFN-╬▒, ILC1/2/3, NKT cell, mast cell, NLRP3 inflammasome έΗΤ Caspase-1 έΗΤ mature IL-1╬▓/IL-18; complement C3/C5a; ROS/NOX2; MPO |
| Adaptive Immunity | CD4 naive έΗΤ Th1/Th2 (UC Th2-dominant)/Th17/Treg/CD8 CTL; B cell έΗΤ plasma cell έΗΤ IgG/sIgA; mesenteric LN; Peyer's patches; ╬▒4╬▓7έΑΥMAdCAM-1 gut-homing axis; CCR9/CCL25; LPAM-1; Tfh; memory T cells |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-╬▒ ┬╖ IL-6 ┬╖ IL-1╬▓ ┬╖ IL-17A/F ┬╖ IL-22 ┬╖ IL-12/IL-23 ┬╖ IL-4 ┬╖ IL-5 ┬╖ IL-13 (Th2-skewed) ┬╖ IL-10 ┬╖ TGF-╬▓1 ┬╖ CXCL8 ┬╖ CCL2 ┬╖ IFN-╬│ ┬╖ TSLP ┬╖ IL-25/IL-33 alarmins ┬╖ OSM ┬╖ VEGF ┬╖ MMP-1/3/9 |
| JAK-STAT / NF-╬║B / S1P Signaling | JAK1/2/3/TYK2 έΗΤ STAT1/3/4/6; NF-╬║B/I╬║B╬▒/IKK╬▓; AP-1/p38 MAPK/ERK; mTOR/PI3K-Akt; S1PR1 lymphocyte egress έΗΦ S1P gradient; PDE4/cAMP/PKA; ROR╬│t έΗΤ Th17; T-bet έΗΤ Th1; GATA3 έΗΤ Th2; Foxp3 έΗΤ Treg |
| Colon Pathology | Cryptitis; crypt abscesses; goblet cell depletion; ulceration/erosion; pseudopolyps; submucosal edema; crypt distortion; muscularis propria; toxic megacolon risk; basal plasmacytosis; colorectal cancer risk (APC/Wnt/╬▓-catenin; p53; MSI) |
| Extraintestinal Manifestations | Primary sclerosing cholangitis (PSC); peripheral arthropathy; axial spondyloarthropathy; uveitis; episcleritis; erythema nodosum; pyoderma gangrenosum; thromboembolic disease; chronic anemia; steroid-induced osteopenia; oral aphthous ulcer |
| Drug PK | IFX (2-cmt IV + TMDD / TNF-╬▒); VDZ (1-cmt IV + TMDD / ╬▒4╬▓7); TOF oral (1-cmt); OZA oral (1-cmt + CC112273 active metabolite); UST IV induction + SC maintenance; Mesalamine (oral/rectal local); Prednisolone (oral) |
| Drug Mechanisms | Anti-TNF (IFX/ADA/GOL/CZP) έΗΤ TNF-╬▒ neutralization; Anti-╬▒4╬▓7 (VDZ) έΗΤ gut-selective lymphocyte trafficking blockade; Anti-IL-12/23p40 (UST) έΗΤ Th1/Th17 suppression; JAKi (TOF: JAK1/3) έΗΤ STAT3/6έΗΥ; S1P1 modulator (OZA) έΗΤ lymphocyte retention; 5-ASA (COX-2/NF-╬║BέΗΥ, local); Steroids (GR έΗΤ NF-╬║BέΗΥ); AZA/6-TGN (purine synthesis inhibition); FMT (microbiome restoration) |
| Biomarkers & Clinical Endpoints | CRP ┬╖ ESR ┬╖ Fecal calprotectin (FC) ┬╖ albumin ┬╖ hemoglobin ┬╖ Mayo total (0έΑΥ12) ┬╖ partial Mayo (0έΑΥ9) ┬╖ UCEIS endoscopic score ┬╖ Geboes histological score ┬╖ Mucosal healing ┬╖ Deep remission (clinical + endoscopic) ┬╖ Steroid-free remission ┬╖ Colectomy rate ┬╖ EIM activity |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![UC QSP Map](ulcerative-colitis/uc_qsp_model.png)](ulcerative-colitis/uc_qsp_model.svg)

### ODE Compartments (24 states)

| Group | States | Description |
|-------|--------|-------------|
| Infliximab PK | IFX_C1, IFX_C2, IFX_RC | 2-cmt IV + TMDD (TNF-╬▒ bound); CL=0.407 L/day; V1=3.28 L; Q=0.484 L/day (Fasanmade 2010) |
| Vedolizumab PK | VDZ_C1, VDZ_RC | 1-cmt IV + TMDD (╬▒4╬▓7 bound); CL=0.271 L/day; V=5.24 L (Rosario 2015) |
| Tofacitinib PK | TOF_GI, TOF_C1 | Oral 1-cmt; ka=3.47/h; CL=42.8 L/h; F=74% (Dowty 2014) |
| Ozanimod + metabolite | OZA_GI, OZA_C1, OZA_M1 | Oral + CC112273 active metabolite; CL=44 L/h; t┬╜~20h (D'Ambrosio 2021) |
| Ustekinumab PK | UST_DEPOT, UST_C1 | SC depot + central; ka=0.44/day; CL=0.192 L/day; F_SC=61.5% (Xu 2017) |
| Cytokines | TNFa, IL17, IL13, IL10 | Turn-over ODEs with Emax drug inhibition; Th2-skewed IL-13 dominant |
| Immune cells | Th2, Th17, Treg, Neutrophil | Cell population dynamics; VDZ reduces gut-homing Th2/Th17; OZA retains lymphocytes |
| Disease state | MayoScore, MucosalHealing, CRP, FC | Continuous disease activity proxies; Mayo (0έΑΥ12); MH (0=none, 1=healed); CRP ratio; FC (┬╡g/g) |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Placebo | έΑΦ | έΑΦ | ACT1/GEMINI1/OCTAVE placebo arms |
| 2 | Infliximab | 5 mg/kg IV wk0, wk2, wk6, then Q8W | TNF-╬▒ | ACT1 (2005): 69% response wk8, 45% remission wk8 |
| 3 | Vedolizumab | 300 mg IV wk0, wk2, wk6, then Q8W | ╬▒4╬▓7 integrin (gut-selective) | GEMINI 1 (2013): 47% remission wk52 vs 17% placebo |
| 4 | Tofacitinib | 10 mg BID ├Ω 8 wk (induction) έΗΤ 5 mg BID | JAK1 / JAK3 | OCTAVE Induct 1 (2017): 59% response wk8 |
| 5 | Ustekinumab | IV ~520 mg single induction, then 90 mg SC Q8W | IL-12/IL-23 p40 | UNIFI (2019): 53% response wk8; 44% remission wk52 |
| 6 | Ozanimod | 0.92 mg QD oral | S1PR1 (lymphocyte retention) | TRUE NORTH (2021): 37% remission wk52 vs 19% placebo |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ numeric inputs (baseline Mayo 0έΑΥ12, CRP mg/L, FC ┬╡g/g, disease duration, prior biologic failure); comorbidity checklist (PSC, arthropathy, osteopenia); action button "Run Simulation"; value boxes (Mayo ┬╖ CRP ┬╖ FC at week 52)
2. **Drug PK** έΑΦ drug selector (IFX/VDZ/TOF/OZA/UST); log-Y concentrationέΑΥtime plot; trough concentration line; DT table of PK parameters (route/dose/Cmax/trough/t┬╜/target/trial)
3. **Cytokine & Immune Dynamics** έΑΦ 4-panel: TNF-╬▒ ┬╖ IL-13 (Th2) ┬╖ IL-17 ┬╖ IL-10 over 52 weeks; lower panel: Th2/Th17/Treg/Neutrophil cell count dynamics
4. **Disease Activity** έΑΦ Mayo score time-course with remission threshold (έΚν2); partial Mayo panel; CRP and FC panels; response table (wk 8/16/52: % clinical remission, % mucosal healing)
5. **Mucosal Healing** έΑΦ mucosal healing index (0έΑΥ1) time-course with 0.7 threshold; endoscopic subscore proxy; histological activity proxy (Geboes); deep remission rate vs week
6. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ multi-scenario toggle; endpoint selector (Mayo/MH/CRP/FC/TNF/IL13); comparative 52-week plot; response summary table at wk8 and wk52 (% clinical remission, % mucosal healing, % deep remission, % steroid-free remission)
7. **Biomarkers & Safety** έΑΦ CRP/FC time-courses for each drug; anemia risk (hemoglobin proxy); infection risk (neutrophil change vs baseline); thromboembolic risk flag for tofacitinib (JAKi class effect); lipid change note; PSC progression note

## Polycystic Ovary Syndrome (PCOS)

> Directory: [`polycystic-ovary-syndrome/`](polycystic-ovary-syndrome/)

**Mechanistic Map** (9 clusters + 6 drug subgraphs, 175+ nodes, 200+ edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| HPO Axis | KNDy neurons (Kisspeptin/NKB/Dynorphin) έΗΤ GnRH pulse frequency έΗΣέΗΣ; GnRHR έΗΤ LH έΗΣέΗΣ / FSH (normal-low); LH:FSH ratio >2έΑΥ3; Inhibin B / Inhibin A / Activin A feedback; E2 negative feedback (impaired); P4 negative feedback (absent, anovulatory); Prolactin; GH |
| Ovarian Steroidogenesis | Theca cells (έΗΣLH έΗΤ cAMP/PKA έΗΤ StAR/CYP11A1/CYP17A1 έΗΣέΗΣ έΗΤ ╬Φ4/╬Φ5 androgens); Granulosa cells (FSH έΗΤ cAMP/PKA έΗΤ CYP19A1 έΗΥ per follicle); DHEA/Androstenedione/Testosterone (ovarian έΗΣέΗΣ); Estradiol E2 (tonic moderate έΗΣ); Estrone E1; Progesterone P4 (έΗΥέΗΥ anovulatory); AMH έΗΣέΗΣ (3έΑΥ8├Ω normal); HSD17B1/3; INSL3 theca marker |
| Folliculogenesis | Primordial έΗΤ Primary έΗΤ Secondary έΗΤ Small antral (2έΑΥ5 mm, excess έΗΣέΗΣ) έΗΤ arrested large antral (6έΑΥ9 mm) έΗΤ dominant follicle selection failure; AMH-mediated arrest έΗΤ FSHR desensitization + CYP19A1 inhibition; AFC >12 per ovary; Ovarian volume >10 mL έΗΤ PCOM criterion; Follicle atresia έΗΣ; Anovulation έΗΤ absent corpus luteum έΗΤ P4 deficiency; Endometrial hyperplasia risk |
| Insulin Signaling | ╬▓-cell compensatory hyperinsulinemia; IR: IRS1 serine phos (JNK/PKC) έΗΣ, IRS1 tyrosine phos έΗΥ; PI3K-AKT έΗΥ (metabolic); GLUT4 translocation έΗΥ; FOXO1 active έΗΤ HGP έΗΣ; MAPK-ERK preserved έΗΤ CYP17A1 έΗΣέΗΣ (key IR-androgen link); mTOR-S6K feedback; IGF1R potentiates LHR; IGFBP1 έΗΥ (insulin-suppressed); SHBG έΗΥ (hepatic); HOMA-IR έΗΣ (έΚξ2.5); T2DM risk 6έΑΥ10├Ω |
| Adrenal Androgen | HPA axis/ACTH έΗΤ Adrenal zona reticularis CYP17A1 έΗΣ (50% of PCOS) έΗΤ DHEA/DHEAS έΗΣ + adrenal androstenedione; Insulin upregulates adrenal CYP17A1; Cortisol (normal/mild έΗΣ) |
| Peripheral Androgen | Total T έΗΣ / Free T έΗΣέΗΣ (SHBG έΗΥ); SRD5A1 (skin) + SRD5A2 (scalp) έΗΤ DHT έΗΣ; AR in sebaceous glands έΗΤ sebum έΗΣ έΗΤ acne; AR in terminal hair follicle έΗΤ hirsutism (FG έΚξ8); Scalp miniaturization έΗΤ androgenic alopecia; Hepatic CYP1A2 / UGT έΗΤ 3╬▒-androstanediol glucuronide (5╬▒-RA activity marker); Clinical hyperandrogenism (PCOS criterion 2) |
| Inflammation / Adipokines | Visceral adiposity έΗΤ M1 macrophage έΗΤ TNF-╬▒/IL-6/IL-1╬▓ έΗΤ NF-╬║B; TNF-╬▒ έΗΤ IRS1-Ser (inflammation-IR loop); ROS/MDA/NOέΗΥ έΗΤ endothelial dysfunction; Leptin έΗΣ / Adiponectin έΗΥ / Resistin/Visfatin/Chemerin έΗΣ; IL-6 έΗΤ CRP έΗΣ (>3 mg/L); IL-18 έΗΤ CVD predictor; AMPKέΗΥ in adipose |
| Drug PK/PD | Metformin (2-cmt oral, F=50%, OCT1 liver έΗΤ AMPK έΗΤ PEPCK/G6PaseέΗΥ / CYP17A1έΗΥ / GLP-1έΗΣ); Letrozole (1-cmt oral, F=99%, t┬╜=48h έΗΤ CYP19A1 Ki=11nM έΗΤ E2έΗΥ97% έΗΤ FSH έΗΣ έΗΤ dominant follicle); Clomiphene (central ER block έΗΤ GnRH έΗΣ έΗΤ LH+FSH έΗΣ, adverse: cervical mucusέΗΥ / endometriumέΗΥ); Spironolactone (AR competitive block + SRD5A έΗΥ έΗΤ FGέΗΥ30έΑΥ40%); Combined OCP (EE έΗΤ SHBG έΗΣ2έΑΥ4├Ω + LH/FSH έΗΥ έΗΤ T έΗΥ); GnRH agonist/antagonist (IVF protocol, pituitary downregulation) |
| Clinical Endpoints | Oligo/amenorrhea (cycle >35 days) ┬╖ Anovulation ┬╖ Infertility (40έΑΥ80%) ┬╖ Pregnancy/Live birth rate ┬╖ Metabolic syndrome (2έΑΥ3├Ω risk) ┬╖ CVD risk (4├Ω) ┬╖ T2DM risk ┬╖ NASH risk ┬╖ Gestational DM (3├Ω) ┬╖ Preeclampsia (2├Ω) ┬╖ Sleep apnea ┬╖ Depression/anxiety (30έΑΥ40%) ┬╖ Endometrial hyperplasia ┬╖ Rotterdam criteria (2/3: OA + HA + PCOM) |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![PCOS QSP Map](polycystic-ovary-syndrome/pcos_qsp_model.png)](polycystic-ovary-syndrome/pcos_qsp_model.svg)

### ODE Compartments (24 states)

| Group | States | Description |
|-------|--------|-------------|
| HPO Axis | GnRH_drive, LH, FSH | GnRH drive state (elevated baseline in PCOS); LH t┬╜έΚΙ20 min (k_deg=0.85/day); FSH t┬╜έΚΙ4 h (k_deg=0.38/day); Inhibin B proxy via AMH├Ω0.55+1 suppresses FSH |
| Steroidogenesis | T_total, E2, P4, AMH | Testosterone: LH ├Ω CYP17A1 activity (up-regulated by insulin, down by metformin) ├Ω (1έΙΤSPR inhibition); E2: FSH + aromatization of T, suppressed by letrozole (EC50_AI=0.012 mg/L); P4: corpus luteum (DF_state┬▓); AMH: auto-regulated quadratic decay |
| Follicle Dynamics | AFC_state, DF_state | AFC approaches steady-state 19 (PCOS) via first-order regulation; Dominant follicle driven by FSH above threshold (4.8 mIU/mL), inhibited by AMH (k=0.28) |
| Insulin/Metabolic | Insulin, Glucose, IGFBP1 | Glucose-stimulated insulin secretion; Peripheral glucose utilization reduced by k_IR├Ω(1έΙΤmetformin effect); Hepatic glucose production reduced by metformin 85%; IGFBP1 suppressed by insulin |
| SHBG & Free T | SHBG, FreeT | Hepatic SHBG synthesis: suppressed by insulin, induced by EE (2έΑΥ4├Ω); FreeT approximated as T ├Ω (22/SHBG) ├Ω 0.19 ├Ω (1έΙΤspiro blockade) |
| Inflammation | CRP, BMI, HirsScore | CRP driven by T and excess BMI; BMI slow drift + metformin reduction; Hirsutism: free T drives FG score increase (blocked by spironolactone AR occupancy) |
| Drug PK | MET_gut, MET_central, MET_periph, LET_plasma, EE_plasma, SPR_plasma, CC_plasma | Metformin 2-compartment (V1=80L, V2=155L, CL=45 L/h, Q=12 L/h, F=50%); Letrozole 1-cmt (V=145L, CL=2.1 L/h, t┬╜=48h); EE 1-cmt (V=250L, CL=38 L/h); Spiro 1-cmt (V=65L, CL=40 L/h); CC 1-cmt (V=105L, CL=1 L/h, t┬╜έΚΙ5έΑΥ7 days) |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Key Trial / Effect |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Untreated PCOS | έΑΦ | έΑΦ | Rotterdam ESHRE 2004 baseline; LH=12.5, AMH=10, HOMA-IR=5.2 |
| 2 | Metformin | 500 mg TID (1500 mg/day) | AMPK / CYP17A1 / IR | PPCOS I (Legro 2007): έΗΥandrogens ~26%, έΗΥHOMA-IR ~35%; Graham 2011 PK |
| 3 | Letrozole | 2.5 mg/day day 3έΑΥ7, q28 days | CYP19A1 (aromatase) | PPCOS II (Legro 2014 NEJM): ovulation 61.7% vs CC 48.3%; live birth 27.5% |
| 4 | Combined OCP | EE 30 ╬╝g/day ├Ω 21 days (21/7 cycle) | HPO axis / SHBG | SHBG έΗΣ2έΑΥ4├Ω (Zimmermann 2014); Free T έΗΥ>70% (Odlind 2002) |
| 5 | Metformin + Letrozole | MET 500 mg TID + LET 2.5 mg d3έΑΥ7 | AMPK + Aromatase | Additive: έΗΥIR + έΗΣovulation; meta-analysis (Palomba 2005); first-line infertility |
| 6 | Spironolactone | 100 mg/day | AR competitive block | FG score έΗΥ30έΑΥ40% at 6 months (van Zuuren 2015 Cochrane); AR Ki=150 nM |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ slider inputs (BMI, insulin resistance k_IR, AMH multiplier, AFC); PCOS phenotype classification table (Rotterdam A/B/C/D); baseline biomarker table (LH/FSH/T/E2/SHBG/FAI/AMH/HOMA-IR/CRP/BMI/FG score vs normal ranges)
2. **Hormone Kinetics** έΑΦ LH & FSH dynamics (color-coded, dashed threshold); Testosterone & Estradiol (dual-axis); Progesterone (P4, corpus luteum); AMH level; SHBG & Free Testosterone
3. **Metabolic Endpoints** έΑΦ HOMA-IR (IR threshold 2.5); Fasting glucose & insulin (dual); BMI trajectory; IGFBP-1; hsCRP (inflammation)
4. **Clinical Endpoints** έΑΦ Dominant follicle / ovulation probability (0έΑΥ1); Antral follicle count (AFC, threshold 12); Hirsutism FG score (threshold 8); Free Androgen Index (FAI, threshold 4.5%)
5. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ 6-arm comparison table (DT, conditional color formatting); all-scenario plots for T / HOMA-IR / ovulation probability / FG score
6. **Biomarker Dashboard** έΑΦ 8 value boxes (LH, T, HOMA-IR, AMH, FAI, SHBG, CRP, FG score έΑΦ green/red status); LH:FSH ratio time-course; risk radar (normalized 6-axis: LH:FSH / T / HOMA-IR / FAI / hsCRP / FG); drug plasma concentration panel

## Dyslipidemia

> Directory: [`dyslipidemia/`](dyslipidemia/)

**Mechanistic Map** (13 subgraph clusters, 211 nodes, 274 edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Hepatic Cholesterol Synthesis | Acetyl-CoA έΗΤ HMG-CoA (HMGCR, rate-limiting) έΗΤ Mevalonate έΗΤ IPP/GPP/FPP έΗΤ Squalene έΗΤ Lanosterol έΗΤ Desmosterol έΗΤ Cholesterol; Side branches: CoQ10, Dolichol, Geranylgeranyl-PP (protein prenylation); ACAT/SOAT1/2 έΗΤ Cholesteryl ester storage |
| LDLR / PCSK9 Regulation | LDLR gene έΗΤ mRNA έΗΤ protein έΗΤ surface receptor έΗΤ LDL endocytosis έΗΤ lysosomal degradation έΗΤ LDLR recycling; PCSK9 gene/mRNA έΗΤ proprotein έΗΤ secretion έΗΤ plasma PCSK9 + LDLR complex έΗΤ lysosomal co-degradation; SREBP-2/SCAP/Insig-1 sterol-sensing loop (ER membrane έΗΤ Golgi έΗΤ nuclear SRE activation έΗΤ LDLR + PCSK9 co-upregulation by statins) |
| Lipoprotein Metabolism | Hepatic ApoB100 synthesis/MTP έΗΤ VLDL1/VLDL2 secretion; LPL (ApoC-II stimulated, ApoC-III inhibited) έΗΤ VLDLέΗΤIDL; HL έΗΤ IDLέΗΤLDL; sdLDL formation; oxLDL (ROS); Lp(a) = LDL + Apo(a)/LPA gene; CETP (CE transfer: HDLέΗΤVLDL/LDL); Chylomicron remnant uptake |
| Reverse Cholesterol Transport (RCT) | Macrophage cholesterol efflux έΗΤ ABCA1έΗΤPre-╬▓ HDL; ABCG1έΗΤHDL3; LCAT (ApoA-I cofactor) έΗΤ HDL3έΗΤHDL2; SR-BI hepatic selective CE uptake; FXR/LXR/PPAR╬▒ transcriptional regulation; ApoA-I synthesis; ApoA-II |
| Intestinal Cholesterol Absorption | Dietary cholesterol + biliary cholesterol έΗΤ Micellar solubilization έΗΤ Enterocyte NPC1L1 uptake; Ezetimibe blocks NPC1L1; ACAT2 έΗΤ CE; ApoB48/MTP έΗΤ Chylomicron assembly; ABCG5/G8 έΗΤ sterol efflux back to lumen |
| Bile Acid Metabolism | CYP7A1 (rate-limiting, FXR-SHP negative feedback); CYP8B1 (CA:CDCA ratio); CYP27A1; FGF19/FGFR4 (intestinal FXRέΗΤhepatic CYP7A1έΗΥ); TGR5/GLP-1 axis; BSEP export; Enterohepatic circulation; Bile acid sequestrants bind lumenal BA έΗΤ CYP7A1 upregulation έΗΤ LDLRέΗΣ |
| Drug Mechanisms | Statin έΗΤ HMGCR inhibition έΗΤ MevalonateέΗΥ έΗΤ SREBP-2 activation έΗΤ LDLRέΗΣ2.5├Ω + PCSK9 paradoxέΗΣ; Ezetimibe έΗΤ NPC1L1 block; Evolocumab/Alirocumab έΗΤ PCSK9 neutralization έΗΤ LDLR rescue; Inclisiran έΗΤ PCSK9 mRNA silencing (siRNA/RISC); Bempedoic acid έΗΤ ATP-citrate lyase (ACL) inhibition έΗΤ Acetyl-CoAέΗΥ έΗΤ HMG-CoAέΗΥ; Fibrate/PPAR╬▒ έΗΤ LPLέΗΣ/ApoC-IIIέΗΥ/TGέΗΥ/HDLέΗΣ; Niacin/GPR109A έΗΤ HSL inhibition έΗΤ FFAέΗΥ έΗΤ hepatic TGέΗΥ έΗΤ VLDLέΗΥ; Omega-3 FA έΗΤ SREBP-1cέΗΥ/DGAT2έΗΥ έΗΤ TGέΗΥ; BAS έΗΤ BA sequestration έΗΤ CYP7A1έΗΣ έΗΤ cholesterol diversion |
| Statin PK | Oral dose έΗΤ GI absorption; Hepatic first-pass (OATP1B1/1B3 uptake transporter); CYP3A4 (atorvastatin/lovastatin/simvastatin) / CYP2C9 (rosuvastatin/fluvastatin) metabolism; Biliary excretion; Active acid form vs lactone form; Myopathy risk (plasma CK, CYP3A4 DDI, hypothyroidism, age >75) |
| Atherosclerosis | Endothelial dysfunction (oxLDL έΗΤ eNOSέΗΥ/ROSέΗΣ/ICAM-1/VCAM-1); Monocyte recruitment (MCP-1/CCR2); MonocyteέΗΤMacrophage differentiation; Foam cell formation (SR-A/CD36 oxLDL uptake); NLRP3/IL-1╬▓/IL-18 έΗΤ hsCRP; Vulnerable plaque (thin cap, lipid core, macrophage-rich); Stable plaque (thick cap, smooth muscle cells, collagen); Plaque regression (statin/PCSK9i έΗΤ cholesterol crystal dissolution) |
| Adipose Tissue | Catecholamine/cAMP/PKA έΗΤ HSL + ATGL έΗΤ TG lipolysis έΗΤ FFA + glycerol; Insulin έΗΤ HSL inhibition έΗΤ FFA suppression; Niacin/GPR109A έΗΤ anti-lipolytic; FFA flux to liver έΗΤ hepatic TG synthesis; Adipokines (adiponectin, leptin) |
| Hepatic TG Synthesis | Citrate έΗΤ Acetyl-CoA (ACL); GPAT έΗΤ LPA έΗΤ PA έΗΤ DAG (Lipin-1); DGAT1/2 έΗΤ TG; VLDL1 (TG-rich, insulin resistance) vs VLDL2 (CE-rich, normal); SREBP-1c/ChREBP/Insulin έΗΤ lipogenic gene upregulation; Glucagon έΗΤ opposing effects |
| Biomarkers | LDL-C ┬╖ HDL-C ┬╖ TG ┬╖ ApoB ┬╖ ApoA-I ┬╖ Non-HDL-C ┬╖ Lp(a) ┬╖ hsCRP ┬╖ PCSK9 plasma ┬╖ FFA ┬╖ VLDL-C ┬╖ sdLDL ┬╖ LDL particle number ┬╖ LDL particle size |
| Clinical Endpoints | MACE (MI ┬╖ stroke ┬╖ CVD death ┬╖ unstable angina ┬╖ revascularization); Plaque regression (REVERSAL/ASTEROID/GLAGOV IVUS trials); CIMT progression; Coronary Artery Calcium (CAC) score; ASCVD 10-year risk (PCE); LDL-C goal attainment; NNT for 5-year MACE prevention |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

[![Dyslipidemia QSP Map](dyslipidemia/dyslip_qsp_model.png)](dyslipidemia/dyslip_qsp_model.svg)

### ODE Compartments (26 states)

| Group | States | Description |
|-------|--------|-------------|
| Atorvastatin PK | AT_gut, AT_central, AT_peripheral | 2-cmt with GI absorption (ka=1.2/h); hepatic first-pass via OATP1B1; CL=78 L/h; V1=381 L; t┬╜=14h; F=12% (Lau 2006); HMGCR inhibition Imax model |
| Evolocumab PK | EVO_depot, EVO_central, EVO_peripheral | SC depot + 2-cmt; ka_SC=0.29/day; CL=0.27 L/day; V1=3.0 L; t┬╜=11.5 days (Gibbs 2017 Clin PK); PCSK9 target-mediated binding |
| Ezetimibe PK | EZE_intestinal, EZE_central | Intestinal compartment (NPC1L1 local exposure) + plasma; ka=2.1/h; CL=15 L/h; NPC1L1 inhibition IC50=1.2 nM (Altmann 2004) |
| Inclisiran PK | INC_depot | Single SC depot with mRNA silencing kinetics; dose on days 0, 90, 270, 450; effect t┬╜έΚΙ10 days from ORION-1 |
| Cholesterol Synthesis | HMGCoA_R, Mevalonate, Hep_Chol | HMG-CoA reductase activity (Emax inhibition by statin); mevalonate pool; hepatic free cholesterol (ACAT equilibrium with CE) |
| Lipoprotein Dynamics | VLDL, IDL, LDL_c, LDL_p, HDL | VLDL production rate (basal 0.32 mmol/L/day); IDL transit (t┬╜=2h); LDL central + peripheral; HDL turnover (t┬╜=5.5 days) |
| LDL Receptor | LDLR_surface, LDLR_internal | LDLR surface density (baseline ~50,000/cell); PCSK9-mediated lysosomal degradation; statin έΗΤ LDLR upregulation (2.5├Ω via SREBP-2); LDL clearance proportional to LDLR ├Ω LDL |
| PCSK9 | PCSK9_liver, PCSK9_plasma, PCSK9_complex | Hepatic PCSK9 synthesis (SREBP-2 co-upregulated by statin +180%); plasma PCSK9 t┬╜=5 days; evolocumab complex (Kd=0.1 nM; tmax-binding 11 days); inclisiran silences PCSK9_liver mRNA |
| Intestinal Absorption | Chol_intestinal | NPC1L1-mediated uptake (baseline ~50% efficiency); ezetimibe reduces by 54% (Altmann 2004) |
| Bile Acid Pool | BA_pool | Enterohepatic circulation with CYP7A1 rate; BAS reduces BA recirculation έΗΤ CYP7A1έΗΣ έΗΤ hepatic cholesterol diversion έΗΤ LDLRέΗΣ |
| Atherosclerosis | Foam_cells, Plaque_burden | Foam cell accumulation driven by oxLDL ├Ω macrophage recruitment; plaque regression when LDL-C < 70 mg/dL sustained; calibrated to REVERSAL/ASTEROID IVUS data |

### Treatment Scenarios (6)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | No treatment | έΑΦ | έΑΦ | Framingham/UKPDS natural history; LDL-C 160 mg/dL baseline |
| 2 | Atorvastatin 40 mg QD | 40 mg oral once daily | HMG-CoA reductase | ASCOT-LLA (Sever 2003): έΙΤ46% LDL-C; TNT (LaRosa 2005): intensive statin reduces MACE 22% |
| 3 | Atorvastatin 40 mg + Ezetimibe 10 mg | Dual oral daily | HMGCR + NPC1L1 | IMPROVE-IT (Cannon 2015, PMID 25405393): additional έΙΤ15 mg/dL LDL-C; CV benefit additive |
| 4 | Atorvastatin 40 mg + Evolocumab 140 mg Q2W | Statin + SC biologic Q2W | HMGCR + PCSK9 | FOURIER (Sabatine 2017, PMID 28304224): έΙΤ59% LDL-C from statin baseline; 15% MACE RRR |
| 5 | Triple: Statin + Ezetimibe + Evolocumab | Three-drug combination | HMGCR + NPC1L1 + PCSK9 | Combination guideline-recommended; LDL-C reduction >80%; FH management |
| 6 | Atorvastatin 40 mg + Inclisiran 284 mg SC | Statin + siRNA (day 0/90 then Q6M) | HMGCR + PCSK9 mRNA | ORION-1 (Ray 2017): έΙΤ51% PCSK9; ORION-3 LTE (2022): sustained έΙΤ45% LDL-C |

### Shiny Dashboard (6 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ Sliders: age, sex, BMI, baseline LDL-C/HDL-C/TG, diabetes, smoking, blood pressure; Pooled Cohort Equations 10-year ASCVD risk calculator; ACC/AHA and ESC risk category display; LDL-C target based on risk (very high <55 mg/dL, high <70, intermediate <100); Lipid classification table; Risk factor radar chart
2. **Drug PK** έΑΦ 14-drug selector (atorvastatin 10/20/40/80 mg, rosuvastatin 10/20/40 mg, evolocumab 140/420 mg, alirocumab 75/150 mg, inclisiran 284 mg, ezetimibe, bempedoic acid); Multi-dose accumulation PK curves over 26 weeks; Hepatic active metabolite panel; Half-life comparison bar chart; OATP1B1/CYP3A4 transporter note
3. **PD έΑΥ Lipid Biomarkers** έΑΦ LDL-C, HDL-C, TG, ApoB, non-HDL-C time-courses (52 weeks); PCSK9 plasma dynamics (statin reactive upregulation έΗΣ180% vs PCSK9i suppression έΗΥ85%); LDL receptor density trend; % change from baseline toggle; ACC/AHA/ESC target lines; Lp(a) note
4. **Clinical Endpoints** έΑΦ CTT RRR model (22% relative risk reduction per 1 mmol/L LDL-C decrease); Cumulative 5-year MACE curves under each treatment; Atherosclerotic plaque regression/progression simulation (IVUS calibrated); NNT vs adherence chart; ARR and NNT summary table
5. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ 6-arm simultaneous comparison; Grouped bar chart (LDL-C at wk 12/26/52); DataTable with conditional formatting (green = at goal, red = not at goal); Multi-dimension radar: LDL-C reduction / HDL-C change / TG change / MACE risk reduction / cost-effectiveness score
6. **Biomarker Dashboard** έΑΦ PCSK9 genetic variant slider (GOF έΗΤ higher LDL; LOF έΗΤ lower baseline); Statin myopathy risk gauge (0έΑΥ14 pt score: age, CK, hypothyroid, DDI, renal function, statin dose); CYP3A4 DDI checker (13 interacting drugs: amiodarone, diltiazem, amlodipine, cyclosporine, erythromycin, fluconazole, itraconazole, clarithromycin, HIV PIs, grapefruit); Guideline LDL-C target reference lines; Real-time NNT calculation

## Behcet's Disease (BD)

> Directory: [`behcet-disease/`](behcet-disease/)

**Mechanistic Map** (10 subgraph clusters, 130+ nodes, 200+ edges):

| Cluster | Coverage |
|---------|----------|
| Genetic & Environmental Factors | HLA-B51 (primary risk allele, OR 5-6├Ω), ERAP1 (antigen trimming), IL-10 gene polymorphism (έΙΤ1082G/A έΗΤ IL-10έΗΥ), TNFSF4/OX40L, STAT4/IRF8 variants, CCR1/CCR3 haplotypes; Gut/oral microbiome dysbiosis; Streptococcus sanguinis molecular mimicry via HSP60/HSP70 cross-reactive epitopes; Silk Road geography |
| Innate Immunity | Neutrophil hyperactivation (HLA-B51 dependent priming); NETs (NETosis έΗΤ coagulation cascade activation + endothelial damage); ROS/MPO/elastase; Monocyte M1 polarization (TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓/IL-6/IL-12/IL-23); mDC (IL-12/IL-23 έΗΤ Th1/Th17 priming); NK cells (IFN-╬│ early); Mast cell degranulation; NLRP3 inflammasome (ASC complex έΗΤ Caspase-1 έΗΤ IL-1╬▓/IL-18 cleavage); NOD1/2 signaling; ER stress/UPR; cGAS-STING pathway; PAMPs/DAMPs; GM-CSF myeloid survival |
| Adaptive Immunity | Th1 (IFN-╬│, TNF-╬▒ dominant in BD); Th17 (IL-17A, IL-17F, IL-22, IL-21); Th22; CD8+ CTL (anti-HSP cross-reactive cytotoxicity at mucosal sites); Treg dysfunction (FoxP3+ suppression insufficient); Tfh έΗΤ IL-21 έΗΤ B cell germinal center; ╬│╬┤ T cells (IL-17A innate-like); NKT (CD1d restricted); ILC3 (IL-22/IL-17); B cell έΗΤ memory έΗΤ plasma έΗΤ AECA IgG (anti-endothelial cell antibodies) + IgA (mucosal) |
| Cytokine Network | TNF-╬▒ (central mediator έΑΦ monocyte/macrophage/Th1/neutrophil source); IL-1╬▓ (NLRP3 product έΑΦ drives oral ulcers + fever); IL-6 (pleiotropic; APR induction; Th17 polarization); IL-8/CXCL8 (neutrophil chemoattractant); IL-17A/F (Th17 + ╬│╬┤T + ILC3; epithelial/endothelial damage); IL-23 (Th17 maintenance έΑΦ IL-12p40 shared with IL-12); IFN-╬│ (Th1/CD8T/NK; M1 macrophage polarization); IL-10έΗΥ (anti-inflammatory deficit); TGF-╬▓/Treg; VEGF (angiogenesis/permeability); MCP-1/CCL5/CXCL10 (leukocyte chemokines); IL-18 (NK/Th1 amplifier); IL-33 (alarmin, ST2 έΗΤ mast cell); GM-CSF |
| Intracellular Signaling | NF-╬║B (p65/p50 έΑΦ TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓/IL-17A έΗΤ ICAM-1/VCAM-1/E-selectin transcription); JAK/STAT cascade (IL-6έΗΤSTAT3έΗΤROR╬│tέΗΤTh17; IL-12έΗΤSTAT4έΗΤT-betέΗΤTh1; IFN-╬│έΗΤSTAT1); MAPK/ERK + p38 MAPK (TNF-╬▒ mRNA stabilization); PI3K/AKT έΗΤ mTORC1 (Th17 expansion); Notch signaling (T cell fate); PDE4 έΗΤ cAMP (apremilast target: cAMPέΗΣ έΗΤ NF-╬║BέΗΥ έΗΤ TNF-╬▒έΗΥ/IL-17AέΗΥ/IL-10έΗΣ); ROR╬│t (Th17 master TF); T-bet (Th1 master TF) |
| Vascular Pathology & Thrombosis | Endothelial cell activation (TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓/IL-17A/IFN-╬│ έΗΤ TNFR1/R2/IL-1R/IL-17R signaling); ICAM-1/VCAM-1/E-selectin upregulation έΗΤ leukocyte adhesion; vWF exocytosis (Weibel-Palade bodies) έΗΤ platelet GPIb╬▒ binding; Tissue factor expression έΗΤ extrinsic coagulation pathway έΗΤ thrombin έΗΤ fibrin; eNOS uncoupling έΗΤ NOέΗΥ έΗΤ coagulationέΗΣ; PGI2έΗΥ έΗΤ anti-thrombotic protection lost; PAI-1έΗΣ έΗΤ fibrinolysis inhibition; Platelet activation (PAR-1/4, GP IIb/IIIa); Venous thrombosis (Budd-Chiari / cerebral vein); Arterial thrombosis; Pulmonary/systemic aneurysm (vasculitis έΗΤ wall destruction); AECA IgG έΗΤ EC activation amplification |
| Organ Manifestations | Oral aphthous ulcers (>95%; IL-17A/TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓ + CD8 CTL έΗΤ mucosal ulcerogenesis; IL-22 repair attempt); Genital ulcers (Th1/CD8/IL-17A); Anterior + posterior uveitis + retinal vasculitis έΗΤ optic atrophy/vision loss (25% blindness untreated); Pseudofolliculitis + erythema nodosum (skin Th17/TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓); Pathergy reaction (neutrophil hyperinflux to needlestick); GI ulcers (ileocecal, punched-out); Neuro-Behcet (parenchymal BD or cerebral vein thrombosis); Non-destructive polyarthritis; Epididymo-orchitis; Budd-Chiari syndrome; Pulmonary infarction |
| Drug Pharmacokinetics | Colchicine: gut depot έΗΤ central (F=44%, CL=17 L/h, Vd=588 L=21 L/kg, t┬╜=27h); Prednisolone: 2-CMT oral (F=80%, CL=8.4 L/h, V1=22 L); Adalimumab: 2-CMT SC (F=64%, CL=0.012 L/h, V1=2.8 L, t┬╜~2 wk, Q2W dosing); Apremilast: 1-CMT oral (F=73%, CL=10 L/h, V1=87 L, t┬╜=9h, BID dosing); Canakinumab: 2-CMT SC (F=66%, CL=0.007 L/h, V1=3.0 L, t┬╜~26 d, Q8W dosing); Cyclophosphamide: IV active alkylating form; Thalidomide: oral (F=67%, t┬╜=5-7h) |
| Drug PD Mechanisms | Colchicine: tubulin polymerizationέΗΥ έΗΤ neutrophil migrationέΗΥ + NLRP3 assembly inhibition έΗΤ IL-1╬▓έΗΥ; Prednisolone: GR┬╖NF-╬║B/AP-1 co-repression έΗΤ broad cytokine mRNAέΗΥ; Azathioprine: 6-TG έΗΤ DNA damage έΗΤ T/B cell proliferationέΗΥ; Adalimumab: mTNF/sTNF neutralization + Treg inductionέΗΣ; Apremilast: PDE4 inhibition έΗΤ cAMPέΗΣ έΗΤ PKA έΗΤ NF-╬║B phosphorylationέΗΥ έΗΤ TNF-╬▒έΗΥ/IL-17AέΗΥ/IL-10έΗΣ; Canakinumab: high-affinity IL-1╬▓ neutralization (Kd~0.3 pM) έΗΤ NLRP3 pathway blockade; Cyclophosphamide: DNA alkylation έΗΤ B/T/plasma cell depletion; Thalidomide: TNF-╬▒ mRNA destabilization + IMiD immunomodulation έΗΤ Th1έΗΥ |
| Clinical Endpoints & Biomarkers | BDCAF score (0-12: oral ulcers/genital/ocular/skin/arthritis/neuro/vascular, remission <3); Oral ulcer frequency (per month); Visual acuity (LogMAR/Snellen); Ocular inflammation score; Serum TNF-╬▒, IL-1╬▓, IL-6, IL-17A (normalized disease activity); ESR/CRP (APR driven by IL-6); SAA; Neutrophil:lymphocyte ratio; Quality of life (SF-36/BDQ); Relapse rate (flares/year); Time to remission; Vascular event rate (thrombosis/aneurysm/Budd-Chiari) |

**Mechanistic Map Preview:**

### ODE Compartments (22 states)

| Group | States | Description |
|-------|--------|-------------|
| Colchicine PK | AGUT_COL, ACOL, ACOL_T | Gut depot έΗΤ 2-CMT; ka=1.2/h; F=44%; CL=17 L/h; V1=28 L; V2=5500 L (Vd=21 L/kg); Q=30 L/h; t┬╜έΚΙ27h; NLRP3 inhibition IC50=1.5 ng/mL; Neutrophil inhibition IC50=0.8 ng/mL |
| Prednisolone PK | APRED, APRED_T | 2-CMT oral; ka=1.0/h; F=80%; CL=8.4 L/h; V1=22 L; V2=50 L; t┬╜έΚΙ3.5h; NF-╬║B inhibition EC50=50 ng/mL; Emax=0.80 |
| Adalimumab PK | AADA, AADA_P | SC 2-CMT; F=64%; CL=0.012 L/h; V1=2.8 L; V2=3.4 L; Q=0.003 L/h; t┬╜~14 days; TNF-╬▒ neutralization EC50=1500 ng/mL; Emax=0.90 |
| Apremilast PK | AAPR | 1-CMT oral; ka=0.58/h; F=73%; CL=10 L/h; V1=87 L; t┬╜έΚΙ9h; PDE4έΗΤcAMPέΗΤTNF-╬▒έΗΥ EC50=200 ng/mL; IL-17AέΗΥ EC50=300 ng/mL |
| Canakinumab PK | ACAN, ACAN_P | SC 2-CMT; F=66%; CL=0.007 L/h; V1=3.0 L; V2=3.2 L; t┬╜έΚΙ26 days; IL-1╬▓ neutralization EC50=800 ng/mL; Emax=0.92 |
| Immune Cells | NEU, TH1, TH17, TREG | Neutrophil activation (TNFA/IL17A driven; colchicine suppressed); Th1 cells (TNF-╬▒ amplification; pred suppressed); Th17 cells (IL-6/TREG ratio dependent; apremilast/pred suppressed); Treg (TGFB driven, TNFA opposed) |
| Cytokines | TNFA, IL1B, IL6C, IL17A | TNF-╬▒ (Th1+NEU driven; adalimumab/pred/apremilast target); IL-1╬▓ (NLRP3/NEU driven; colchicine/canakinumab target); IL-6 (IL-1B/TNFA synergy; pred target); IL-17A (Th17+gdT driven; apremilast target) |
| Organ Activity | EA, OUL, OCI, BDCAF | Endothelial activation (TNFA/IL1B/IL17A driven; resolved by anti-TNF); Oral ulcer index (cytokine + NEU driven; 4-drug sensitivity); Ocular inflammation (EA driven; anti-TNF/steroid target); BDCAF composite score (OUL+OCI+EA+cytokines weighted) |

### Treatment Scenarios (8)

| # | Scenario | Dose Regimen | Primary Target | Clinical Reference |
|---|----------|-------------|----------------|-------------------|
| 1 | Untreated | έΑΦ | έΑΦ | Natural disease course (HLA-B51+ severe BD) |
| 2 | Colchicine monotherapy | 0.5 mg BID oral | Tubulin / NLRP3 | Yurdakul et al. Arthritis Rheum 2001 (PMID 11710724): mucocutaneous flare reduction |
| 3 | Prednisolone monotherapy | 40 mg/day oral | NF-╬║B (broad cytokines) | Standard of care for acute flares; NF-╬║B/AP-1 co-repression |
| 4 | Adalimumab (anti-TNF) | SC 40 mg Q2W | TNF-╬▒ (mTNF + sTNF) | Saadoun et al. ADABT trial (PMID 21821622): uveitis remission; Hatemi 2018 EULAR update |
| 5 | Apremilast (PDE4i) | 30 mg BID oral | PDE4 έΗΤ cAMP έΗΤ TNF-╬▒/IL-17AέΗΥ | Hatemi et al. NEJM 2015 (PMID 25853758) + NEJM 2019 (PMID 31722153): oral ulcer NNT=2.4 |
| 6 | Canakinumab (anti-IL-1╬▓) | SC 150 mg Q8W | IL-1╬▓ (NLRP3 product) | Vitale et al. Dermatology 2014 (PMID 24577264): refractory oral/genital ulcers |
| 7 | Colchicine + Prednisolone | Combination | NLRP3 + NF-╬║B | Standard combination for moderate BD with mucocutaneous + systemic features |
| 8 | Adalimumab + Apremilast | Combination (refractory) | TNF-╬▒ + PDE4 | Combination for refractory multi-organ BD; EULAR 2018 refractory pathway |

### Shiny Dashboard (7 Interactive Tabs)

1. **Patient Profile** έΑΦ Disease demographics (Silk Road geography, HLA-B51 status); ISG diagnostic criteria checklist; organ involvement selector; BDCAF scale reference table with scoring rubric; pathomechanism HTML summary (innate/adaptive/vascular cascade)
2. **Drug PK** έΑΦ 5-drug selector (colchicine/prednisolone/adalimumab/apremilast/canakinumab); dose/frequency/duration inputs; concentration-time profile (plotly); PK reference table (F%/t┬╜/Vd/CL/Cmax); summary statistics (Cmax/Cmin/Cavg/AUC)
3. **Cytokine & Immune Dynamics** έΑΦ Single-treatment simulation; cytokine panel (TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓/IL-6/IL-17A time-course); immune cell dynamics (NEU/Th1/Th17/Treg); Th17/Treg balance ribbon plot (key pathological feature of BD)
4. **Clinical Endpoints** έΑΦ BDCAF composite score; oral ulcer activity; ocular inflammation; endothelial activation (vascular risk proxy); Day-90 endpoint summary datatable; remission threshold line (BDCAF < 3)
5. **Scenario Comparison** έΑΦ 8-arm simultaneous comparison; BDCAF/oral/ocular plots; color-coded by treatment type; Day-90 summary datatable with conditional formatting (green = remission)
6. **Biomarker & HLA-B51 Stratification** έΑΦ HLA-B51+ vs HLA-B51έΙΤ response comparison under selected therapy; serum cytokine biomarker dynamics; time-to-remission bar chart by genotype; clinical reference ranges table (TNF-╬▒/IL-1╬▓/IL-6/IL-17A pg/mL normal vs mild/active/severe BD)
7. **Dose Optimization** έΑΦ Drug-specific dose-response analysis (4 drugs); dose-range slider; BDCAF/OUL/OCI at Day-90 curves; optimal dose summary table with remission flag
